(jitadharmakāyavargāḥ parivarto hyanityatā । apramādaḥ kāmatṛṣṇe strī ca madyena te daśa ।। ।। om namo buddhāya ।। prahīṇasarvāsrava nirmalaśrīryaḥ kleśajambālanimagnalokam ।
kṛpāguṇenodaharatsamena praṇamyate asmai tribhavottamāya ।। saddharma smṛtyupasthānasūtravaipulyasāgarāt । gāthāḥ samuddhariṣyāmi lokalocanatatparāḥ ।। apramādastathā śraddhā vīryārambhastathā dhṛtiḥ ।
jñānābhyāsaḥ saṃtāśleṣo mokṣasyāyatanāni ṣaṭ ।। dānaṃ śīlaṃ damaḥ kṣāntirmaitrībhūteṣvahiṃsatā । karuṇāmuditopekṣā śāntisamprāptihetavaḥ ।। cāpalyaṃ pāpasaṃśleṣaḥ krūratā vitathaṃ vacaḥ ।
mithyādṛṣṭiḥ pramādaśca narakasyāgrahetavaḥ ।। mātsaryamīrṣyā kaṭuvākyatā hi pramādasevā viratiḥ śubhācca । tattveṣvabhidroharataṃ manaśca preteṣu panthāna ihodbhavanti ।। ajñānasevā jaḍa ca buddheḥ saddharmanāśaḥ priyamaithunatvam ।
āhāraśaktiḥ prabalā ca nidrā tiryaggatau ca pravadanti hetum ।। aśubhaṃ trividhaṃ kṛtvā kāyavāṅmanasāṃ mahat । uttarottarasambaddhaṃ karmaṇā sampradṛśyate ।। bālānāmapi sambaddhamuttarottarameva tat ।
śubhañca trividhaṃ kṛtvā sādhavo yānti nirvṛtim ।। tasmāt karmaphalaṃ matvā pramādasya ca varjanam । śreyase kriyate buddheretat sukhamanuttamam ।। dānaśīlavato nityaṃ sarvasattvānukampinaḥ ।
siddhayanti sarvaśastulyāstasmācchīlaparo bhavet ।। maitrīkaruṇāyuktasya gatākāṃkṣasya dehinaḥ । parānugrahayuktasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।। santuṣṭasyāpramattasya sarvasattvahitaiṣiṇaḥ ।
rāgadveṣavimuktasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।। mitrāmitraprahīṇasya samacittasya dehinaḥ । apāyagatibhinnasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।। evaṃ ca tasya dhīrasya dharmadānaratasya ca ।
mātsaryerṣyāpramuktasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।। saṃvarasthasya śāntasya gurupūjāratasya ca । kāryākāryavidhijñasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।। aśaṭhasyātidakṣasya priyavākyasya nityaśaḥ ।
dhyānādhyayanaśaktasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।। deśakālavidhijñasya sādhyāsādhyaṃ vijānataḥ । śakyopāyavidhijñasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।। akrodhena hataḥ krodhaḥ kṣamayā krūratā jitā ।
dharmeṇa nirjito adharmaḥ prabhayā vijitaṃ tamaḥ ।। mṛṣāvākyaṃ satyahataṃ paiśunyaṃ ca samādhinā । pārūṣyaṃ mārdava jitaṃ abaddhaṃ bandhanā jitam ।। prāṇātipāto maitryā ca steyaṃ dānaiḥ sadā jitam ।
ayoniśomanaskāro yonijena sadā jitaḥ ।। avidyā vidyayā jitā divasena tathā kṣapā । śuklapakṣeṇa ca kṛṣṇapakṣo sarvaśo jitaḥ ।। mithyākāmeṣvavijito buddhayā tattvavicārayā ।
āryāṣṭāṅgena mārgeṇa yonijena sadā jitaḥ ।। vaiśāradyaiścaturbhiśca kadarya jitameva tat । vismṛtiśca hatā smṛtyā kṣaṇenātmānameva ca ।। araṇyavāsaniyatairjitā rāgavaśā narāḥ ।
meruṇā parvatā jitā vanamālikā ।। samudreṇa jitā sarve tīrthā jalasambhavāḥ । ādityatejovijitā sarve ca grahatārakāḥ ।। nityā jitā anityena dāridrayaṃ dānasampadā ।
śāṭhyaṃ na mārdava jitaṃ satyenānṛtiko hataḥ ।। bhūtena nirjito abhūto vahninā tarusampadaḥ । pipāsā vijitā toyairjighitsā bhojanaistathā ।। siṃhena vijitāḥ sarve mṛgāḥ sattvādhikāśca ye ।
santāpena mahecchā ca jitā nityaṃ prakīrtyate ।। dayā praśasyate nityamadayā naiva śasyate । vīryeṇa nirjitaṃ sarva kausīdyaṃ mohavardhanam ।। tattvadarśipuruṣapraśaṃsā jñānādhikaiḥ sadā dāntaiḥ puruṣaistattvada bhiḥ ।
vijitāḥ krūrakarmāṇo mithyāvādādhikā narāḥ ।। buddhena nirjitāḥ sarve tīrthyāḥ kuṭilavādinaḥ । asurā vijitā devairdharmateyaṃ vyavasthitā ।। ।। iti jitavargaḥ prathamaḥ ।।
yo hi deśayate dharma kṣemaṃ nirvāṇagāminam । sa sarvabandhanacchettā gururbhavati dehinām ।। chittvā mohamayaṃ pāśaṃ yo hi deśayate śivam । sanmārgadeśakaḥ prokto durmārgavinivārakaḥ ।।
dharmasya pravaratvam yena dharmeṇa manujāstaranti bhavasāgaram । saddharmaprabaraḥ prokto na dharmo laukiko hi saḥ ।। kṣetrāṇīmāni catvāri vidyante yasya dehinaḥ । tasyedaṃ saphalaṃ janma kathitaṃ mārgadeśakaiḥ ।।
sakalendriyatāṃ prāpya labdhvā buddhasya śāsanam । yo na dharmarato martyaḥ sa paścādanutapyate ।। yamasāyujyam vyāsaktamanasāṃ nityaṃ nityaṃ kāmagaveṣiṇām । putradāraprasaktānāmantako abhyeti dehinām ।।
cittasya vaśīkaraṇam saṅkalpadoṣamanasaṃ taistairdoṣaiḥ samākulam । cittaṃ nayatyupāyena cittabaddhā hi dehinaḥ ।। durdamasyāticaṇḍasya siddhiprepsorviśeṣataḥ । na cittasya vaśaṃ gacchet śatrubhūtaṃ hi tannṛṇām ।।
saśrutena sudiṣṭena bhāvitenāpyanekaśaḥ । dharmeṇa śāmyate cittaṃ jālineva yathā hayaḥ ।। saddharmaśravaṇaphalam saddharmaśravaṇaṃ kṛtvā pāpād viramate pumān । śreyase pratipattiṃ ca nityamevopapadyate ।।
saddharmaśravaṇaṃ kṛtvā manaḥ prahalādamṛcchati । kuśalaṃ cāsya sumahat sandhāne sampratīkṣate ।। śrutvā bhavati dharmātmā śrutvā pāpaṃ na kurvate । śrutvā karmaphalaṃ jñātvā nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।
śrutvā vedayate dharma śrutvā buddhaḥ prasīdati । śrutvā dharmaṃ vimokṣāya yatate paṇḍito naraḥ ।। dharmalakṣaṇatattvajñaḥ śrutvā bhavati mānavaḥ । tasmācchrutvā prayatnena buddhiḥ kāryā prayatnataḥ ।।
śrutvā saṃsāravimukhāṃ kathāṃ sugatadeśitām । prahāya tṛṣṇāṃ vividhāṃ prayāti padamavyayam ।। caturvidhāṃ pratyayitāṃ dharmāṇāṃ codamavyayau । śrutvā tāṃ jñāyate sarvā pumān śraddhāvibhāvitaḥ ।।
skandhāyatanadhātūnāṃ yadetallakṣaṇadvayam । śrutvā tajjñāyate sarva tasmāt dharmaparo bhavet ।। prabalā ye trayo doṣāḥ sarvasaṃsārabandhanāḥ । te praṇaśyantyaśeṣeṇa saddharmaśravaṇena vai ।।
pravṛtterlakṣaṇaṃ kṛtsnaṃ nivṛtteścāpyaśeṣataḥ । śrutimāṃstat prajānāti tasmācchrutamanuttamam ।। mṛtyukālopapannasya vedanārtasya dehinaḥ । na vyathā śrutamālambya svalpāpi hṛdi jāyate ।।
samyagjñānena ye dagdhāḥ kleśavṛkṣāḥ samantataḥ । na teṣāmudbhavo bhūyaḥ kadācidupalabhyate ।। apramādavidagdhaṃ hi śrutaṃ sarva sukhodayam । śreyasaśva śrutaṃ mūlaṃ tasmācchrutaparo bhavet ।।
saddharmaśravaṇaṃ śrutvā vṛddhāṃścopāsya paṇḍitaḥ । prayātyanuttamaṃ sthānaṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitam ।। dharmeṇa vartate śrutvā duḥkhānmucyeta vai yathā । śrutvā bhavati maitryātmā tasmācchreyaḥ paraṃ śrutam ।।
kāyavāṅmanasāṃ buddhiḥ śrutvā bhavati dehinām । tasmāt sadbuddhikāmo yastena śrotavyamādarāt ।। śrutvā bhāvaṃ samāśritya dṛḍhavīryaparākramam । taranti puruṣāstūrṇa tribhava vipulaṃ mahat ।।
śrutvā yaḥ puruṣaḥ sarvairdhanavānabhijāyate । aśrutārthadhanairyuktaṃ daridraṃ prāhustaṃ budhāḥ ।। saddharmadhananaṣṭasya guruṇā varjitasya ca । viphalaṃ jīvitaṃ ceṣṭaṃ pāpairupahatasya ca ।।
pramādinaḥ kusīdastha pāpamitrasya dehinaḥ । jīvitaṃ niṣphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ bījamuptaṃ yathosare ।। śrutadṛṣṭivinirmuktamarthamāhurvicakṣaṇāḥ । na cakṣurbhyāṃ vinirmuktamarthamityabhidhīyate ।।
dharmasevanāgrahaḥ yo hi dharma parityajya adharmamanutiṣṭhati । sa bhaiṣajyaṃ parityajya vyādhimevopasevate ।। sevatāṃ sevatāṃ puṃsāṃ dharmo bhavatyanekaśaḥ । varṣāṇāṃ samavāyena yathodyānaṃ pravardhate ।।
iha vajrāsane bhūmirna saṃsāre anyathā bhavet । bodhicittasamutthānaṃ bodhiprāptistathottamā ।। dharmacārī praśāntātmā kāyotthāyī samāhitaḥ । avaśyaṃ śubhabhāgīsyāt sa pramādena vañcitaḥ ।।
jñānasevanāgrahaḥ tasmājjñānaguṇānmatvā jñānaṃ seveta paṇḍitaḥ । nahyajñānena saṃyuktaṃ pumān kaścit pratibhavet ।। dharmānusāriṇī śraddhā dharmānusāriṇī śraddhā yathā yāti sukhāvahā । sātidurgatisanyaktā vyasaneṣu mahad balam ।।
pradīpakalpā tamasi vyādhitānāmivauṣadham । arthānāṃ netra bhūtā sā daridrāṇāṃ mahadbalam ।। bhavādyairhriyamāṇānāṃ pūrvabhūtā sukhāvahā । pramādamadamattānāṃ sā pramādavighātikā ।।
śāntapadaprāpteḥ phalam sa hi yattatpadaṃ śāntaṃ nirvāṇamunibhirvṛtam । tat prāpayatyakhedena samyagjñānapuraḥsaram ।। ।। iti dharmopadeśavargaḥ dvitīyaḥ ।। satkārairvṛhaṇairmāsairapi śayyāsanādibhiḥ ।
na svīkartumayaṃ kāyaḥ kadācit kenacit kṛtaḥ ।। kṛtaghnasyāvidakṣasya nityaṃ randhraprahāriṇaḥ । kaḥ kāyasya riporartha pāpaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। rogānī tamanarthānāṃ bahūnā bhājanaṃ tathā ।
aśucyaṅgasya nikaraṃ kāyamityabhidhīyate ।। upasthitamavijñeyaṃ maraṇaṃ tattvacintakaiḥ । jīvitaṃ ca kṣaṇādūrdhvaṃ na gacchati nirūpyate ।। āyuṣkarmārthanirmāṇametaṃ kāyaṃ tyajyayam ।
api viddhastathā śete kāṣṭhaloṣṭhasamo bhuvi ।। kṣaṇe kṣaṇe api kāyo ayaṃ jīryate na nivartate । tathā yauvanamadairbālā muhayante ।। dhanadhānyamadairmattāḥ kurvantyahitamātmanaḥ ।
tannāśamupayātyevaṃ sa ca pāpena dahayate ।। na manuṣyā manuṣyāste yebhyo dharmo na rocate । na mārge ca sthitāstattve nirvāṇapuragāmike ।। kathaṃ prāpya hi mānuṣyaṃ śreyasāmālayaṃ mahat ।
na jñānaplavamārūhaya taranti bhavasāgarāt ।। vidyudālātasadṛśaṃ gandharvanagaropamam । sadā tad yāti rabhasaṃ jīvitaṃ sarvadehinām ।। śarīre na madaṃ kuryāt kṣaṇike bhaṅgure sadā ।
itvare capale asāre jarāmaraṇabhīruke ।। dhyāyinānnagataṃ hyetat śokānāmālayo mahān । śubhāśubhānāṃ kṣetraṃ ca śarīramavadhīyate ।। jñānaśīladayādānairyasya gātraṃ vibhūṣitam ।
tasya sattvaikasārasya śarīraṃ saphalaṃ matam ।। dhātūnāṃ mārakāt sarvamidaṃ muktaṃ kalevaram । śarīradhātu vicayāt sākṣād bhavati netarāt ।। śarīradhātuṃ yo muktvā dhātuṣvanyeṣu rajyate ।
sa dhātukatvaśikṣāto duḥkhenaiva pramucyate ।। hiraṇyadhāturna tathā duḥkhaśāntyai hi vartate । śarīradhātutattvajño yathā duḥkhāt pramucyate ।। duḥkhād duḥkhodayastena duḥkhī na parirakṣyate ।
pravīṇo rājacaurādibhayaiḥ sarvairūpadrutam ।। tasmādanarthakaṃ nityaṃ dūratastaṃ vivarjayet । varjanāt sukhito duṣṭasaṅgrahād duḥkhitaḥ pumān ।। śarīradhātutattvajño dhātulakṣaṇatattvavit ।
dhyānādhyayanasaṃsakto dahati kleśaparvatān ।। tasmāccharīrajān dhātūn paṇḍitaḥ pratyavekṣate । teṣāṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ jñātvā mokṣo bhavati dehinām ।। ।। iti kāyajugupsāvargastṛtīyaḥ ।।
kāmairevāvitṛṣṇasya tṛṣṇayā tṛṣitasya ca । cañcalendriyacittasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। anityadhyeyatā yasya sukhasaktasya dehinaḥ । strīdarśanena mattasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
jātimaraṇavaśyasya mohitasya ca tṛṣṇayā । bālasya tu janasyāsya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। gaticārakabaddhasya udvegavaśagasya ca । pramādaviṣamūḍhasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
auddhatyādiprasaktasya gātraśobhāratasya ca । lābhairatṛptamanasaḥ kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। pañcabandhanabaddhasya ṣaḍbhirvyāmohitasya ca । trailokyavidhimūḍhasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
vinipātānabhijñasya vitarkopahatasya ca । janasya saktamanasaḥ kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। tatkālaramaṇīyeṣu pariṇāmahiteṣu ca । kāmeṣu saktamanasaḥ kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
pūrvaduḥkhānabhijñasya divyasaukhyaratasya ca । viprayogānabhijñasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। karmajālena baddhasya manasyeva viceṣṭinaḥ । satpathāt paribhraṣṭasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
bhavadoṣānabhijñasya tṛṣṇayā mūḍhacetasaḥ । mohāndhakāramagnasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। kāmaikapāśabaddhasya niḥsahāyasya dehinaḥ । devīgaṇavimūḍhasyaṃ kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
indriyād vyapakṛṣṭasya satpathabhrāmitasya ca । traidhātukarasajñasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। saṃvarāsaṃvarajñasya vyāpādabahulasya ca । naṣṭasambuddhamārgasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
hitāhitavahirgasya kāryākāryajaḍasya ca । krīḍābāla sadṛśasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। nadīprastravaṇocceṣu vanopavanabhūmiṣu । krīḍātatparasyāsya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
vimānagiripṛṣṭheṣu dharmākaravaneṣu ca । ramataḥ kāmabhogeṣu kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।। karmadharma vipākeṣu nirāsaktasya dehinaḥ । kevalāhārasaktasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।
karmaṇāyuḥ pariśrāntaṃ traidhātukamidaṃ sadā । bhramanti cakravannityaṃ na ca vindanti bāliśāḥ ।। vinipātocchru yamayaṃ yo nāmārohate jagat । na ca doṣāvadheyatvaṃ prakurvanti vimohitāḥ ।।
etat paramaṃ saukhyaṃ yat kāmaparivarjanam । vītakāṃkṣasya dhīrasya gataśokasya tāpinaḥ ।। tadādimadhyanidhane kalyāṇaṃ kṣemamuttamam । yad prāpyamunayaḥ śrāntāścaranti vigatajvarāḥ ।।
satkāmajaṃ bhavet saukhyaṃ vinipātagataṃ tu tat । na hi kāmaviśeṣaṃ ca kiñcid duḥkhavipākajam ।। tasmāt kāmeṣu matimān na lubhyet kathañcana । te hi saṃsāraduḥkhānāṃ hetubhūtāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।।
vanopavanaśaileṣu padmākaravaneṣu ca । vibhrāntāstṛṣṇayā bālāḥ patanti saha daivataiḥ ।। kāñcaneṣu śaileṣu vaidūryaśikhareṣu ca । kṣīyate hi śubhaṃ karma yatasva saha daivataiḥ ।।
kalpavṛkṣeṣu ramyeṣu nadīprastravaṇeṣu ca । caratastaiḥ śubhaṃ kṣīṇaṃ yatasva saha daivataiḥ ।। bhūmibhāgeṣu ramyeṣu ratnākaravaneṣu ca । na śubhaṃ te sadā cīrṇa yatasva saha daivataiḥ ।।
pañcātmakena vīryeṇa manaḥprahalādakāriṇā । hatasya gatakālasya yatasva saha daivataiḥ ।। kāmaṃ saṃsakta manasairnityaṃ viṣayatatparaiḥ । na jñāyate hitaṃ devairyadamantrāhitaṃ bhavet ।।
alpaśiṣṭamidaṃ puṇyaṃ cyavanaṃ samupasthitam । gantavyamanyatra suraiḥ sukarmaphalabhojibhiḥ ।। ye nityaṃ śubhasaṃsaktāḥ kurvanti vā śubhaṃ sadā । teṣāṃ visadṛśo heturmūrkhāṇāṃ hi vivartate ।।
bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । śubhaśīlatamo ajñānāḥ sarvadā na parāyaṇāḥ ।। bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । ye na karmavipākasya jñānaṃ roṣavadhe ratāḥ ।।
bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । prajñāpayanti na samā stṛṣṇāgniparivāritāḥ ।। bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । viprayogakṛtaṃ duḥkhaṃ ye na paśyanti dāruṇam ।।
bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । strījanāsaktahṛdayā na vindanti punarbhavam ।। bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । vipattivyādhiśokebhyo nodvijanti kathañcana ।।
bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । ye pāpamitrasaṃsarga prakurvanti mahārūṣam ।। bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । bhāvitaṃ cetasā yairna na ca tattvapraveśitā ।।
bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । yena sarvāsvavasthāsu saṃsārabhayabhīravaḥ ।। bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । kāryākāryeṣu ye nityaṃ na subhāṣitacetasaḥ ।।
bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । ye na tattvadhiyo nityaṃ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।। bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । ye śarīra sukhārthena dharma hiṃsanti mohitāḥ ।।
ekāntamanasā nityaṃ śubhaṃ kāryaṃ prayatnataḥ । aśubhaṃ ca sadā varjyametat paṇḍitalakṣaṇam ।। kṣayaṃ yātaṃ ca yat śīlaṃ spṛṣṭvā yaḥ samupāgataḥ । pramādāvañcito avaśyaṃ vinipāto bhaviṣyati ।।
gatā gacchanti yāsyanti deveśāścaiva sarvataḥ । tiṣṭhanti śikhare ramye nānāratnavibhūṣite ।। vaidūryaśikharā ramyāstathānye vanamālinaḥ । viṣayāstādṛśā eva janastu parivartate ।।
vanopavanaramyāṇi bhūmibhāgāni sarvaśaḥ । tiṣṭhantyavikalānyeva janastu parivartate ।। vaidūryamayanālāni kāñcanāni viśeṣataḥ । padmākarāṇi tānyeva janastu parivartate ।।
sarāṃsi sarito ramyāḥ pakṣisaṅghairnirantaram । tathaivāvikalā hyete janastu parivartate ।। vimānāni rathāścaiva harmyāṇi ca tathaiva ca । tiṣṭhantyavikalā hyete janastu parivartate ।।
parivartanaṃ lokasya viṣayairvañcitasya ca । tathāpi nāmalokasya nodvego hṛdi jāyate ।। abhyāsena kharī bhūtaṃ cittaṃ saṃsāracāriṇam । yena manye mahad duḥkhaṃ hṛdaye naiva vartate ।।
śūlikena yathā baddhāḥ paśavo gṛhapañjare । ekaikaśo vinaśyanti śeṣāṇāṃ nāsti sambhramaḥ ।। sukhāya kāmināmeva iyaṃ bhūmiravasthitā । cyutāścaivopapannāśca tathāmī bāliśāḥ surāḥ ।।
pramādāya hatāḥ sattvā mṛtyuḥ kṣaṇikaduḥkhadaḥ । nāvabuddhayanti maraṇaṃ paśuvad vītasambhramāḥ ।। te paścād dīrghamanasaḥ kālasya vaśamāgatāḥ । paścāttāpamayo vahnirdhakṣyate niṣpratikṣayaḥ ।।
dāruṇaṃ niṣpratīkāramavaśyaṃ rūpadehinām । maraṇaṃ kālavaśagaṃ tad viditvāgamaṃ caret ।। samāgamāḥ priyāloke viyogāścāpriyāḥ sadā । saṃyogo viprayogānto dharmateyaṃ sanātanā ।।
kṣaṇe lave muhūrte ca divārātrau tathādhvani । maraṇaṃ cintayed dhīrastasya nāsti pratikriyā ।। smṛtimagnyāṃ praśaṃsanti yeṣāṃ maraṇasaṃbhavā । śreyasaikaparāṃ śānti prayāntiṃ gatakalmaṣāḥ ।।
mṛtyorarthamanusmṛtya doṣo ayaṃ kasya sammataḥ । nirdoṣaṃ hi manaḥ sarvaṃ śāntaṃ bhavati nityaśaḥ ।। apramādaparaṃ śreṣṭhamidamuktaṃ tathāgataiḥ । yanmṛtyoḥ smaraṇaṃ nityamaśubhānāṃ ca varjanam ।।
।। iti parivartavargaścaturthaḥ ।। kṣayāntaṃ hi sukhaṃ sarva na sukhaṃ vidyate dhruvam । saṃsṛjenna sukhaṃ tasmāt yadīcchet sukhamātmanaḥ ।। gacchatāṃ tiṣṭhatāṃ caiva hasatāṃ krīḍatāmapi ।
avisahyo mahāvego mṛtyurnaśyati dāruṇaḥ ।। na tatstha mihāmutra yatrāsau pratipadyate । tathāpi nāma saṃmūḍhā janayitvā vaśaṃgataḥ ।। na sthavirameva vā ।
gṛhasthamagṛhasthaṃ vā yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।। sukhitaṃ duḥkhitaṃ vāpi guṇavantaṃ tathaiva ca । vratasthamavratasthaṃ vā yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।। duḥśīlaṃ śīlavantaṃ ca ।
rājānaṃ cottamaṃ cāpi yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।। daivaṃ vā nārakaṃ vāpi tiryañca pratajaṃ tathā । pramattamapramattaṃ vā yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।। kāmadhātūpapannaṃ vā rūpadhātau sthitañca yaḥ ।
ārupyadhātūpapannaṃ vā yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।। karmapāśo jarādaṇḍo vyādhidaṇḍo mahāvanam । raktopamo mṛtyurayaṃ sattvānādāya gacchati ।। evaṃvidhe pratibhaye mṛtyau paramadāruṇe ।
surāḥ kāmavimohitāḥ ।। yad duḥkhaṃ cyavamānasya devalokāt surasya ca । narake yadbhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ viprayogapuraḥsaram ।। viṣamākṣikasaṃyuktaṃ yathānnaṃ cāpi ।
devagataṃ saukhyaṃ patanāntaṃ visarjayet ।। kṣīṇapuṇyasya dīnasya svadārairvarjitasya ca । yad duḥkhaṃ cyavamānasya tasyaupamyaṃ na vidyate ।। sukṛtakṣīṇamandasya dvipasyeva gatattviṣaḥ ।
śāmyati devasya yadduḥkhaṃ mahadduḥkhaṃ prajāyate ।। tṛṣṇāviṣayavṛddhasya śokopahatacetasaḥ । mandavāgdehaceṣṭasya devasya cyavanād bhayam ।। yathā yathā sukhāsvādāḥ kāmā paramavañcakāḥ ।
tathā bhavatyeva teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ mahattaram ।। yatamānasya yad duḥkhaṃ devalokān prajāyate । tasyāntareṇa narakaṃ kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm ।। cyavanāntaṃ devalokaṃ maraṇāntaṃ tadā bhuvi ।
dṛṣṭvā duḥkhaṃ ।। patanāntaṃ sadā saukhyaṃ nāsti lokasya nityajāḥ । tad buddhvā kāraṇaṃ sarva śreyase kriyatāṃ manaḥ ।। sarve kṣayāntā nicayā patanāntā samucchrayāḥ ।
saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ hi jīvitam ।। jātasya maraṇaṃ nityaṃ na tasyāstīti nityatā । na bhūtārāvitānena triṣu dhātuṣu dṛśyate ।। garbhameke vinaśyanti tathaike sūtikāgṛhe ।
parisarpaṇakāścaike tathaiva ।। udayāstaṃ ca gamanaṃ bhāskarasya pradṛśyate । tathā jātasya sarvasya sthitaṃ maraṇamagrataḥ ।। kṣayāntaṃ hi sukhaṃ sarva yo na vindati mohadhīḥ ।
sa paścānmaraṇe prāpte ।। kuśalaṃ kārya priyaḥ sadā । sukhaṃ hi dharmācaraṇaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। anityamadhruvaṃ sarva pariṇāme kaṭuḥ sadā ।
saṃsāraḥ kathito buddherhetustattvavicāraṇe ।। devāḥ sukhapramattā ye teṣāṃ sukhamaśāśvatam । cyavamānasya ca yadduḥkhaṃ devalokāt surasya hi ।। tasyopamānaṃ naivāsti narakānnarakaṃ hi tat ।
kimete nāvabudhyante patanāntaṃ sadā sukham ।। ajarāmaravallokaṃ paśyanti sukhamohitāḥ । cyutyupapattimallokaḥ saṃkhyā tasya na vidyate । na codvijanti puruṣāstṛṣṇayā parivañcitāḥ ।।
abhiyāti sadā janma tvaritaṃ yāti yauvanam । saṃyogo viprayogaśca sahajaḥ paridṛśyate । vimūḍhā nānupaśyanti viṣayaiḥ parivañcitāḥ ।। cyavanti devāḥ vivaśāstṛṣṇayā parimohitāḥ ।
sā bhūmistāni padmāni vanāni vividhāni ca ।। śikharāgrāṇi ramyāṇi ratnavanti mahānti ca । sarāṃsi nadyo vividhā ratnapāṣāṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। vṛkṣā vicitrakusumāḥ paṅktibhirvividhaiḥ sthitāḥ ।
harmyāgrāṇi ca ramyāṇi ratnavanti mahānti ca ।। kalpavṛkṣā hemamayā kecidvaidūrya nirmalāḥ । rājatāstapanīyāśca vimiśrā vararohiṇaḥ ।। bhramarairūpagītāśca vibhānti kamalākarāḥ ।
vibhūṣaṇāni ramyāṇi devārhāṇi ca sarvataḥ ।। sarvametat tathaivāsti janastu parivartate । māyābudbudaphenābhaṃ gandharvanagaropamam ।। sukhaṃ sarvasya devasya tṛṣṇayā vañcitasya hi ।
sa vināśya janaṃ sarva bhrāmayitvā bhavārṇave ।। tṛṣṇā viṣāgnisadṛśā lokānāmatra tiṣṭhati । avitṛptā kāmabhogairapi taptā sukhodbhavā ।। kālānalena nirdagdhā kva te devagaṇāḥ gatāḥ ।
sarvathādhigatā yeyaṃ tṛṣṇā lokavitanvinī ।। yayā vimohitā devāḥ kālasya vaśamāgatāḥ । devāsurā narā yakṣā narake yānti jaṅgamāḥ ।। gacchanti vivaśāḥ sarve kālapāśaṃ durāsadam ।
traidhātukamidaṃ sarva kālapāśena yojitam ।। na ca paśyanti vivaśāstṛṣṇāmohena mohitāḥ । anena hi yathā devāḥ śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ ।। gatāḥ kālāgninirdagdhā viṣayairdhanasaṃbhavaiḥ ।
parasya dṛśyate maraṇamātmano naiva dṛśyate ।। paścātte vyasane prāpte vindante duḥkhamātmanaḥ । pramādakaluṣaṃ ceto viṣayābhirataṃ sadā ।। na vindanti dhruvaṃ mṛtyuṃ dehināṃ sahajasthitam ।
sukhottaramanāśasya pramādābhiratasya ca ।। mṛtyusainyamupaitīdaṃ pramāthi viṣasannibham । na mantrauṣadhakarmāṇi na devā nāsurāstathā ।। kālapāśena baddhasya trātāro na bhavanti te ।
rajasā guṇṭhitaṃ vaktraṃ ātmano naiva vindati ।। prāpteścyavanabhūto ayaṃ mṛtyuḥ paścād bhaviṣyati । lolupasya sadā yatnairavitṛptasya tṛṣṇayā ।। sahasābhyeti maraṇaṃ yannadṛṣṭaṃ sukhārthinām ।
ayaṃ tavāgraho duḥkhaṃ mṛtyunā preṣito mahān ।। asmādanantaraṃ mṛtyurbhaviṣyati sudāruṇaḥ । mahāgirivarādasmāt vanopavanabhūṣitāt ।। baddhānarā viṣayagā svakarmaphalabhoginaḥ ।
krīḍāvihāriṇastāvat kvacit tṛṣṇāsukhaṃ na hi । tarṣyayā tṛṣṇayā mūḍhāḥ patanti vivaśā bhuvi ।। dhūmasyānantaraṃ vahniryathā bhavati nityaśaḥ । tathā cyavanaliṅgasya pṛṣṭhataścyavanaṃ sthitam ।।
jātyā jātyā dhruvaṃ mṛtyuścārogye sati ruk sthitā । sampattau vyasanaprāptiyauvane sahajā jarā । sarvaiḥ priyairviyogaśca na saṃyogo dhruvaṃ sthitaḥ ।। dharmateyaṃ sadāloke samyagbuddhena deśitā ।
ubhayasya kṣayo nāśo janasyo parivartate ।। jātau satyāṃ yathā mṛtyuravaśyaṃ sthita eva hi । kṣīyate sukṛtaṃ karma āyūṃṣi kṣaṇikāni hi ।। saṃvara dharmavinaye bhajadhvaṃ puruṣottamāḥ ।
abhyeti yauvanaṃ sarvaṃ jīvitaṃ cānugacchati ।। naśyanti sarvadā sarvā mā pramāde manaḥkṛthā । na nityaṃ labhyate svargo na nityaṃ kṣaṇasampadā ।। yasya yāvannābhipatanaṃ tāvat kṣipraṃ yujyatām ।
।। ayaṃ sa hi drumavano nānāratnavibhūṣitaḥ । latāgahvarasaṃcchannaḥ padmākaravibhūṣitaḥ ।। jāmbūnadamayaiśśuddhaiḥ prāsādaiḥ ratnacitritaiḥ ।
nānāvidhaiḥ prastravaṇairlatābhirupaśobhitaḥ ।। karmasākṣījanasyāsya bhitvā gaganamucchritaḥ । kalpāgnivirato meruḥ sarvathā na bhaviṣyati ।। kiṃ punarye surāstatra phenabudbudasannibhāḥ ।
utpadyante vinaśyanti pramādamadamohitāḥ ।। sukhaduḥkhamanantaṃ ca svecchākāmaphalodbhavam । devalokād yathā devāḥ patanti narake punaḥ ।। śarīramānasaiduḥkhairvidyamāneṣu sarvataḥ ।
na tacchakyaṃ pramatte syāt tadduḥkhaṃ paramaṃ kaṭu ।। viyogaduḥkhaṃ duḥkhanāmagrataḥ paripaṭhyate । taccadevagatau nityamagrataḥ sampravartate ।। sarvapriyairmanāpaiśca viprayogo bhaviṣyati ।
na ca devāḥ prapaśyadhvaṃ maraṇāntaṃ hi jīvitam ।। cyutikāle tu samprāpte vihvalendriyacetasā । jānīdhvaṃ tatparaṃ duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। akālacakrapratimaṃ gandharvanagaropamam ।
tribhave saṃbhavaṃ sarva phenabudbudasannibham ।। yaḥ phenarāśau saṃmūḍhaḥ kuryācchādanasaṃstaram । sa mūḍhaḥ saṃskṛte kuryādabhisvādaṃ bhramātmakam ।। na devā na narā yakṣā nāsurā garuḍāstathā ।
trāyante mṛtyusamaye karmaṇā paritapyatām ।। yāvannāyāti samaye mṛtyurājaḥ sudāruṇaḥ । tāvattu sukṛtaṃ kārya mā paścāt paritapyatha ।। yadbhūtakāmajaṃ saukhyaṃ prākṛtaṃ viṣayodbhavam ।
mṛtyukāle samutpanne tiṣṭhanti na budharṣamā ।। kiṃ kariṣyanti saukhyāni kiṃ striyaḥ kiñcabāndhavāḥ । mṛtyunā hriyamāṇasya devalokāt samantataḥ ।। sthirāstā bhūmayaḥ sarvā vanopavanabhūṣitāḥ ।
mṛtyurajjvā vibaddhaśca tvantu kālena nīyase ।। ākāśe jaladā yadvada vāyunā samudīritāḥ । saṃśliṣṭāśca viyujyante saṃsāre prāṇinastathā ।। ṛtau ṛtau yathā puṣpamāgatairdṛśyate naraiḥ ।
vyatīte tu ṛtau sarve pratiyānti yathāgatāḥ ।। yathā kāle samutpanne modante sukṛtaiḥ surāḥ । vyatīte tu śubhe kāle pratiyānti yathāgatāḥ ।। ṛtau ṛtau yathā vṛkṣe parṇajāyate anekaśaḥ ।
vyatīte tu śubhe kāle śīryate tat samantataḥ ।। yathā parṇopamādetanna saukhyamabhayaṃ bhave । śīryate satataṃ saukhyaṃ nāsaukhyaṃ vidyate dhruvam ।। prābṛṭkāle yathā varṣamākāśe na nivartate ।
tathā saukhyamidaṃ sarva gacchati na nivartate ।। barhiṇāṃ ca yathā nādo vāyunā samudīritaḥ । śrūyate tatpraṇāśāya tathā saukhyamidaṃ smṛtam ।। yathā hi jvalane kṣiptaṃ dhruvaṃ kālaṃ pradahayate ।
tathā vahanyupamaḥ kālaḥ kāṣṭhavaccaratāṃ smṛtaḥ ।। āgatāśca gatāścaike śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ । saṃvego na bhavatyeṣā tṛṣṇayā mohitāstathā ।। yathā yathā mahāsaukhyaṃ svayaṃ bhogo yathā yathā ।
tathā tathā mahad duḥkhaṃ patanāntodbhavaṃ dhruvam ।। jātirduḥkhā jarā duḥkhā maraṇaṃ duḥkhameva ca । priyaiśca saha viśleṣo duḥkhasyaiṣā paramparā ।। ekasya patanaṃ dṛṣṭvā kathaṃ nodvijate janaḥ ।
mamāpi patanaṃ hyetat sarvapāpairbhaviṣyati ।। yaḥ paśyati bhayaṃ dūrāt pratipattau ca vartate । mprāpte mṛtyusamaye na vibheti gatavyathaḥ ।। vibhujyamāno daunaiśca mṛtyuḥ svajanabāndhavaiḥ ।
yadduḥkhaṃ mṛtyusamaye tanna śakyaṃ prabhāṣitum ।। patanāntaṃ hi maraṇaṃ patamāno yathā giriḥ । niṣpratyanīkaṃ balavat puruṣānapakarṣati । saṃśliṣyate mahāvegaḥ samprahārī ca sarvadā ।।
taṃ jñātvā mā pramādeṣu stubadhvaṃ devasattamāḥ । saṃśleṣayati viśleṣaṃ yauvane ca sadā jarā ।। jīvite ca sadā mṛtyuḥ padametat sadā sthitam । anityenāgnināvaśyaṃ dagdhabyo yatra gocaraḥ ।।
kalpānte kiṃ punardevā ye phenakadalīsamāḥ । na tadasti bhavet kiñcid yad jñānaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ calam ।। yannityaṃ sukhaṃ vā syādetatsthānaṃ na vidyate । upasthitamiva jñeyaṃ maraṇaṃ sarvajantubhiḥ ।।
yasmāt tasya pratīkāraḥ sarvopāyairna śakyate । rūpaṃ kṣaṇikameteṣāṃ vayo api kṣaṇikaṃ tathā ।। kṣīyate ca tathā saukhyaṃ na ca buddhayantyamedhasaḥ । yadā tat sarvameteṣāmanekaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam ।।
janmataḥ kālacakreṇa paripāṭayā vināśitam । tathaivaitat purā naṣṭamanekaśatalakṣaṇam ।। tathaitadapi janmaiṣāṃ mṛtyurājo hariṣyati । pramādamanasāṃ hyeṣāṃ nityaṃ sukhavihāriṇām ।।
nidhanāya kālapāśo ayamabhyeti sukhanāśakaḥ । sukhārogyabalaprāṇapriyaviśleṣakārakaḥ ।। balavanmṛtyurājo asau samīpamupasarpati । yaḥ samīpagato hyeṣāṃ pramattānāmanekaśaḥ ।।
jīvitaṃ saha saukhyena tvaritaṃ nāśayiṣyati । dīrghakālamidaṃ dhvastaṃ pramādāpahatāḥ surāḥ ।। nāvabuddhayanti mohāndhāḥ saukhyena pratibodhitāḥ । yadā hīnaprabhāhyete vihvalendriyacetasaḥ ।।
yamalokaṃ patiṣyanti tadā jñānasya tatphalam । jīyate bata kālo ayaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ ca yathā sukham ।। tathāpi raktamanaso nāvabuddhayantyacakṣuṣaḥ । ramyād ramyataraṃ yānti nityaṃ sukhavihāriṇaḥ ।।
prayāsyanti yathā hayete mṛtyurājo hariṣyati । jarā jātivipattīnāṃ yo na mūḍho viṣīdati ।। sa paścāt mṛtyusamaye tapyate । sukhaṃ deveṣu samprāpya guṇasammatam ।।
kṛtahutaṃ vināśāntaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ jīvitaṃ calam । yathā hi yad vināśāntaṃ tathaiṣāmapi jīvitam ।। acireṇāpi kālena bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ । yāvannāyāti maraṇaṃ yāvad buddhiranāvilā ।।
tāvaddharmarataṃ dhārya manobalena dhīmatā । sarvajīvitanāśāya sarvasaukhyakṣayāya ca ।। sarvapriyaviyogāya mṛtyurāśrayameti ca । tasminnāpte mahādhyāne mṛtyuḥ paramadāruṇaḥ ।।
nānyat trāṇamṛte dharmāt tasmād dharmarato bhavet । upapannasya devasya yā prītirupapadyate ।। nāsau cyavanaduḥkhasya kalāmarhati ṣoḍaśīm । mṛtyukāle samutpanne na kaścit kasyacit tathā ।।
na ca gacchantimapyekaṃ padamekaṃ hi gacchati । yadā jātaṃ tadāramya naro mṛtyuparāyaṇaḥ ।। nānāmohaparītastu bhayametanna vidyate । yadā te cyavanaṃ prāpte bhavabhogakaraṃ param ।।
tadā vindati mūḍhātmā yad bhayaṃ mṛtyujaṃ mahat । viṣayoragasandaṣṭā tṛṣṇā viṣavimohitā ।। na vindanti sadā devāścyavanānte mahad bhayam । cyavanti ca tathā duḥkhamutpādayanti dehinām ।।
yathopapattiścyavanaṃ devānāṃ samprajāyate । karmavāyusamudbhrāntaṃ prayogeṇa ca duḥkhitam ।। puruṣaṃ nayate mṛtyuravaśaṃ । na mātaro na pitaro na mitrāṇi na bāndhavāḥ ।।
sahāyatāṃ vrajantīyaṃ puruṣaṃ kālacoditam । asahāyo janaścāyaṃ janaḥ prakṛtivañcitaḥ ।। kevalaṃ tu manaḥpāśairbandhanairbadhyate janaḥ । na janaḥ svajanaśceha trātā bhavati kasyacita ।।
mṛtyukāle samutpanne svajano api yathā janaḥ । yastvaṃ paśyasi devānāṃ sukhametanmahodayam ।। tat prasahyamahādevo mṛtyurājo hariṣyati । tvaritaṃ yāti janmedaṃ na ca vindati bāliśaḥ ।।
paścāttu vyasane prāpte prativindanti duḥkhinaḥ । yadi duḥkhādbhayaṃ tvaritaṃ yadi mṛtyubhayaśca yaḥ ।। dharme hi kriyatāṃ buddhirevaṃ sukhamavāpsyatha । vināśāntaṃ sadā saukhyamanityaṃ sarvataścalam ।।
sarvadevakṛtaṃ saukhyaṃ na ca vindanti mohitāḥ । abhūtvā ca cyavantyete bhūtvāvaśyaṃ hi cañcalāḥ ।। devāḥ patanabhāvāya dharmateyaṃ vyavasthitā । pramattāḥ kāmabhogeṣu ye devāścalamānasāḥ ।।
na paśyanti surāstīvraṃ vyasanāntaṃ hi jīvitam । yadaiva jāyate devastadaiva maraṇāya saḥ ।। divasānte yathā rātriravaśyaṃ pratipadyate । divasaṃ jīvitaṃ proktaṃ rātriḥ sthānmaraṇopamā ।।
tasmāt tadubhayaṃ jñātvā śreyase kriyatāṃ manaḥ । tadetadartha nṛṇāṃ hi strīrāgavaśavartinām ।। tadiṣṭaṃ mṛtyusainyena prasahayamavamarditam । bhāvābhāvādibhirmūḍhān vañcayitvā striyo narān ।।
prayānti mṛtyusamaye svakarmaphalabhoginaḥ । padmopavanaśaileṣu nadīnāṃ nirjhareṣu ca ।। bahuśaḥ krīḍanaṃ kṛtvā kūpāyābhigatāḥ priyāḥ । avaśyambhāvi maraṇamavaśyaṃ ca viyogitā ।।
tathāpi nāma puruṣā nityaṃ rāgavaśānugāḥ । sukhitaṃ duḥkhitaṃ vā jīrṇamanyatra yauvanam ।। duṣkulīnaṃ kulīnaṃ vā mṛtyurājo avamardati । surūpaṃ vā virūpaṃ vā balavantaṃ tathābalam ।।
sanāthaṃ naṣṭanāthaṃ vā mṛtyurājo avamardati । rājānaṃ vā tathā mṛtyuḥ gṛhiṇaṃ vā tathā yatim ।। krūraṃ vā mṛdukaṃ vāpi mṛtyurājo avamardati । nirdhanaṃ vā daridraṃ vā saguṇaṃ nirguṇaṃ tathā ।।
striyaṃ vā puruṣaṃ vāpi mṛtyurājo avamardati । pravāsinaṃ gṛhasthaṃ vā jale vāpi sthalesthitam ।। sthitaṃ vā giriśṛṅgeṣu mṛtyurājo avamardati । jāgarantaṃ tathā suptaṃ bhuñjānaṃ vā tathā sthitam ।।
pramāthī sarvalokasya mṛtyurājo avamardati । bhūmisthaṃ vimānasthaṃ videśasthaṃ tathā gṛhe ।। krakacaḥ kālacakro ayaṃ mṛtyurājo avamardati । bhāgyavantaṃ tathā dhanya nistriśaṃ dharmikam ।।
rogiṇaṃ svasthadehaṃ vā mṛtyurājo avamardati । caṇḍaṃ suśīlinaṃ cāpi kadarya dhaninaṃ tathā ।। pramattamapramattaṃ vā mṛtyurājo avamardati । nārakeyaṃ tathā pretaṃ tiryañco manujaṃ tathā ।।
anivṛttabalotsāho mṛtyurājo avamardati । kāmadhātau ca ye devā rūpadhātau ca ye sthitāḥ ।। tān sarvān hi pratibalān mṛtyurājo avamardati । ārūpyeṣu ca ye devāḥ samāpattiniveśakāḥ ।
tān sarvānapi vai devān mṛtyurājo avamardati ।। yad jātaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ kiñcid tad vināśāntameva hi । tannāsti saṃskṛtaṃ kiñcid yasya nāśo ca vidyate । mṛtyorbalamidaṃ jñātvā kāmadoṣaṃ ca sarvataḥ ।।
tṛṣṇayā vañcanaṃ cāpi viramadhvaṃ bhavārṇavāt । tadaitad vyasanaṃ matvā mṛtyorapi calācalam ।। sudāntaṃ kriyatāṃ cittaṃ yenedaṃ bhrāmyate jagat । vanopavanaśailebhyo vimānebhyaśca sarvataḥ ।।
sarvadevāḥ paciṣyanti kālāgnivinipātitāḥ । pramādamanaso mūḍhā bhūyo viṣayajihimatāḥ ।। tṛṣṇāpāśena sambaddhā devāḥ yāsyanti durgatim । rabhasaṃ jīvitaṃ saukhyaṃ prayāti khalu dehinām ।।
na ca vindanti vibudhā jātyandhā iva satpatham । jalabudbudasaṃkāśaṃ jīvitaṃ sarvadehinām ।। nadītaraṅgacapalaṃ yauvanaṃ vyativartate । anityā kaṭākṣekṣāpraduḥkhāstuṣitāḥ surāḥ ।।
nirvāyatyavaśo dīno dīpaḥ snehakṣayādiva । karmakṣayaparikṣipto dvādaśāro mahābalaḥ ।। dharmacakro bhavatyeṣa nipātī syānna cañcalaḥ । vicitraviṣayāramyā anekasukhamaṇḍitāḥ ।।
tuṣitāḥ patanti vivaśāḥ kālasya vaśamāgatāḥ । kālasya vaśamāpannā yathā rohanti pādapāḥ ।। te punaḥ kālamāsādya bhavanti vigatatviṣaḥ । yathā kālaṃ samāpadya bhavanti sukhitāḥ surāḥ ।।
punastamaiva saṃsṛtya patanti vivaśā hi te । karmakālaṃ samāsādya loko ayaṃ parivartate ।। sukhaṃ vrajati duḥkhaṃ hi kālasya vaśamāgataḥ । yadvṛttaṃ prākśubhaṃ karma tacca duṣṭamahodayam ।।
tadidaṃ bhuñjate svargaṃ kṣīyate ca tataḥ punaḥ । sahetukasya sarvasya kṣaṇikasya viśeṣataḥ ।। anityatāparāmarśo nāsau bhavati sarvataḥ । ye bhāvāḥ saṃskṛtā nityāḥ sarve te vipralobhinaḥ ।।
vipralobhya janaṃ yāti dharmateyaṃ vyavasthitā । śīghrasrotā yathā nadyastathā saukhyaṃ śarīriṇām ।। kṣaṇikaṃ jīvitaṃ sarva na ca vindanti bāliśāḥ । jarā vyādhiśca mṛtyuśca vipattiḥ karmasaṃkṣaye ।।
bhavantyetāni devānāṃ nityānāṃ kāmacāriṇām । nāyurdhruvaṃ bhavatyeva na saukhyaṃ triṣu dhātuṣu ।। na vindanti vivaśā devāḥ kāmena mohitāḥ । varṣadhārā yathākāśe duḥsthā bhavati sarvataḥ ।।
tathā saukhyamidaṃ sarva varṣadhāropamaṃ sadā । vāyunā pāṃsavo yānti anyonya parighaṭṭitāḥ ।। bhrāmyate gagane avaśyastathā śleṣaḥ śarīriṇām । suciramapi saṃramyaṃ nityatā nāsti dehinām ।।
acintyārthe saukhyamidaṃ na ca vindanti bāliśāḥ । vāteritaṃ tu yat saukhyaṃ vināśāntaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। vināśaṃ naiva budhyanti kāminaścittavañcitāḥ । duḥkhamiśraṃ sukhamidaṃ pracchannamiva vidyate ।।
padmamālāparicchinno viṣapūrṇo yathā ghaṭaḥ । odanaṃ viṣasammiśraṃ maraṇāntaṃ tat tathā ।। tathā saukhyamidaṃ sarva tasmāt tat parivarjayet । ādau madhye tathā cānte narakāya bhaviṣyati ।।
utpādasthitabhṅgāntaṃ sarva saṃskṛtamucyate । sarva ca saṃskṛtaṃ saukhyaṃ nanu bhaṭṭārameva tat ।। bhaṭṭārañca vilāsaśca vyayakṣaṇikaṃ tathā । sukhaṃ ca jīvitaṃ sarva tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।।
ādau madhye tathā cānte śreyasyeva manaḥ sadā । sudāntaḥ śuddhacitasya mṛtyukāle na sīdati ।। avaśyambhāvi maraṇaṃ priyasya ca viyogatā । na ca cintayataḥ kāle viṣaye vipralobhinaḥ ।।
jarāmaraṇacakraṃ tamaviṣahyaṃ sudāruṇam । pādapān devagān sattvān na ca buddhayantyacakṣuṣaḥ ।। cyavamānasya devasya vikalendriyacetasaḥ । yad duḥkhaṃ sukaraṃ tasya naupamyamiha vidyate ।।
yathā yathā mahat saukhyaṃ tṛṣṇopahatacetasaḥ । tathā tathā mahad duḥkhaṃ cyavamānasya duḥsaham ।। kṛtvā hi saṃskṛtaṃ karma na jñātvā karmaṇaḥ sthitiḥ । mṛtyukāle samutpanne paścāttāpena dahayate ।।
yāvannāpyeti maraṇaṃ yāvacca kṣaṇasampadaḥ । tāvat svahitamādheyameṣa mārgaḥ sukhāvahaḥ ।। cyavanaṃ devalokeṣu maraṇaṃ narabhūmiṣu । viditvā kaḥ pumān āsthāṃ kuryātsopadrave bhave ।।
tailavartipraṇāśena dīpanāśo yathā dhruvam । karmakriyā tathā kasya vinipātaḥ surālayāt । bhittināśo yathāvaśyaṃ cittanāśo dhruvaṃsthitaḥ ।। karmanāśāttathā saukhyamavaśyaṃ vinipadyate ।
kṣīṇapuṇyāḥ nipatyante devāḥ sarve surālayāt ।। anityataiṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ sattvānāṃ vinipātikā । mṛtyuḥ pivati bhūtāni jarā pivati yauvanam ।। vyādhiḥ pivati cārogyaṃ na ca loko avabudhyate ।
upapannāḥ subahuśaḥ pratītāścāpyanekaśaḥ ।। jāyate jīryate cāyaṃ cyavane copapadyate । na kṣaṇo asti muhūrto vā parivartastathāpi vā ।। yatra mṛtyurvilambena na ca loko avabudhyate ।
upapannāstu bahuśaḥ pratītāścāpyanekaśaḥ ।। yanna mṛtyuvilambaḥ syānna ca loko avabudhyate । anityaṃ jīvitaṃ sarva na vilambi ca yauvanam ।। sarvabhūtānyanityāni na ca loko avabudhyate ।
ante krameṇa naśyanti bhāvāḥ kṣaṇavilamvinaḥ ।। sambaddhāḥ karmasūtreṇa na ca loko avabudhyate । devakoṭisahastrāṇi vanopavanasevinām ।। nimīlitāni kālena na ca loko avabudhyate ।
paṅkābhāvacarā devāḥ pramattā bhogatṛṣṇayā ।। yāsyanti vilayaṃ sarve na ca loko avabudhyate । phenabudbudasaṅkāśaṃ svapnadravyopamaṃ sukham ।। kṣayaṃ prayāti śīghraṃ ca na ca loko avabudhyate ।
sarvasya sarvathā sarvo vināśo niyato bhave ।। na ca bālasya saṃsārānnirvedamupapadyate । na sarvaḥ sarvathā sarva sarvopāyaiḥ prayatnaśaḥ । saṃtrātā bhavane prāpte mṛtyukāle sudāruṇe ।।
vyucchettā sarvasaukhyānāṃ duḥkhanāmākaro mahān । viśleṣaḥ sarvabandhānāṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।। bhayopanetā bhūtānāṃ duḥkhānāmudadhiḥ samaḥ । vyāmohakarttā buddhīnāṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।
sañchettā jīvitānāmindriyāṇāṃ ca nāśakaḥ । amṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।। adhṛṣyaḥ sarvabhūtānāmajeyaḥ sarvakarmaṇām । vināśaḥ sarvasattvānāṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।
avaśyambhāvi tattvānāmantakaṃ sarvadehinām । nikāyabhāganāśo ayaṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।। sadeva yakṣagandharvapiśācoragarakṣasām । kālacakravināśī mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।
asaṃyamī pramāthī ca bahnivat sarvadehinām । krūraścāvinivarttyaśca mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।। skandhāyatananāśaśca ārupyasyātha cetasaḥ । kāladharmo mahāveśo mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।
sa eva dhā ve śīghraṃ vinipātāya dehinām । śreyase kriyatāṃ yatno mā pramādeḥ manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। yathā gamanaṃ pakṣiṇāṃ pavanasya vā । tathā śīghrataraṃ yāti jīvitaṃ sarvadehinām ।।
gato nivartate vāyurnivartante ca pakṣiṇaḥ । jīvitaṃ yanniruddhaṃ tu tasya nāgamanaṃ punaḥ ।। drutaṃ kṣīyanti karmāṇi drutamabhyeti cāntakaḥ । avaśyambhāvi viśleṣaṃ na ca vindanti devatāḥ ।।
anirvāyo mahāvegaścatuḥsatyanivarhaṇaḥ । avaśyambhāvi balavāneṣa mṛtyurupaiti ca ।। śruti pramādino devāḥ sukhena parivañcitāḥ । na vindanti mahad duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
saṃskṛtasya hi sarvasya samayasya viśeṣataḥ । vināśo bhavati sau dharmateyaṃ bhave bhave ।। jarāyauvananāśāya prāṇanāśāya cāntakaḥ । vipattibhūtanāśāya sthitā nāśahetavaḥ ।।
evaṃvidhe mahāghore vyasane mahad bhaye । pramādino hi yad devāḥ nūnamete ca cetanāḥ ।। anāgatabhayaṃ yo hi paśyati jñānacakṣuṣā । sa paṇḍita iti jñeyo viparītastu bāliśaḥ ।।
vimūḍhamanasaḥ sarve vañcitāḥ svena cetasā । karmakṣaye tu naśyanti dīpā snehavaśādiva ।। anekaviṣayāṇāṃ ca idaṃ saukhyamanuttamam । bhuktvā karmakṣayo bhūta vinipāto bhaviṣyati ।।
jalataraṅgacapalaṃ jīvitaṃ yāti dehinām । na ca budbudaniḥsāramavagacchanti bāliśāḥ ।। phenarāśiściraṃ tiṣṭhed upāyaiḥ katibhirnanu । na tu devāściraṃ tiṣṭhantyanityo bhāvanamiti ।।
kṛṣyate bhūriyaṃ sarvā manujaiḥ phalakāṃkṣibhiḥ । na ca saṃdṛśyate mṛtyurlābhasaktairapaṇḍitaiḥ ।। kṣaṇe kṣaṇe vivardhante lobhāśā mohite jane । na ca vindanti saṃsārāḥ kṣīyamāṇāḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe ।।
jarādaṇḍo ayamabhyeti yauvanāntakaro nṛṇām । ārogyaśaktināśāya vyādhidaṇḍo ayamāgataḥ । daṇḍatrayamidaṃ ghoraṃ sasurāsuranāśakam ।। abhyeti na ca mūḍho ayaṃ lokaṃ paśyati bāliśaḥ ।
parasparaṃ pralobhācca svajanaṃ snehacañcalam ।। gacchatyanyonyasaṃśliṣṭo mohabaddhe jane janaḥ । putrapautraprapautrāṇāṃ vaśagāścāpi ye narāḥ ।। sarve tena bhaviṣyanti tvaṃ tu saṅgena bādhyase ।
jīvitāntakaraḥ śatrurna viśaṅko mahābalaḥ ।। so avilambī mahāvego mṛtyureṣo abhyupaiti ca । calācalavidhirjñeyaḥ karmaskandhairnidarśitaḥ ।। devanāgāḥ gandharvā piśācoragarākṣasāḥ ।
na śaktāścyavane kṣāntaṃ balaṃ tasya tathāgatam ।। calācalavidhirjñeyaḥ karmaṇā tattvadarśakaḥ । aliptaḥ pāpakairdharmairna sa gacchati durgatim ।। yaḥ pramādarato janturnāsau mokṣāya kalpate ।
pramādaviṣamūḍhasya nirvāṇaṃ dūrameva tat ।। na pramādeṣu badhyet pramādaḥ śatruruttamaḥ । pramādaparamā devāḥ patanti narake punaḥ ।। svabhāvatāmimāṃ jñātvā dharmāṇāmudayavyayam ।
na pramāde manaḥ kārya pramādaviṣamuttamam ।। apramādo amṛtapadaṃ pramādo mṛtyunaḥ padam । apramattā na bhriyante pramattāstu sadātmṛtāḥ ।। yathā viṣaṃ tathā vahniḥ pramādaḥ prāṇināṃ tathā ।
pramādonmāditāḥ satvāḥ duḥkhād duḥkhaṃ prayānti te ।। apramattāḥ sadāmartyāḥ sarva prakramasaṃskṛtāḥ । prayānti paramāṃ śānti pramādo yatra nāsti hi ।। yaḥ pramāde rato janturna śubhānyanuceṣṭate ।
tasya dharmavimūḍhasya kutaḥ svargo bhaviṣyati? ।। pramādaṃ varjayed yasmāt pramādaṃ viṣamuttamam । apramattā na bhriyante pramattāstu sadātmṛtāḥ ।। saubhāgyaṃ prāpya yo martyaḥ pramādeṣu ca vartate ।
na paṇḍita itikhyāto viparītastu nānyathā ।। na pramādasya kālo hi harṣasya na kathañcana । vyāmohajananācceto mṛtyukāle mahābale ।। harṣo dhūmaḥ pramādo agnirdevān dahati naikaśaḥ ।
viṣayairmohitā mūḍhā na ca vindantyacakṣuṣaḥ ।। avyucchinnāni paśyanti saṃskārāṇi ca dehinām । yathā hi viṣayairmūḍhā nāvagacchanti yaddviṣaḥ ।। tasmāt pramādaṃ viṣavat kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
sukhaṃ na dṛśyate pūrva pramādomandabuddhibhiḥ ।। pramādopakṛtāḥ prayānti narakaṃ punaḥ । phale prāpte pramādo ayaṃ paścāt santapyate vyathā ।। sarvānarthakaro dṛṣṭaḥ pramādaḥ paṇḍitaiḥ naraiḥ ।
tathā ca kuśalaṃ prāyo yaḥ pramādaṃ na sevate ।। duḥkhaṃ yasya bhavediṣṭaṃ sa pramādaṃ niṣevatām । na pramādaparaḥ kaścit kadācit sukhamāpnuyāt ।। pramādaviratāḥ santo gacchanti padamacyutam ।
nā pramādaparaḥ kaścinnarake duḥkhitānnayet ।। yadi devāḥ sahantīmaṃ ramante mandamedhasaḥ । tiraścāṃ hi surāṇāṃ ca viśeṣo naiva vidyate ।। pratyekaṃ karmavaicitryaṃ pramādaparamāḥ surāḥ ।
nāvagacchanti patanaṃ devalokād bhaviṣyati ।। sannikṛṣṭaṃ sadā duḥkhaṃ patanaṃ vā bhaviṣyati । devalokottarā devā yathā syāt sukhamātmanaḥ ।। devalokaṃ samāsādya yaḥ pramādeṣu rakṣate ।
sa kṣīṇaśubhakarmāntaṃ cyavanānte vibudhyate ।। mā pramādaparobhūyāḥ pramādo nocitaḥ suraiḥ । pramādairdoṣavihatāścyavanti tridaśālayāt ।। dahyate puruṣaḥ sarvaḥ pramādena vimohitaḥ ।
sa paścād vigate tasmin pratyādeśena rakṣyate ।। doṣodbhavāmimāṃ bhūmiṃ pramādāvṛttaśādvalam । vicaranti sadā mūḍhāḥ surāḥ satkṛtamohitāḥ ।। cañcalā viṣamāstīvrā pramādāḥ kāmahetavaḥ ।
na teṣāṃ viśvased vīro yasmāt svapnopamā hi te ।। na svapno narake hetuḥ kāmāḥ svapnasya hetukāḥ । tasmāt kāmamimaṃ muktvā nityaṃ sucaritaṃ caret ।। yatrāvāptaṃ padaṃ kṛtsnaṃ suraiḥ kāmavimohitaiḥ ।
tat prāpyate padaṃ vīrairapramādaparairnaraiḥ ।। pramādamūlasaṃsāro devānāmālayastathā । ye pramādaviṣairmattāste magnā bhavasaṅkaṭe ।। tamaḥ pramādamūlañca avidyā hayapakārikā ।
andhakāreṇa ye mūḍhāsteṣāṃ cakṣurna vidyate ।। tejasā hi tathā mūlairagninā na ca kathyate । mohānāṃ pravarastadvat pramādaḥ parikīrtyate ।। pramādānalataptena manasā tad viceṣṭate ।
muhayante yena te bālāḥ prayānti narakaṃ punaḥ ।। pramādonmāditā devāstrividhā ye calātmakāḥ । viyogaduḥkhaṃ vismṛtya saṃyoge sukhakāṃkṣiṇaḥ ।। upasthite mahāduḥkhe patanānte hi jīvite ।
paścād vahanti virasaṃ patanāntaṃ sukhaṃ calam ।। saṃyogo viprayogāntaḥ patanāntaḥ sukhaṃ sadā । jarāntaṃ yauvanaṃ sarva karmāntaḥ sarvadehinām ।। śubhāśubhena baddhā hi karmaṇā sarvadehinaḥ ।
naṭavannaṭayantyete gatyāṃ gatyāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।। karmanāṭakasambaddhaḥ saṃsāro bhramate sadā । na tatra viśvaseddhīmānanityā karmaṇāṃ gatiḥ ।। sarvapāpāni viṣavat pramādaḥ paribarjyatām ।
pramādena tu ye muktā tīrṇāsti bhavārṇavāt ।। prapātapatito doṣī kadācidapi jīvati । na pramādaprapatitaḥ kadāpi sukhavān bhavet ।। pramādaḥ paramo doṣaḥ kadācit sarvakarmasu ।
na rātrau na divā tasya śubhaṃ bhavati karhicit ।। yat sukhaṃ laukikaṃ kiñcid yacca lokottaraṃ matam । naśyate tat pramādena tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।। apramādo amṛtapadaṃ pramādo mṛtyunaḥ padam ।
apramādena te devāḥ devānāṃ śreṣṭhatāṃ gatāḥ ।। pramādamūlaḥ saṃsāraḥ apramādaśca gatiḥ । tasmād pramādavirataḥ sukhī bhavati sarvadā ।। icchate yatsukhaṃ nityaṃ yaśca duḥkhād vibheti ।
sa pramādād viramet pramādo viṣavannṛṇām ।। pramādanidrāvihatā pramādaviṣamohitāḥ । prapātaṃ hi prapadyante janāḥ śukla kṛtātmakāḥ ।। apramādaḥ paraṃ śreyo na pramādaḥ kathañcanaḥ ।
apramādena sukhinaḥ pramādena duḥkhitāḥ ।। pramādamūḍhā hi narā bhūyo madyena mohitā । dhik pramādavimūḍhāste caranti narakaṃ punaḥ ।। pramādavāgurābaddhā viṣayārṇavasaṃsthitāḥ ।
tṛṣṇāviṣayasambaddho devaḥ krīḍatyanekaśaḥ ।। jātamātrasya devasya tat kṣaṇaṃ kṣīyate sukham । na vindanti vivaśāḥ pramādāvṛttacetasaḥ ।। pramādod bhrāntamanaso nityaṃ viṣayatatparāḥ ।
atṛptāḥ kāmabhogeṣu sukhena sukhitā hi ca ।। kāmānalena sandagdhāḥ vipramādena mohitāḥ । na vindanti balaṃ sarva vināśāntaṃ hi jīvitam ।। anekāni sahastrāṇi surāṇāṃ niyutāni ca ।
kāmānalena sandagdhāḥ pramādena vimohitāḥ ।। hriyate puruṣaḥ sarvaḥ pramādena vimohitaḥ । sa paścād vyasane prāpte budhyate tasya tatphalam ।। viṣavat prāṇahṛd dṛṣṭaḥ pramādastattvadarśibhiḥ ।
agnivad dahyate nityaṃ śastravacca nikṛntatiḥ ।। mitravad dṛśyate pūrva paścād bhavati śatruvat । vahiśaḥ sarvadevānāṃ pramādaḥ sampravartate ।। devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ nāgānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
pramādaḥ kāraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sarvānnarthān karoti saḥ ।। yaḥ pramādahato nityaṃ nāsau kalyāṇamarhati । kalyāṇavarjitaḥ puruṣo narakānupakarṣati ।। vividhā kṛtayastiryag pramādaparivañcitāḥ ।
maithune bhojane caiva yeṣāṃ buddhiḥ sadāratāḥ ।। yadā sucaritaṃ karma cāntībhūtaṃ divaukasām । bhaviṣyati tadābhūyaḥ kva yāsyanti pramādinaḥ ।। pramādavāriṇāṃ duḥṣṭāḥ karmavāyubhirāhatāḥ ।
patanti vṛkṣavad devā gatyāṃ gatyāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।। śataśo na hutaścaiva divi jātā divaukasaḥ । na ca saṃvegajanito hṛdi śokaḥ prajāyate ।। pramādakaluṣaṃ pītvā mohātpānaṃ divaukasaḥ ।
patanti narakaṃ tīvraṃ vahninā parivāritam ।। sulabdhaṃ mānuṣaṃ janma ye labdhvā apramādinaḥ । kurvanti sukṛtaṃ karma devalokopagāminaḥ ।। durlabhaṃ mānuṣaṃ karma labdhvāpi ye pramādinaḥ ।
te pramādāt paribhrāntāḥ patanti narake narāḥ ।। pramādaratasattvo yaḥ kṛpayā parivartate । sa paścānmṛtyusamaye tapyate svenacetasā ।। na tathā dahyate vahnirna ca śastraṃ vikṛntati ।
pañcendriyasamudbhūtaṃ pramādo dahyate tathā ।। sukharūpaṃ tathā duḥkhaṃ mitrarūpaṃ tathā ripuḥ । pramādināṃ hi tannityaṃ tasmāttaṃ parivarjayet ।। pramādatṛṣṇayā miśro rāgastadanuvardhakaḥ ।
trayaste ripavaḥ kruṣṭāḥ nāśayanti sukhaṃ nṛṇām ।। ye pramādaratā nityaṃ na ca dharmaratā budhāḥ । te mṛtyusamaye prāpte yamadūtaiḥ parākṛtāḥ ।। pramādaṃ viṣavad ye tu parirakṣanti paṇḍitāḥ ।
te mṛtyusamaye prāpte bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ ।। pramādaḥ paramo mṛtyurapramādaḥ paraṃ sukham । tasmāt sukhārthināḥ nityaṃ mā pramāde matiṃ kṛthāḥ ।। dhātvāyatanasammohaḥ śreyasāṃ vighnakārakaḥ ।
sanyāsaḥ sarvakarmāṇāṃ pramādaḥ sampravartate ।। doṣayantravilagnāya māyādvārasya dūtakaḥ । sammohasyāgraṇī pāpaḥ pramādaḥ sampravartate ।। ye pramādaratā bālāste mṛtyorhastamāsthitāḥ ।
pramādasevakā ye tu te sarve nidhanaṃgatā ।। puṇyakṣayāya devānāṃ pramādena vihiṃsitāḥ । patanti sukhasaṃmūḍhāstrāṇaṃ teṣāṃ tadā kutaḥ ।। eko dharmastathāśreyaḥ kṛpayā saṃyataḥ pṛthuḥ ।
kṣāntiścāpi sadā yuktā dayā bhūteṣu sarvadā ।। balabhūtā bhavantyete mṛtyukāle mahābhaye । tasmāt pramādarahitaiḥ sevanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।। avidyāvartanaṃ śreyo vidyāyā rakṣaṇaṃ sadā ।
vidyāvidhijño yaḥ pramādastasya śāmyati । puruṣārtho niyato yat pramādasya varjanam ।। apramādaratasyaiva puruṣārthaḥ satāṃ mataḥ । pramādo bandhanaṃ prāyo muktistasyāpramādataḥ ।।
evaṃ matvā sadā devo yaḥ pramādena rakṣati । sa paścānmṛtyusamaye jñāsyate tasya tatphalam ।। yathā yathā hi santoṣaḥ sevyate yatibhiḥ sadā । tathā tathā hi nirvāṇamanike tasya vartate ।।
virāgaḥ sarvakāmeṣu nirvāṇe ca pravartatām । nāsau mārasya viṣayaḥ kadācit sampravartate ।। narāṇāṃ paśya manaso nityaṃ vyāpārameva ca । udyogaśca sadājñānaṃ sa kathaṃ duḥkhameṣyati ।।
atītabhayasampannaḥ pratyutpanne ca buddhimān । anāgatavidhijño yaḥ sa muktaḥ kleśabandhanāt ।। apramādarato nityamaviśvāse ca kātaraḥ । saṃjñānasevī vimalo nirvāṇasyāntike sthitaḥ ।।
pramādenāpi naśyanti devāḥ prāpyamahatsukham । kiṃ punaryena vā mūḍhāḥ pramādavaśasevinaḥ ।। mṛtaḥ sa naro bhavati yaḥ pramādavihāravān । jīvite ca pramatto ayaṃ satataṃ jñānadhāraṇe ।।
apramādapramādābhyāmidamantaramiṣyate । mṛtyuṃ ca varjayed doṣaṃ pramādaṃ duḥkhamūlakam ।। nityaṃ pramuditā devāḥ nityaṃ pramuditā vayam । pakṣiṇāṃ ca surāṇāṃ ca viśeṣo nopalabhyate ।।
na dharmācaraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mokṣacaryā na yātyasau । tathaiva yadi devānāṃ te gatāḥ pakṣibhiḥ samā ।। ye pramādavinirmuktā ye ca dharmaratāḥ sadā । te devāḥ satpathā loke na pramādavihāriṇaḥ ।।
yadi krīḍāratā devāḥ pramādacaritāḥ sadā । devānāṃ ca khagānāṃ ca viśeṣo nopalabhyate ।। karmaṇāṃ tu viśeṣeṇa jātirdharmairviśiṣyate । na dharmapatitaḥ kaścid jātyā bhavati śobhanaḥ ।।
yena nindanti saṃsāramimaṃ sarvakṣayātmakam । te surāpisamā nityaṃ pakṣibhirmūḍhabuddhibhiḥ ।। yeṣāmevasthitā buddhiramatā dharmagocare । te devāḥ sammattā loke na pramādavicāriṇaḥ ।।
ye janmahetuprabhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ budhyanti śobhanam । te devā na tu ye saktāḥ kāmeṣu hitakāriṣu ।। viyujyamānā bahuśo bhṛtyasvajanabāndhavaiḥ । ye nodvijanti saṃsāre te devāḥ pakṣibhiḥ samāḥ ।।
madyapānādhiko dṛṣṭaḥ pramādastattvadarśibhiḥ । jīryate madyapānaṃ hi pramādo naiva jīryate ।। pramādopahatoloko bhramate gatipañcake । tasmāt pramādamatto hi sarvopāyairviśiṣyate ।।
ekāhaṃ paramaṃ madyaṃ pramādayati dehinaḥ । pramādaḥ kalpakoṭibhirbhramato api na jīryate ।। ye pramādairvirahitāste gatāḥ padamavyayam । ye tu pramādavaśagāste bhavanti khagā narāḥ ।।
hitārthinā manuṣyeṇa pramādovarjya eva hi । yasmāt pramādavaśagāḥ kleśā buddhena deśitāḥ ।। khagā yadi pramādena kurvanti laghucetasaḥ । kasmāddevāḥ pramādaṃ na jahaṃti viśeṣataḥ ।।
yastu dūrāt pramādena bhayaṃ nāvaiti durmatiḥ । so avaśyaṃ vyasane prāpte paścāttāpena dahyate ।। patanaṃ devalokāt te dānai rakṣanti dāruṇam । tad vicintya pramādaste na saṃsevyaḥ kathañcana ।।
ye pramādaratā nityaṃ na te saukhyasya bhāginaḥ । pramādo duḥkhamūlaśca mūlamekaṃ sudāruṇam ।। padmakoṭisahastrāṇi niyutānyarbudāni ca । asaṃkhyāni ca devānāṃ pramādena vitanvitāḥ ।।
apramādaḥ paraṃ nityaṃ hitakaraṃ nṛṇām । pramādastu paraṃ śatrustasyanmitraparo bhavet ।। śubhasyāntakaro hayeṣa viṣavad dāruṇaṃ param । durgatīnāṃ paraṃ mārgaḥ pramāda iti kathyate ।।
pramādena pramattā ye viṣayaiścāpi rañjitāḥ । narāste mūḍhamanaso nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhoginaḥ ।। yeṣāṃ bhayaṃ na duḥkhaṃ na ca jñānāvalokanam । paśubhiste samāviṣṭā na purā sukhakāṃkṣiṇaḥ ।।
āhāramaithunaratiḥ paśūnāṃ hṛdi vartate । sā ratiryadi devānāṃ te gatāḥ paśubhiḥ samāḥ ।। krīḍantyatiśayaṃ hyete mṛtyorgamye puraḥsthitā । samprāpte mṛtyusamaye phalaṃ dāsyanti ।।
viṣavat pariheyo sarvairapi । mṛtyoḥ paryāyanāmaiṣa pramādo hṛdi dehinām ।। pramādena hatān pūrvaṃ paścānmṛtyuḥ pramardati । dharmajīvitasaukhyānāṃ tamekāṃśaṃ prakathyate ।।
apramāda iti khyātaḥ svargamārga pradeśakaḥ । arthānathau samāvetau paścānmokṣastathaiva ।। apramādaḥ pramādaśca guṇadoṣasamāvibhau । tatraiva mūḍhamanaso vijānanti ca dehinaḥ ।।
śatruṇā saha rakṣanti jñāne pariharanti ca । pramādaviṣavṛkṣasya śākhāstistraḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। jarā vyādhiśca mṛtyuñca nityaṃ tasyoparisthitāḥ । jarādayo na bādhyante puruṣaṃ satkriyānvitam ।।
saṃsāre tiṣṭhate dhīmānapramādarataḥ sadā । nikṛntanti sadā doṣā na pramādaṃ pariṣvajet ।। sadā bhayavinirmuktaḥ sukhaṃ prāpnotyanuttamam । pramādācca yat saukhyaṃ śāśvataṃ sa bhayaṃ hi tat ।।
yattu tasmād vinirmuktaṃ tat saukhyaṃ dhruvamacyutam । śataśo manujā pramādena vimohitāḥ ।। tathāpi nāma vaśagāste pramāde pratiṣṭhitāḥ । catvāro hi viparyāsāḥ pramādasyoparisthitāḥ ।।
pramādavirahāttepi naśyanti lokaśatravaḥ । yadanekavikalpo ayamanekabhayasaṅkaṭaḥ ।। saṃsāro bhramate duḥkhe tat pramādasya ceṣṭitam । ekaḥ pramādavirahāt prāpyate sukhamacyutam ।।
pramādena vinaśyanti sarvadharmā hatāstravāḥ । devānāṃ ca pramādo ayamuparyupari vartate ।। kathaṃ pramādasammūḍhāḥ devā yāsyanti nirvṛtim । tade t saumyamanasā cintayitvā vikalpayet ।।
tathā me hita māstheyaṃ yathā yat syāt । ye devā yacca tatsaukhyaṃ paśyan yadapikiñcana ।। tat sarva dhruvaṃ gatvā saṃskṛtasyaiṣa sambhavaḥ । avaśyaṃ te vinaśyanti ye bhāvāḥ saṃskṛtāścalāḥ ।।
pramādaniratā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ । pramādāpahatajano yasteṣāṃ kurute matiḥ ।। saṃviyoge samutpanne duḥkhena paritapyate । viṣayeṣu sakāmeṣu tṛṣṇāvanagateṣu ca ।।
tena te vañcitā devāḥ pramādavaśavartinaḥ । mūlametadanarthānāṃ yatpramādānusevanam ।। tasyaitad varjanaṃ dhanyaṃ sarvakṣemakaraṃ mahat । satvā naivāpannasukhā duḥkhaiścāpi samanvitāḥ ।।
tathā buddhiranuṣṭheyā yathā matsyā jalānugāḥ । svarge pramādavaśagā strīvidheyāśca te surāḥ ।। te strīvahnivinirdagdhā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ । tasmāt prayatnaśo devairaṅganā parivarjanam ।।
karttavyaṃ kāmalolasya manasā dhṛtivardhanam । kāryākāryevimūḍhasya dharmādharme tathaiva ca ।। puruṣasyātmabhaṅgasya nirvāṇaṃ dūrameva tat । gurutābhāvatattvajño nipuṇo dharmagocaraḥ ।।
dharmākāṃkṣī phalākāṃkṣī tādṛśaṃ labhate sukham । nidhautamaghakalmāṣāḥ nityaṃ dharmānuvartinaḥ ।। sukhinaste sadā dṛṣṭā na pramādavihāriṇaḥ । pramādāpahataḥ pūrva pramādena vimohitaḥ ।।
devo vā puruṣaścāpi na sukhasyāntike hi saḥ । mṛtaḥ sa puruṣo nityaṃ yo madyena pramādyati ।। madyadoṣādhṛtāḥ sarve bhavanti narake narāḥ । asaṃsargacaro doṣo madyamityabhidhīyate ।।
madyena mohitā nityaṃ devāḥ narakagāminaḥ । asambhūteṣu rakṣante na sambhūte kathañcanaḥ ।। madātsvākāramalinā devāḥ kāmairvimohitāḥ । kāmena mohitā devā madyenāpi tathaiva ca ।।
na tattvamatra paśyanti jātyandhā iva satpatham । pramādākulitaṃ cittaṃ na tattvamanupaśyati ।। pramādaścāgnivattasmāt parivarjyaḥ samantataḥ । pramādena vinaśyanti kuśalā dharmayonayaḥ ।।
mārga ca viṣasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ sarvathā naiva paśyati । daśadharmā vinaśyanti pramādaviṣasevinām ।। dhyānāni caiva catvāri praṇaśyanti pramādinaḥ । apramādaṃ praśaṃsanti buddhāḥ kāmavivarjitāḥ ।।
pramādañca jugupsanti jarāmaraṇapañjaram । apramattā jarāmuktā pramattā duḥkhabhoginaḥ ।। pramāda eva bandhanam । pramādo bandhanaṃ hayetad duḥkhitaṃ mandabuddhinām ।
apramādena kuśalā devānāṃ samitiṅgatāḥ ।। tasmāt te patitā bhūyo ye pramādānusevinaḥ । pramattapuruṣaḥ sarva saṃsārānnaiva mucyate ।। pramādapāśapāśena yena baddhā hi dehinaḥ ।
akārya kāryasadṛśaṃ kārya kurvanti sarvadā ।। apramādānnaraḥ sarva viparītaṃ paśyati । na laukikeṣu kāryeṣu kuto na śraiyaseṣu ca ।। pramādaṃ na praśaṃsanti paṇḍitā buddhipāragāḥ ।
yathā śubhaṃ parikṣīṇaṃ bhaviṣyati divaukasām ।। tadā pramādasya phalaṃ jñāsyanti kaṭukaṃ hi tat । kāmasaṃsaktamanasāṃ tasyānte sukhasevinām ।। bhaviṣyati sukhaṃ tasmād vinipātodayo mahān ।
viṣayābhimukhepsūnāṃ nityamāśāgatātmanām ।। strīdarśanasumattānāṃ vinipāto bhaviṣyati । niṣevante pramādarāgasevinaḥ ।। tāḥ sarvā mṛtyusamaye parityakṣyanti yoṣitaḥ ।
cyavamānaṃ suraṃ sarve na kaścidanugacchati ।। karmaṇā pṛṣṭhataḥ sarva gacchantamanuyāti ca । yuktaṃ ca sadā sevyaṃ varjanīyaṃ ca duṣkṛtam ।। pramādaṃ ca madaṃ jahayāt pramāda rato bhavet ।
pramādo bhavamūlo ayaṃ pramādastu na śāntaye ।। apramādapramādābhyāmidamuktaṃ svalakṣaṇam । tad vicintya sadā dhīraḥ sukhaṃ sucaritaṃ caret ।। na dharmacārī puruṣaḥ kadācid duḥkhamṛcchaiti ।
saṃsarantyatha saṃsāre prāṇinaḥ svena karmaṇā ।। kimarthamihaloko ayaṃ pramādena vihanyate । pramādaḥ śreyasāṃ nāśaḥ pramādo bandhanaṃ param ।। pramādo vinipātāya pramādo narakāya ca ।
duḥkhasya heturevaikaḥ pramādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। tasmāt sukhārthī puruṣaḥ pramādaṃ parivarjayet । yaiḥ pramādaḥ parityaktaḥ prāptaṃ taiḥ padamacyutam ।। apramādarato yo hi nirvāṇasyaiva so antike ।
apramādapadaṃ hayetannirvāṇasyāgrataḥ padam ।। pramādo vinipātāya hetureṣaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । pramattaḥ puruṣaḥ sarvaḥ sonmāda iva lakṣyate ।। laghutvaṃ yāti loke asmin pratyavāyeṣu pacyate ।
pramattaḥ puruṣaḥ śakto viparīteṣu vartate ।। hetau karmavipāke ca mṛtyūtpattau tathaiva ca । pramādāgniśca yaṃ tīkṣṇo narakānupakarṣati । tasmānnarakamokṣārtha pramādaṃ vinivarjayet ।।
ye pramādaṃ vinirjitya nityaṃ jñānaratā narāḥ । te kleśabandhanaṃ chitvā padaṃ yātāḥ sukhodayam ।। karmasūtrairnibaddhāśca cittadolāṃ samāśritāḥ । bhramanti vibhave sattvā mā pramādeṣu rakṣathaḥ ।।
sukhī bhavati duḥkhī vai duḥkhitaścāpi sukhitaḥ । bhartāpi tṛpto bhavati mā pramādeṣu rakṣathaḥ ।। mātā pitā vā bhavati bhāryā mātṛtvameva ca । parivarto mahāneṣu mā pramādeṣu rakṣathaḥ ।।
pramādājjāyate rāgo rāgād dveṣaḥ prapadyate । sa doṣapathamāpanno narakānupadhāvati ।। prajñāprāsādamāroha yogakṣemamanuttamam । eṣa panthāḥ śivaḥ śreṣṭho yaḥ pramādavivarjitaḥ ।
tena mārgeṇa satataṃ nirvāṇaṃ yānti paṇḍitāḥ ।। virodho mārgasampattau cittasantānadūṣakaḥ । āchettā dharmasetūnāṃ pramādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। smṛti sandūṣakaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mokṣāya vṛttināśakaḥ ।
durgatīnāṃ paraṃ netā pramādaḥ sampravartate ।। aneka puruṣaḥ kṣipto nātmano vindate hitam । nāvācyaṃ na ca kāryāṇāṃ vindate amṛtakopamaḥ ।। ta ete paśubhistulyā devavigrahadhāriṇaḥ ।
pramādopahatā mūḍhā nṛtyanti ca hasanti ca ।। utpannāvicyutāḥ mārgāt kṣāntiṃ ye nāśayanti ca । nṛbhavārṇavabhūtā ye te pramādānudhāvinaḥ ।। janakaḥ sarvadoṣāṇāṃ bandhanaṃ pāpakarmaṇām ।
pramoṣaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ pramādāriḥ pravartate ।। nādhyātmikāni karmāṇi na bāhayāni kathañcana । pramādopahato janturjānīte naṣṭamāsanaḥ ।। krīḍāyāṃ vyagramanaso nṛtyagāndharvalālasāḥ ।
atṛṣṇārviṣayairdivyairnakṣyanti vibudhālayāḥ ।। bhayasthāne hasantyete pramādena vimohitāḥ । mārgāmārga na vindanti jātyandhena surāḥ samāḥ ।। kāmadhātau bhramanyete cakravadgati pañcake ।
dhyānebhyo yaddhi patanaṃ tat pramādasya ceṣṭitam ।। ārūpyebhyaśca yatsthānaṃ caturthaṃ prāpyalaukikāt । bhramanti bhramadolāyāṃ tat pramādasya ceṣṭitam ।। pramādabandhanairbaddhaṃ tṛṣṇāpāśaiśca yantritam ।
traidhātukamidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ na ca buddhayantya cetasaḥ ।। yat prayānti dharmasthānaṃ tṛṣṇābhayadarśitāḥ । na bhūyaḥ khedamāyāti tat pramādasya ceṣṭitam ।। priyaviśleṣajaṃ nṛṇāṃ yadduḥkhaṃ hṛdi jāyate ।
sevanād yat pramādasya kathayanti tathāgatā ।। anarthā hi trayo loke yairidaṃ naśyate jagat । vyādhirjarā ca mṛtyuśca pramādālasya sambhavāḥ ।। prarohanti yathā bhūmau savauṣadhitṛṇādayaḥ ।
tathā pramādināṃ kleṣāḥ pravartante pṛthagvidhāḥ ।। strīśleṣo madyapānaṃ ca krīḍā ca viṣayaiḥ saha । cāpalyamayakausīdyaṃ pramādasya viṣāṅkuraḥ ।। pramādaḥ paramaṃ duḥkhapramādaḥ paraṃ sukham ।
samāsāllakṣaṇaṃ proktamapramādapramādayoḥ ।। tasmāt pramādo na nareṇa sevyaḥ, sa durgatīnāṃ prathamāgrameva । vihāya taṃ duḥkhasahastrayoniṃ, prayānti buddhā bhavapāragrayam ।। ।। iti apramādavargaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ ।।
na kāmeṣu ratiṃ kuryāt kāmāḥ paramavañcakāḥ । saṃsārabandhanā ghorāḥ sarve narakahetavaḥ ।। yaḥ saṃrakṣati kāmeṣu tasya duḥkhamanantakam । na kāmoragadaṣṭasya sukhamasti kathañcana ।।
varaṃ niśitadhāreṇa kṣureṇa svayamātmanaḥ । saṃkṣoditā bhavejjihvā na coktaṃ kāmagaṃva ।। rāgeṇa vañcitāḥ sattvā dveṣeṇa paripīḍitāḥ । mohasya vaśamāpannā bhāṣante amadhuraṃ vacaḥ ।।
alparāgānniruddho yaḥ kurute duṣkṛtaṃ bahu । sa rāgavaśago mūḍho duḥkhād duḥkhamavāpnuyāt ।। atṛptirasmāt kāmāste na sukhā nāpi śāśvatāḥ । pariṇāme mahātīvrāstasmāt tān parivarjayet ।।
rāgābhibhūtāḥ puruṣā narakālayavartinaḥ । na rāgavaśagā ye tu na teṣāṃ narakād bhayam ।। caṇḍācaṇḍisamutthāśca caṇḍāśca pariṇāmataḥ । kāmā viṣāgnipratimāḥ parivarjyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
parivarjitakāmasya nityaṃ mokṣaratasya ca । naśyantyakuśalā dharmāstamaḥ sūryodaye tathā ।। indriyāṇīndriyārthajño mohayitvā pṛthagvidhāḥ । narake pātayantyete kāmāḥ bālamanoharāḥ ।।
pañcendriyaprasaktasya viṣayaiḥ pañcabhistathā । muhūrtamapi rāgāgnirviṣayairnaiva tṛpyati ।। saṃśleṣājjāyate vahnirviśleṣānnaiva jāyate । saṃśleṣādapi viśleṣo gnirjīryate nṛṇām ।।
dūrānna dāhako vahnirviṣayastasya nāsti saḥ । dūrāntikasamo ghoro rāgāgniratidāhakaḥ ।। saṅkalpakāṣṭhaprabhavaḥ spṛhākuṭilavegavān । tṛṣṇā ghṛtaprasakto ayaṃ rāgāgnirapi dāhakaḥ ।।
dagdhvā śarīrametaddhi jvalanaḥ sampraśāmyate । nāmarūpavinirmukto rāgāgnirnaiva śāmyate ।। udvejayati bhūtāni vahniḥ paramadāhakaḥ । rāgāgniratitīkṣṇo api nodvegaṃ kurute nṛṇām ।।
pañcendriyasamuttho ayaṃ viṣayaiḥ pañcabhirvṛtaḥ । tṛṣṇāsamīraṇabalād rāgāgni prajāḥ ।। vitarkāraṇisambhūto viṣayaiḥ parivardhitaḥ । kāṣṭhavad dahyate tena na ca dṛśyo janasya saḥ ।।
yathā yathā hi prabalo rāgāgnistapyate mahān । tathā tathā rāgāndhaiḥ svasukhaṃ parisevyate ।। agniḥ prakāśako bhavati rāgāgnistamasāvṛtaḥ । tasmācchiśiravad dhīmān rāgāgniṃ parivarjayet ।।
viṣayābhirato janturna sukhī syāt kathañcana । viṣayāḥ viṣayairdaṣṭāḥ pariṇāme ca dāruṇāḥ ।। nādye nānte na madhye ca nāsmiṃlloke na cāpare । sukhadā viṣayā kāmaṃ bhavantīha kathañcana ।।
bāliśasya hi sarvasya tṛṣṇākrīḍanasaṃbhavaiḥ । na tṛpto viṣayairagnirjvalanasya yathendhanaiḥ ।। atṛptoḥ viṣayaiḥ sarvo jano ayaṃ parivañcitaḥ । mṛtyunābhyāsanirata etairdoṣairvidahyate ।।
sukhānāṃ kāmacārāṇāṃ mohasya khalu ceṣṭitam । tadeva yadi devānāṃ khagaiḥ syuste samāḥ surāḥ ।। kalpānteṣvabhisantaptaḥ śasyate saritāṃ patiḥ । na dṛṣṭistṛpyate rūpaiḥ kalpakoṭiśatairapi ।।
syāt samudrasya caryāptiḥ salilairvaśagādibhiḥ । na tu dṛṣṭiḥ samudrasya rūpārthaistṛptirasti hi ।। avitṛptasya kāmebhyaḥ kiṃ sukhaṃ parikalpyate । tṛptiryāsti vitṛṣṇasya gataśokasya dehinaḥ ।।
mādyante bahumohāndhā na ca buddhayanti bāliśāḥ । mandena kṣaṇikā yadvat malayendhanapādapāḥ ।। svapnapramoṣadharmāṇo gandharvanagaropamāḥ । riktāstucchā asārāśca kāmāḥ paramavañcakāḥ ।।
mā mohena samāḥ kiṃ pākasadṛśopamāḥ । kāmā lokahitakarā vahnivat parikīrtitāḥ ।। kāmasyādīnavaṃ jñātvā yena tatphalamohitāḥ । tena taddarśakāḥ prītā gatakāṃkṣasya ।।
nyathā cintyamānānāṃ yathā prāptā punastathā । sarvataḥ pāpakartāraḥ kāmā loke viṣopamāḥ ।। kāmairatṛptamanasaste te devāścyutāḥ punaḥ । patanti narake mūḍhāḥ kāmena parivañcitāḥ ।।
nadītaraṅgacapalā vidyullekhasamāśca te । mīnāvartabalā nāryaḥ kāmalokaviṣāspadāḥ ।। vicintitā vivardhante varddhitā vahnisannibhāḥ । ādau cānte tathā kāmāstasmāt kāmān vivarjayet ।।
yathā yathā hi sevyante vivardhante tathā tathā । vahnijvālāsamāsṛṣṭāḥ kāmāḥ kaṭuvipākinaḥ ।। evaṃ doṣaṃ sadā jñātvā dhīraḥ kāmān vivarjayet । parivartitakāmasya sukhaṃ bhavati naiṣṭhikam ।।
asaṅkhyāni sahasrāṇi devānāṃ niyutāni ca । patanti kāmadahanaṃ narakaṃ vahnibhairavam ।। yathāgniviṣaśastrāṇi varjayanti sukhārthinaḥ । tathā kāmāḥ sadā varjyā hetavo narakasya te ।।
na dṛṣṭo na śrutaḥ kaścid yaḥ kāmavaśagaḥ pumān । na kāmairvipralabdhaḥ syānna ca duḥkhena pīḍitaḥ ।। tasmādalamalaṃ kāmairmā caiteṣu manaḥ kṛthāḥ । sarve sarvāsvavasthāsu kāmā vahniviṣopamāḥ ।।
anādirmati saṃsāre śatravaścittasambhavāḥ । ahantvāttu bhavet prītirna sā kāmaiḥ kathañcana ।। sakalmaṣā kaṭuphalā duḥkhāt kāmodbhavā ratiḥ । yā tu kāmavinirmuktā sā ratiḥ pari ।।
tāṃ samāśritya gacchanti yoginaḥ paramāṃ gatim । na tu kāmakṛtā prītirnayate padamacyutam ।। āpātamadhurā ramyā vipāke jvalanopamā । ratirbhavati kāmāgnijanyā narakagāminī ।।
āpātaramyā madhurā madhye ramyā ca sarvadā । śāntamante ca vimalaṃ nayate padamacyutam ।। ādyantamadhyakalyāṇī nityaṃ māteva śobhanā । tāṃ vyudasya kathaṃ bālā rakṣante ।।
madhyādinidhane duḥkhā nityaṃ doṣādibhirvṛtā । kathaṃ sā sevyate bālairyā na dṛṣṭā sukhāvahā ।। viṣamañjarivad ramyā sparśe jvalanasambhavā । tathā kāmakṛtā prītiḥ pariṇāme viṣopamā ।।
hūyamāno yathā vahnirjvalanena praśāmyati । dāhena ca prarohaḥ syāt tadvat kāmakṛtā ratiḥ ।। pataṅgaḥ paśyati hyagni dāhadoṣaṃ na paśyati । tathā kāmakṛtāṃ prītiṃ paśyantyakṛtabuddhayaḥ ।।
yastu rāgakṛto dāhaḥ pacyate kāmināṃ sadā । pataṅgasadṛśaṃ dāhaṃ sarvathā nai paśyati ।। tasmāt kāma tyaktvā nityaṃ jīvatha he surāḥ । bhavantu mā vṛthā janmapramādena prapātanam ।।
saṃkṣīṇaśubhakarmāṇo nityaṃ kāmairvimohitāḥ । taṃ hitvā narakaṃ yānti kāmamohena vañcitāḥ ।। viṣavṛkṣamayaṃ puṣpaṃ pīyate bhramarairyathā । tathā viṣātmakamidaṃ sukhaṃ bhuṅkte hi mohitaḥ ।।
jīveyuḥ pāmarāḥ kecit viṣaṃ pītvāpi durbhagāḥ । na kāmaviṣapītasya jīvitaṃ durlabhaṃ bhavet ।। yathā hi narake vahnirjvalayatya vicāriṇam । tathā kāmamayo vahnirdahatīha divaukasaḥ ।।
śrutipāśamayo vahniḥ pretāneṣa dahatyati । dahane hiṃsako vahnirnṛṇāṃ paryeṣaṇātmakaḥ ।। evamagnisamaṃ tāvat parihārya samantataḥ । sarvalokamaśeṣeṇa dahyate kāmamohitaḥ ।।
viṣayeṣu sadācittaṃ dhāvantaṃ cañcalaṃ mahat । na tyājyaṃ vyasane mūḍha yad paśyasi bhaviṣyati ।। kāmeṣu rakṣa te cittaṃ vyasanenāvabudhyate । vyasanaughe samutpanne tat paścāt paritapyate ।।
vṛthā kāmamadairmattā devāḥ prakṛtidurbalāḥ । bhramanti bhramitāḥ kāmairna paśyanti mahad bhayam ।। viśvasanti hi ye devāḥ kāmeṣvahitakāriṣu । vyatirekeṣu te paścāt pratibudhyantyamedhasaḥ ।।
na ca paśyanti budhāścittena parivañcitāḥ । kṣaṇikā madhurā jātāḥ kāmāḥ paramavañcakāḥ ।। śataśaśca sahastraiśca koṭiśaḥ padmaśastathā । labdhā naṣṭā punaḥ kāmā na teṣāṃ viścaset pumān ।।
viṣayād bandhanaṃ tīvraṃ sarve narakahetavaḥ । tasmādatyantatastyaktvā śreyase kriyatāṃ manaḥ ।। rāgeṇa rañjitāḥ pūrvaṃ dveṣeṇa ca tiraskṛtāḥ । mohena mohitāścaiva te aśrutākṛtakāriṇaḥ ।।
kāmārthaireṣyate bālaḥ punaḥ kāmairvimohitaḥ । sa pataṅgasamo mūḍhaḥ dahyate narakāgninā ।। avaśyambhāvi patanaṃ suralokāt samantataḥ । na jñātvā kāmavaśago syādiha kathañcana ।।
kāmena vañcitāḥ sattvāḥ kāmena ca vimohitāḥ । kāmapāśāpakṛṣṭāste patanti narake sadā ।। tadetad vyasanaṃ sattvāḥ svahite kriyatāṃ manaḥ । manasāpi svadāntena nānutapyanti dehinaḥ ।।
manoviṣeṇa ye daṣṭāḥ kāmavegena sarvadā । te mūḍhā mṛtyuvaśagāḥ kāmānalahatā narāḥ ।। na tṛptirasti kāmānāṃ tṛṣṇayā hitakāriṇām । tṛṣṇāpi tṛptijanikā mano naiva hi tṛpyati ।।
na jātu viṣayaistṛptirindriyāṇāṃ bhaviṣyati । yadi na jñānadīpena kṣapayiṣyanti ।। yoṣitaḥ sevyamānā hi vitarkaśatamālikāḥ । pravardhati yathā vahnirvāyunā samudīritaḥ ।।
taṃ matvā vegarabhasā nityaṃ kāmo agnidīpitaḥ । kāmān hāpayati jñānī buddhatattvavicintakaḥ ।। ye nityaṃ bhrāntamanaso nityaṃ viṣayatatparāḥ । ramante vibudhāḥ sarve tat sarvaṃ mohaceṣṭitam ।।
sevyamāno hi vibudhairviṣayāgnirvivardhate । pāśenānena saṃyukto vahnirvāyusamīritaḥ ।। amarāḥ rāgavivaśā nityaṃ viṣayatatparāḥ । devalokāt patantyete moharāgeṇa vañcitāḥ ।।
ramante viṣayairete tatra tallīnamānasāḥ । na ca vindanti yad duḥkhaṃ viprayogo bhaviṣyati ।। yadetat sukhamevādau divyaṃ pañcaguṇānvitam । viyogajasya duḥkhasya kalāṃ nārhatiṣoḍaśīm ।।
kāmānāṃ tadvighāto hi janenaivopayujyate । satṛṣṇasya tathā tṛptiḥ kāmebhyo naiva jāyate ।। anapekṣitacittasya nityaṃ kāmānusevinaḥ । dīrgharātrānuśayikaṃ duḥkhaṃ naiva praśāmyate ।।
tvaritaṃ rakṣyate mūḍho vyasanenaiva budhyate । paścāttu vyasane prāpte jānīte yasya tat phalam ।। āsvādabhadrakā hyete kāmāḥ paramadāruṇāḥ । dūtakān narakasyaitān carantyahitakāriṇaḥ ।।
yasteṣāṃ viśvaset martyo jñānacakṣurvigarhitaḥ । viṣayāgnirabhratulyaḥ sa yāti narakaṃ naraḥ ।। alpāsvādālpahṛdayā nityaṃ puruṣavañcakāḥ । gandharvanagaraprakhyāḥ kāmā āsvādabhadrakāḥ ।।
dīpaprabhā sañchanneva punaḥ punaḥ । na ca bindatyamanaso devā viṣayamohitāḥ ।। viṣayeṇātirabhasā nityaṃ kāmavaśānugāḥ । na vidanti mahad duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
ramaṇīyāni kāmāni yasyaivaṃ jāyate matiḥ । sa paścād vyasane prāpte mūḍho asau vipralapyate ।। na kāmena madāndhasya viṣayairmohitasya ca । naityikaṃ bhavati śarmma yatsukhānāmanuttamam ।।
yacca kāmasukhaṃ loke yacca tṛṣṇodbhavaṃ sukham । ekasyādhyātmikasyedaṃ kalāṃ nārhatiṣoḍaśīm ।। na sukhī vartate tāvadya yasya kāmo hṛdi sthitaḥ । sa sarvaduḥkhabhāgārho narakānupadhāvati ।।
na tṛptirvidyate kāmairapi śataṃ nṛṇām । yatra saukhyaṃ na tatrāsti tṛptirviṣayasevinām ।। sevyamānāḥ sadā kāmā vardhante ca muhurmuhuḥ । te vardhitā viṣasamā bhavanti vinipātinaḥ ।।
vipattikuśalā ghorā nityaṃ patanahetavaḥ । na ca teṣāṃ parityāgaṃ kurvanti viṣayotsavāḥ ।। yasya dṛṣṭisamudrasya rūpaistṛptirna vidyate । tathā śarmamanojñaiśca rasatṛptirna vidyate ।।
gandhairapi sadā ghrāṇaṃ na tṛptimadhigacchati । sparśāḥ sammukhasaṃsparśāḥ sevyante naiva tṛpyate ।। śabdaiḥ kāntaiḥ sumadhuraiḥ śrotrameti na tarpaṇam । mano api tṛptiviśvastaṃ vardhamānaṃ na tṛpyati ।।
ṣaḍendriyāṇi capalānyādhṛtāni ratau punaḥ । bhramanti muṣitā nityaṃ kāmabhūmiṣvanekaśaḥ ।। na tṛptirasti devānāṃ gajānāṃ vai tṛṇairyathā । analasya svabhāvo ayaṃ tasya tṛptirna vidyate ।।
ṣaḍete vahnayastīvrā vitarkānilamūrchitāḥ । bhramanti muṣitā nityaṃ kāmabhūmiṣvanekaśaḥ ।। tairayaṃ dahyate loko na ca vindatyabuddhimān । āsvādabhadrakā hayete narakasya ca hetavaḥ ।।
kāmā viṣayalobhāste lelihānā yathoragāḥ । vilocanavaro hayeṣa na ca kāmairvimohitaḥ ।। sukhānusāriṇaḥ kāmo narakānupadhāvati । na netrahīno narake pātyate satkriyānvitaḥ ।।
tasmād varaṃ vicakṣuḥ syānna tu kāmavaśo naraḥ । aśakyavañcitā mūḍhāḥ kāmairahitakāribhiḥ ।। anirvidyanti kāmebhyo mohitāḥ svena cetasā । na jñānaṃ nāpi vijñānaṃ vidyate kāmacāriṇām ।।
yad duḥkhakāmajaṃ hatvā punaḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ । mitrarūpā ca ye kāmāḥ kimpākaphalasannibhāḥ । nayanti mṛtyubhavanaṃ durgatīśca punaḥ punaḥ ।। anivarttya yathā toyamāpagānāmanekaśaḥ ।
tathā saukhyagataṃ nṛṇāṃ sarvathā na vivartate ।। vanopavanabhogeṣu sukhaprāpteṣvanekaśaḥ । yo na tṛpyati kāmeṣu sa naro adhamagāmikaḥ ।। pramādo pahato jantuḥ kāmāsvādeṣu tatparaḥ ।
rūpeṣu rakṣyate nityaṃ pariṇāme ca vidyate ।। ghanacchāyāsvarūpāṇi karmamiśrāṇi yāni vai । tāni caiva kathaṃ devāḥ śakṣyante kāmagocare ।। yadi nityā bhaveyurna kāmāste syurviṣopamāḥ ।।
tathāpi kāmatṛṣṇā yā na sā jāti vilakṣaṇā । prāgeva nityaṃ duḥkhāya śūnyamātmānameva ca ।। teṣu duḥkhavipākeṣu kathaṃ rakṣantyabuddhayaḥ । kāmāsvādeṣu rakṣyante bāliśāḥ mandabuddhayaḥ ।
ādīnavaṃ na buddhayante kimpākaphalasannibham ।। rūpaśabdādibaddho ayaṃ tṛṣṇāviprakṛto janaḥ । dīpyate vivaśo nityaṃ, kukarmaphalamohitam ।। āsvādayitvā puruṣāḥ kāmān viṣaphalopamān ।
tṛṣṇayā tṛptamanasaḥ patanti narake punaḥ ।। yathābhivarṣate toyaṃ vardhante sarito yathā । tathā kāmābhivarṣeṇa devānāṃ vardhate analaḥ ।। jalasambhavamīno api dṛśyate tṛṣṇayāturaḥ ।
evaṃ sukhābhivṛddhā ca na vitṛpyati devatā ।। ākāśasya yathā nānto vidyate nāpi saṃśayaḥ । evaṃ kāmeṣu nāstyantaḥ kāmināṃ nāsti saṃkṣayaḥ ।। salilādibhiratṛptasya sāgarasyormimālinaḥ ।
na tu kāmairatṛptasya tṛptirasti kathañcana ।। aprāptairviṣayairdevā na vitṛpyanti bāliśāḥ । viṣayairnaiva tṛpyanti sukhalālasatatparāḥ ।। saṃprāpte vyasane tīvre cyavamānepyanekaśaḥ ।
tapyate viṣaye tasmāt paraṃ kāmo na śakyate ।। vilokya puruṣānete kāmaviśvāsaghātinaḥ । tyajanti vyasane prāptā vipadyante hi te narāḥ ।। atṛptasya sukhaṃ nāsti viṣayaiścāpi tṛpyate ।
ye vā tṛiptikarā dṛṣṭāstān buddhvā vivarjayet ।। sukhamūlā sadā śāntirasukhā viṣayā matāḥ । tasmācchāntisukhā devā varjayitvā viṣayoragān ।। badhabandhanarogādi viṣayebhyo mahadbhayam ।
sambhrāntiriha saṃsāre viṣayaireva jāyate ।। saṃyogā viprayogāntāḥ śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ । jātau jātau sadā dṛṣṭāḥ saugataistattvadarśibhiḥ ।। anekasukhasaṃsāro viṣayeṣu hi vidyate ।
viṣayaiśca bhavet sarva jātau jātau prajāyate ।। kaṣṭairyairanakāmairna śakyate amūḍhacetasā । punastāneva mohāndhāḥ sevante akṛtabuddhayaḥ ।। varjate hi sadā śatruvañcanāśaṅkayā naraḥ ।
viṣayāḥ śatrubhūtā hi na vaśyante kathañcana ।। kāmabaddhāḥ sadā mohabāliśā vā bhavanti te । na tyajanti kathaṃ mūḍhā mohitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।। yathā bahnibhayāt kaścid vahnimevopasevate ।
tathā viṣayasaṃmūḍho viṣayānupasevate ।। snāyusaṅgrathitaḥ pāśo dṛṣṭiramyo yathā bhavet । tathā viṣayaramyo ayaṃ pāśaḥ paramadāruṇaḥ ।। kiṃpākasya yathāsvādo madhurāgro mahodayaḥ ।
paścād bhavati nāśāya sukhaṃ tadvadidaṃ nṛṇām ।। pradīpasya śikhāṃ yāvat pataṅgo mohamūrchitaḥ । patate dahyate caiva tathedaṃ sukhamiṣyate ।। ajñātvā hi tathā bālā ramyadehasukhecchayā ।
spṛśanti jvalanaṃ tadvat sukhametad bhaviṣyati ।। yathā ramyo vanamṛgastṛṣṇārta upadhāvati । na ca tṛṣṇāvighāto asya tadidaṃ sukhamiṣyate ।। na tṛptā na ca tṛpyanti na ca tṛptirbhaviṣyati ।
viṣayaiḥ sarvadevānāṃ tasmāt kāmo na śāntaye ।। pratyutpannasukhāḥ kāmā nāntakalyāṇakārakāḥ । rañjitā viṣayairdevā vikṣiptamanasaḥ sadā ।। nānāsaukhyapramattasya viṣayairvañcitasya ca ।
samprāpte mṛtyukāle ca na śamāyāsya vidyate ।। anukrameṇa maraṇamabhyeti tacca vidyate । viṣayāpahatairdevaiḥ kāmavyāsaktabuddhibhiḥ ।। jānīyādadya me devā yad duḥkhaṃ viprayogajam ।
muhūrtamapi kāmeṣu na kuryāt tatra saṃsthitim ।। anityātmabhayāḥ kāmā nityaṃ cāhitakāriṇaḥ । tathā vimohitān kālaḥ punastānanusevate ।। rāgāgninā pradahayante nityaṃ devāḥ pramohitāḥ ।
dahyamānāḥ punastattvaṃ praśaṃsanti punaḥ punaḥ ।। viṣayeṣu na rakṣyante teṣāṃ duḥkhamiva sthitam । traidhātukamidaṃ sarva bhrāmyate rathacakravat ।। sattvā avidyayā mugdhā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhoginaḥ ।
vidyudālātacakreṇa samāḥ kāmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ । svapne gandharvanagarasadṛśā vipralambhinaḥ ।। anityaduḥkhaśūnyeṣu na kuryānmatimātmavān । pañcaskandhāsuraiḥ proktaḥ śubhai riktaḥ svabhāvataḥ ।।
anyathā viṣavad vijñaḥ kāmeṣu ca prasahyate । sa budhaḥ pāragaḥ śāntaḥ sattvānāmanukampakaḥ ।। nirvāṇonmukha eva doṣācchāntimadhigacchati hitvā kleśamayaṃ pāśaṃ nirvāṇasyāntike sthitaḥ ।। prabhavenna ca doṣeṣu kāmacaryāratasya ca ।
vibhrāntamanasastasya kutaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati? ।। vibhrāntaṃ paśyatu mano viṣayeṣu pradhāvati । saddharmapathavibhrānto narakeṣūpapadyate ।। aśaktaprāptavibhraṣṭe kiṃ kāmairvidyutopamaiḥ ।
kiṃpākaviṣaśastrāgnisannibhairduḥkhahetubhiḥ? ।। yathā yathā hi sevyante vardhante te tathā tathā । avitṛptikarā hyete vahnidāhasya hetavaḥ ।। dāhadoṣeṇa sambhrāntāḥ ye surāḥ sukhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।
varjayitvāśivān kāmāstataḥ saukhyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। vañcayitvā janaṃ mūḍhaṃ śāṭī kṛtyeva bandhanam । pratyayo netracapalaḥ kāmā vidyud guṇopamāḥ ।। uparyupari kāmā yaiḥ sevyante kāmatṛṣṇayā ।
te rāgavahninā dagdhā dāhād dāhamavāpnuyāt ।। atimūḍhatamā hyete ye surāḥ kāmamohitāḥ । athavā ye na gacchanti yatsukhāt sukhamuttamam ।। nirvāṇagāmino nāsti vinā muktyā kutaḥ sukham? ।
tasmāt kāmānna seveta kaṣṭaḥ kāmasamāgamaḥ ।। indriyāṇi na tṛpyante viṣayai rāgasevinaḥ । atṛptau ca kutaḥ śarma sarvathā sampraveśate ।। tasyāgramubhayād vetti saṃsārād duḥkhasāgarāt ।
kāmān tṛṣṇāviṣayagān parityajati pāpakān ।। etāni girikūṭāni ramyāṇi vividhairdrumaiḥ । dhyāyante tāni saṃśritya kāmānāmudayavyayau ।। na kāmabandhanestṛptāḥ kāmajaṃ nidhanaṃ hi tat ।
na śīlaśraddhe yeneṣṭe labhyate aśivakāraṇam । kāmajaṃ nidhanaṃ hyetat saṃsārāṭavideśakam ।। yatra kāmavisaṃyuktaṃ bandhanaṃ vanamucyate । yatra bhāsayate pāpād yatra śāntiḥ sukhāvahā ।
tat kevalaṃ mahājñānaṃ kathyate nidhanaṃ dhanam ।। ye prasaktā na kāmeṣu tṛṣṇayā na pralobhitāḥ । te śivaṃ sthānamāpannā na kāmāgnipraveśakāḥ ।। tṛptirnāsti sadā kāmairna kāmāḥ śāntaye smṛtāḥ ।
tṛṣṇāsahāyasaṃyuktā jvalanti jvalanopamāḥ ।। avitṛptā vinaśyanti narā devāstathoragāḥ । te kevalaṃ praṇaṣṭā hi narakāgni pradarśakāḥ ।। vitarkāpahatasyāsya viṣayairvañcitasya ca ।
tṛṣṇayā mohitasyaiṣa mṛtyū rājā bhaviṣyati ।। saṃsaktakāmabhogeṣu pathyāpathyaṃ na vidyate । janā vimohitāḥ sarvaiviṣayaiḥ kāmasaṃjñakaiḥ ।। viṣayaireva kṛṣyante ye surā mūḍhacetasaḥ ।
ye buddhaguṇairyuktā na te kāmavaśānugāḥ ।। pratyutpanneṣu kāmeṣu sadoṣeṣu viśeṣataḥ । yo na muhyati saukhyeṣu sa adhīra' iti kathyate ।। svapnakāyavicitreṣu jvālāmālopameṣu ca ।
gandharvapuratulyeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।। tṛṣṇājanakabhūteṣu vināśāntakareṣu ca । kāntāreṣu viśāleṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।। ittvareṣu trichidreṣu nadīvegopameṣu ca ।
cañcaleṣvatidurgeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।। pavanoddhṛtavegormijalacandre caleṣu ca । atātacakralokeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।। samaṃ vidyullatācakramṛgatṛṣṇopameṣu ca ।
phenavaccāpyasāreṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।। kadalīgarbhatulyeṣu gajakarṇopameṣu ca । nadītaraṅgavegeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।। kiṃpākaphalatulyeṣu vahnisannibhajātiṣu ।
māyāraśminibheṣveṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।। jñānāṅkuśena vāryante viṣayāstattvadarśibhiḥ । ye amuktāścapalāstīvrāḥ sarvānarthakarā matāḥ ।। viṣayāśā ca mūḍhānāṃ saṅkalpahṛtacetasām ।
mṛtyupāśo ayamabhyeti jīvitāśā bandhakaḥ ।। pacanti niraye kāmāḥ prāṇinaṃ laghucetasam । na ca vindanti mūḍhā ye mohena parivañcitāḥ ।। viṣayāścapalāḥ sarve gandharvanagaropamāḥ ।
duḥkhasaṃvartakā hyete narakāḥ pañcahetavaḥ ।। saṅkalpājjāyate rāgaḥ rāgāt krodhaḥ pravartate । krodhābhibhūtaḥ puruṣo narakānupasevate ।। tasmāt kāmaṃ parityajya krodhaṃ nirvāsya paṇḍitaḥ ।
mohaṃ cāpi parityajya nirvāṇābhimukho bhavet ।। śatruvad viṣayā jñeyā nirvāṇaṃ caiva mitravat । pumān viśrāntaviṣayo nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।। alolupaḥ kāmamalairaliptaḥ prahīṇadoṣo hatavāṇatṛṣṇaḥ ।
saṃkṣīṇadoṣo vimalaprakāśaḥ prayāti śāntiṃ svaphalopabhogī ।। sarveṣu sattveṣu sadā sukhārthī । prāpnoti nirvāṇasukhaṃ prasahya ।। iti kāmajugupsāvargaḥ saptamaḥ ।
bhavotārāya tṛṣṇāgnirjvalanaḥ śīta ucyate । narake nārake yo agnistṛṣṇāgnistriṣu dhātuṣu ।। kalpabhūto hyayaṃ vahniḥ yo ayaṃ narakasambhavaḥ । bahujvālākulo vahniḥ tṛṣṇāhetusamudbhavaḥ ।।
karmakṣayād vimucyante narakāt pāpakāriṇaḥ । triṣu dhātuṣu dahyante narāstṛṣṇāvaśānugāḥ ।। anādimati saṃsāre tṛṣṇāgniratibandhakaḥ । tṛṣṇāgnirnarakaṃ tasmānnāgnirnarakasambhavaḥ ।।
gātradāhaṃ paraṃ kuryānnārakeyo hutāśanaḥ । śārīraṃ mānasaṃ dāhaṃ tṛṣṇāgniḥ kurute nṛṇām ।। tasmād viśiṣyate vahniḥ tṛṣṇāhetusamudbhavaḥ । nārakeyo asamaścaiva tṛṣṇāgnirnitarāṃ smṛtaḥ ।।
tristhānagaḥ trihetuśca trikarmaparidīpakaḥ । trikālasambhavo jñeyastṛṣṇāgniparakastathā ।। rāgāgnirdahyate svarge dveṣāgnistiryage tathā । mohāgnirdahyate pāpe tṛṣṇāgniḥ sarvadā sthitaḥ ।।
mānerṣyādhūmaviśikhaḥ saṅkalpe dhanasambhavaḥ । lobhāgnirdahate lokaṃ nāgniḥ kāmasamudbhavaḥ ।। lobhāśīviṣadaṣṭā ye teṣāṃ śarma na vidyate । sevito bhāvito lobho bhūya evābhivardhate ।।
yathā yathendhanaṃ prāpyānalo vardhatyanekaśaḥ । śakyaḥ pālayituṃ rlobhavahnirna ।। cakravad bhramate loko lobhena parivañcitaḥ । anādinidhane loke nāsti lobhasamo ripuḥ ।।
viśanti sāgarajale lobhena parivañcitāḥ । śastrasaṅghātagahanaṃ yuddhaṃ saṃpraviśanti ca ।। lobhahetorhi bhūpālā nāśayanti parasparam । śastrāsibhairavaprotā yuddhayante dhanatṛṣṇayā ।।
tṛṣṇāviṣavinirmuktā lobhāṅgāravivarjitā । samaloṣṭakāñcanā ye nirvāṇasyāntike hi te ।। atīvānupapannasya dhanalobhena dahyate । na vahnirviṣamastatra lobhāgniryatra vartate ।।
lobhādhāraprayatnena hanyāt tān rabhasā budhaḥ । anirvāpitalobhasya nirvāṇaṃ dūrataḥ sthitam ।। bhavābhilāṣiṇīṃ nāndīṃ nābhinandanti ye narāḥ । na teṣāṃ bhavajaṃ duḥkhaṃ svapne samupavidyate ।।
matsyān yathā jālabaddhān śambūkaḥ parikarṣati । tṛṣṇābaddhāṃstathā sattvānmṛtyuḥ samupakarṣati ।। saviṣaiḥ sāyakairviddho mṛgo yatra dhāvati । tatra tatra viṣaṃ yāti tathā tṛṣṇāviṣaṃ nṛṇām ।।
pravāhapravahannadyā gatirgatya'nudhāvinī । yathā nirdahate bālān śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।। āpātaramyā vipākajvalanopamāḥ । tasmāt tṛṣṇā vimoktavyā yadi saukhyaṃ hi rocate ।।
yathā hi vaḍiśagrastā mīnā mṛtyuvaśānugāḥ । tathā prataptā viṣayān paridhāvanti duḥkhitāḥ ।। narakaṃ nārakeyaṃ ca tṛṣṇānihitaṃ mahat । patanti nidhanā martyāḥ paradāropajīvinaḥ ।।
na ceṣṭitamanopāpatṛṣṇayā prerito muniḥ । ṣaḍindriyasamudbhūto viṣayendhanadāhakaḥ ।। tṛṣṇāgnirdahate devaṃ kāyāgnirna kathañcana । sukhāvṛtāḥ sukharatāḥ sukhe parivañcitāḥ ।।
patanaṃ nāvagacchanti tṛṣṇayā parivañcitāḥ । jvālāmālākulaḥ sarvaḥ saṃsārastṛṣṇayāvṛtaḥ ।। tṛṣṇāgninā vaśībhūtā janā gacchanti durgatim । tṛṣṇāgnibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ suralokaḥ samantataḥ ।।
dahyate vivaśo raktaḥ kāmabhogavaśīkṛtaḥ । yathā yathendhanaṃ prāpya jvalanaṃ saṃpravardhate ।। tathā tathā sukhaṃ prāpya tṛṣṇāgnirvardhate nṛṇām । parivartayate puṃsaḥ kāṣṭhāgnirdāhadīpakaḥ ।।
tṛṣṇāgnirdahate lokaṃ parihātuṃ na śakyate । ye viśālāṃ nadīṃ tīrṇā saṅkalpakṛtabhairavīm ।। te gatāḥ paramāṃ śāntiṃ yān hi tṛṣṇā na bādhate । tṛṣṇāpāśavimuktā ye saṅgadoṣavivarjitāḥ ।।
nirmuktapāpakalmāṣā vītaśokā hi te budhāḥ । kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi tṛṣṇayā vañcitā narāḥ ।। te tyajanti māyāmohavaśaṃgatāḥ । tṛṣṇayā vañcito lokastṛṣṇāmevopasevate ।।
lavaṇodaṃ tṛṣātoyaṃ yathā pibati nārikaḥ । na tena janturmuhuśca pariśuṣyati ।। viṣayeṣveva tṛṣṇārtaśceṣṭate puruṣo adhamaḥ । tasmāt tṛṣṇāṃ na seveta sā hi tṛṣṇā durāsadā ।।
tṛṣṇāvaśo hi puruṣaḥ saṃsārānnaiva mucyate । anuttamāni saukhyāni bhuktvā deveṣu jantavaḥ ।। tṛṣṇāpāśavikṛṣṭāste patanti narakaṃ punaḥ । asvatantrādikalyāṇaṃ nityaduḥkhamayaṃ kaṭu ।।
tṛṣṇāyāḥ sevanānmuktaḥ sanmārgamadhigacchati । satṛṣṇasya kutastuṣṭirviṣayeṣu bhaviṣyati ।। sā tṛptiryā vitṛṣṇasya vītaśokasya dehinaḥ । evaṃ vitarkavihitāḥ pramādena ca vañcitāḥ ।।
tṛṣṇayāḥ toṣitā devāḥ patanti narakaṃ punaḥ । viḍambaneyaṃ paramā yatsurā narakaṃ gatāḥ ।। krīḍakāḥ paramā bhūtvā kāmasya vaśamāgatāḥ । na codvijanti saṃsārān prāṇinaścittamohitāḥ ।।
duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ yānti tṛṣṇayā parivañcitāḥ । yathā yathā sukhasyāptirvardhate jālinī tathā ।। jālinīvahnidagdhasya narakānupakarṣati । satṛṣṇasya vitarkā ye teṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate ।।
avitarkavitarkantu mṛtyurājo vikarṣati । vitarkakāmavaśagāstṛṣṇāviṣayagāminaḥ ।। sukhasya bhoginaṃ dṛṣṭvā na vidvadbhistatheṣyate । kāmāsvādapramattānāṃ prāṇināṃ viṣayārthinām ।।
jālinī bādhate nityaṃ yathā badhnanti dehinaḥ । pañcālambanametattu tṛṣṇayā naiva dahayate ।। tṛṣṇāvimuktavimalā na pāpapuragāminaḥ । saṅkalpadoṣā kuṭilā tridoṣarajasodbhavāḥ ।।
pramādajalagambhīrāḥ strīrāgakṛtasevanāḥ । gītatūryasvarāḥ śīghraṃ surāpānācca cañcalāḥ ।। sañchannaviṣayā sarve manaḥ kṣiptataraṅgiṇaḥ । tṛṣṇānadīṣu viṣame vahanti na ca gocare ।।
gāhante te ca sammūḍhāḥ surā rāgeṇa vañcitāḥ । tridoṣakāṣṭhasaṃbhūtāḥ pramādānilavegataḥ ।। tṛṣṇānalaḥ suragaṇān dahate na ca te viduḥ । na kṣaṇo nāpi hi lavo na muhūrta kathañcana ।।
yā na tṛṣṇāvaśagataiḥ suraiḥ samupabhujyate । tṛṣṇābhūmiriyaṃ kāṣṭhā vitarkajalasambhṛtā ।। yasmin krīḍanti vivaśāḥ devāḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ । cittādinā pracaṇḍena tṛṣṇāviṣavisarpiṇā ।।
daṣṭānupañcaśīrṣeṇa kiṃ vṛthā vilapasyatha । tṛṣṇānadī viśāleyaṃ pañcatīrthasamudbhavā ।। tṛṣṇāmohendrajālena viprakīrṇena sarvadā । tathā prapañcitā devā yathā na śubhabhāginaḥ ।।
nendriyāṇi sadā kāmaistṛpyanti hi kathañcana । saṃvardhate tathā tṛṣṇā ghṛtasikto yathānalaḥ ।। nānāvidhaiḥ sukhaireṣā jālinī lokanāśinī । narakapretatiryakṣu bhrāmayantī narān sadā ।।
mṛtyūpapattidolāyāṃ śliṣyante bāliśāḥ janāḥ । suśīlāvītatṛṣṇāśca gatāste paramāṃ gatim ।। nirmuktabandhanā dhīrā gataśokā gatavyathāḥ । sukhaṃ prāpnuvanti nityaṃ ye na tṛṣṇāvaśānugāḥ ।
janmaduḥkhamayaiḥ pāśairna te vidhyanti sūrayaḥ ।। yeṣāṃ sarvāsvavasthāsu jñāneṣu vihitaṃ manaḥ । animitte mano yeṣāṃ visṛṣṭā ye ca tṛṣṇayā । te vītamalakāntārāḥ pāraṃ prāptāḥ sukhodayam ।।
tṛṣṇāmohapramattā ye ratisaukhyāstathaiva ca । mohitāste devagaṇā bhramiṣyanti bhave bhave ।। kuṭṭanavyavahārā ye paricittāpahāriṇaḥ । avidyābahulā ye vā nityaṃ dāhābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।
na rātrau na divā teṣāṃ hṛdayaṃ suprasīdati ।। lobhābhibhūtamanasāṃ parivittābhikāṅkṣiṇām । teṣāṃ tuṣāgnikalpānāṃ viśvasenna svabhāvataḥ ।। bibheti hi naraḥ sarvaḥ sarpādiva viṣendhanāt ।
lobhena viṣayeṇaivābhibhūtāste narā bhṛśam ।। te mṛtā narakaṃ yānti pretayoniṃ tathaiva ca । tasmādapi vinirmuktā narakād vahnisammukhāt ।। pañcajanmaśatānyete bhavanti parikāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।
vivarṇā dīnavadanā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ । bhavanti manujāḥ sarve lobhopahatacetasaḥ ।। prahīṇalobhā ye santi nityaṃ jñānābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ । buddhimantaḥ sadā santaḥ te gatāḥ paramāṃ gatim ।
nirvāṇahṛdayā vītalobhamohāḥ sadā narāḥ ।। lobhāśīviṣadaṣṭasya vinipāto dhruvaṃ sthitaḥ । kriyamāṇo dhruvaṃ loko vardhate sa muhurmuhuḥ ।। śuṣkendhanaṃ samādāya yathā vahniḥ pravardhate ।
dhanatṛṣṇāratāḥ sattvāḥ dhanopārjanatatparāḥ ।। mṛtyukāle samutpanne tyajanti vivaśā dhanam । yacca tatsambhavaṃ yogāt tat sarva na vinaśyati ।। tena vittena lobhātmā nīyate narakaṃ bhṛśam ।
anyaistadbhujyate vittaṃ sa tu pāpena lipyate ।। prayānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ paścāttāpena dahyate । anartho hyartharūpeṇa sukharūpeṇa vā sukham ।। amitraṃ mitrarūpeṇa lobho ayaṃ hṛdi vartate ।
na lobhaṃ saṃśrayet prājño lobhāgnirdahyate sadā ।। tena dagdhā bhṛśaṃ sattvāḥ paścānnarakagāminaḥ । lokasādhāraṇā hyete vibhavāḥ sukhavarjitāḥ ।। teṣāmarthe kathaṃ pāpa kriyate mandabuddhibhiḥ ।
tṛṣṇābhayavimuktasya nirāśasya hi sarvataḥ ।। vītakāṅkṣasya dhīrasya nityaṃ padamavasthitam । sampattau dhābate loko vipattau nāvabudhyate ।। vipadantā hi sampattiḥ kṣayāntaṃ divasaṃ yathā ।
yathā tiṣṭhati sampattiḥ vipattiḥ pāpikā tathā ।। avitṛptasya kāmebhyastṛṣṇayā paridahyate । yasyeṣṭāḥ sampado nityaṃ sukhaṃ cābhimataṃ sadā ।। jani nāśayate tāsāṃ tṛṣṇā naṣṭā sukhāvahā ।
te devā narakaṃ yānti kāmabhogaistathārpitāḥ ।। analāceṣṭitaṃ sarva tad vadanti tathāgatāḥ । manuṣyā yacca narakaṃ prayā śataśastathā ।। ceṣṭitaṃ tad viśālāyāḥ yoṣikāyā vidurbudhāḥ ।
vimohitā na vindanti tvaritaṃ svalpajīvitam ।। sukṛtāni ca naśyanti tṛṣṇā naiva vinaśyati । bhave bhave gatā satvāḥ na vindanti śubhāśubham ।। śubhasya phalameveṣṭaṃ yat surāḥ paribhuñjate ।
aśubhasya tathā dṛṣṭamasukhaṃ vinipātajam ।। śubhāśubhaprahīṇā ye saṅgadoṣavivarjitāḥ । te gatāḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitam ।। pañcāraṃ bhavacakraṃ tat tṛṣṇānābhipuraḥsaram ।
