nadīrāgaparikṣiptaṃ na ca loko avabudhyate ।। doṣāvartatarā jñeyā saṅkalpamakarākulāḥ । tṛṣṇānadī viśāleyaṃ na ca loko avabudhyate ।। trikāle vañcanī tṛṣṇā nityamajñānakāriṇī ।
na tasyāṃ viśvased dhīmān saṃsārabandhanā hi sā ।। mitravad dṛśyate kāle śatruvacca nikṛntati । na tasyāṃ viśvaset prājñaḥ sā hi lokasya bandhanam ।। śakyaṃ hi bandhanaṃ chettumāyasaṃ dāruvattathā ।
na tṛṣṇābandhanaṃ chettuṃ nityaṃ kāmagaveṣibhiḥ ।। yasyeṣṭo bandhabhedo ayaṃ yasyeṣṭaṃ sukhamavyayam । sa tṛṣṇayā vimuktaḥ prajñāśo bhavet ।। jñānālokaḥ sukhāloko duḥkhaṃ tṛṣṇātamaḥsmṛtam ।
tasmādālokamāsthāya tamo nudati paṇḍitaḥ ।। jñānakhaḍgena tīkṣṇena tṛṣṇāvṛkṣaṃ nikṛntati । nikṛttavṛkṣaḥ naraḥ sukhaṃ prāpnotyanuttamam ।। doṣeṇa bahulā hyeṣā nadī prasravaṇākulā ।
doṣā netānahitvā bhavānmuñcati paṇḍitaḥ ।। tṛṣṇānadīṃ tripathagāṃ pramādāvartadustarām । prajñānāvaṃ samāśritya pāraṃ gacchantyanāmayam ।। mahecchatāmahacchatraṃ yena cāyānti bāliśāḥ ।
tasmānmahecchatā badhyā tvayeyaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā ।। mahecchatāvraṇastīvro hṛdaye yasya jāyate । na rātrau na divā tasya sukhaṃ bhavati lobhinaḥ ।। saṅkalpe tu na sambhūtaḥ tṛṣṇāvāyusamīritaḥ ।
mahecchatāmayo vahnirdahate hṛdayaṃ nṛṇām ।। lobhenāveṣṭitamanāḥ puruṣo laghucetasā । jīvitānyapi sārāṇi jahāti dhanatṛṣṇayā ।। pāpāni hi ca karmāṇi kurvanti puruṣāḥ kṣitau ।
dhanalābhena tat sarva pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। ye sāhasaṃ na kurvanti viśanti jvalanaṃ ca yat । tat sarva lobhadoṣeṇa kurvantyahitamātmanaḥ ।। śastrānilāni duḥkhāni vividhāni ca ।
viśanti narā mūḍhā lobhastatra hi kāraṇam ।। hṛdayastho manovahnirnityaṃ bahvicchatāṃ nṛṇām । alpecchatayā hṛcchāntirbhavatilābhinaḥ ।। yathāgnirindhanenaiva praśāntimadhigacchati ।
tathā vahvicchatāṃ nṛṇāṃ dhanairvṛddhiḥ prajāyate ।। bhūpālā dhanaistṛptāḥ koṭiśo nidhanaṃ gatāḥ । yāsyanti cānye nidhanaṃ tasmādalpecchatā sukham ।। duḥkhaṃ vahvicchatā nṛṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।
idamuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ । eṣa panthāḥ śivaḥ śreṣṭho yena tṛṣṇā vaśīkṛtā ।। ।। iti tṛṣṇāvargo aṣṭamaḥ ।। striyo mūlaṃ pāpasya dhananāśasya sarvathā ।
svahite ye na niratāḥ kutasteṣāṃ bhavet sukham ।। anarthakarmaratayaḥ śāṭhyerṣyābahulāstriyaḥ । lokadvayavināśāya puruṣāṇāmavasthitāḥ ।। nityaṃ sarāgakuśalā nityaṃ tadvacanāḥ parāḥ ।
anyacca hṛdaye tāsāṃ kathayantyanyadeva vā ।। āpātamadhurāḥ sūkṣmāḥ vipāke vajracetasaḥ । nopakāreṇa satkāraṃ smaranti laghucetasaḥ ।। nāśayitvā priyaśataṃ smarantyekaṃ hi vipriyam ।
vidyutsvabhāvahṛdayāḥ striyaḥ pāpasya bhūmayaḥ ।। strīhetunāśamicchanti puruṣā vakracetasaḥ । strīvināśo vināśo drāgiha loke paratra ca ।। evaṃ tu sarvaviṣayāḥ strīdarśanamihaikajam ।
abhibhūya sarvaviṣayān nāryagnijvalanaṃ mahat ।। saṃśleṣādapi viśleṣaḥ smaraṇāt kathanādapi । strīṇāṃ dāhasamuttho ayaṃ vahnirantarjahāsakaḥ ।। rāgeṇa saha jāyante nityaṃ vai dāruṇāḥ striyaḥ ।
dānena saha jāyante yathā loke hutāśanāḥ ।। na bhavet tādṛśo dāho yo ayaṃ vahnisamudbhavaḥ । yādṛśaḥ strīmado hyasti dehināṃ hṛdayodbhavaḥ ।। sarvalokavināśāya sarvadharmakṣayāya ca ।
hetavo narakasyaitāḥ striyaḥ proktā maharṣibhiḥ ।। mukhato madhurāmarṣā hṛdayena viṣopamāḥ । anavasthitasauhārdā nāsāṃ kaścit priyo naraḥ ।। muhūrtena priyastāsāṃ muhūrtena tathāpriyaḥ ।
anavasthitasauhārdāścañcalā kṣaṇikopamāḥ ।। vañcanāhetukuśalā nityaṃ kāryaparāyaṇāḥ । nityaṃ saṃyogamanaso nityaṃ mānaparāyaṇāḥ ।। devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ ।
na bandhabhūtā yādṛśyaḥ striyaḥ kālaviṣopamāḥ ।। nopakāraṃ smarantyetā na kuśalaṃ nāpi vikramam । anavasthitacittāśca vāyuvegasamāḥ striyaḥ ।। bhavanti sampado yatra rakṣyante yatra yoṣitaḥ ।
vyasaneṣu viraktāstu tyajanti puruṣaṃ dhruvam ।। yaṃ yaṃ gacchanti puruṣaṃ rakṣyante tatra yoṣitaḥ । śīghraṃ śīghraṃ naraṃ hyetāstyajanti puruṣaṃ sthitam ।। yathā hi bhramarī puṣpaṃ śuṣkaṃ tyajati sarvadā ।
tathā vittena rahitaṃ puruṣaṃ tyajati priyā ।। nistriṃśahṛdayāḥ krūrāścañcalāstamasāvṛtāḥ । striyaḥ puruṣanāśāya jātāḥ kenāpi hetunā ।। devānāṃ bandhanaṃ nāma yathā strībandhanaṃ matam ।
strībandhananibaddhāstu patanti narakaṃ punaḥ ।। etadagraṃ hi rāgāṇāṃ yo rāgaḥ strīsamudbhavaḥ । strīrāgadagdhamanasaṃ paścād dahati pāvakaḥ ।। pratyakṣāṇyapi karmāṇi rāgaiścāpahataḥ pumān ।
na vetti mūḍhahṛdayaḥ strīrāgeṇa vimohitaḥ ।। viśvāsya viṣaye puruṣaṃ bad dhvā priyamanekaśaḥ । tyajanti vittanāśena tvacaṃ yadvadbhujaṅgamāḥ ।। sarvopāyabhṛtā nāryaḥ sarvaśaḥ paripālitāḥ ।
na śakyāḥ svavaśīkarttuṃ striyaḥ paramadāruṇāḥ ।। āsāṃ sarvasvabhāvānāṃ nārīṇāṃ calacetasām । na yāyājjātu viśvāsaṃ pumān dhīreṇa cetasā ।। strīvidheyāstu ye martyā nityaṃ kāmagaveṣiṇaḥ ।
paścimadarśanaṃ teṣāṃ suraloke bhaviṣyati ।। pañcāṅgikena tūryeṇa vipralubdhāḥ samantataḥ । vindanti vyasane duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। imāstāścañcalā nāryo yāsāṃ rāgaḥ kṛtastvayā ।
tā bhavantaṃ parityajya punaranyaṃ tato gatāḥ ।। dvidhā hi prakṛtiryāsāṃ sahacāriṇī । bhūyo abhiyanti puruṣaṃ vyasaneṣu tyajanti ca ।। mṛgavanmohayantyetāḥ puruṣaṃ rāgamohitam ।
paścāt vyasane prāpte tyajanti laghucetasaḥ ।। nopakāraṃ na satkāraṃ na priyāṇi na santatim । smaranti yoṣitastīvrā vyasane samupasthite ।। mlānaṃ puṣpaṃ yathā tyaktvā bhramaro anyatra dhāvati ।
tathā hi vyasane prāpte tyajanti khalu yoṣitaḥ ।। anapekṣitasauhārdāścañcalāśca raṇapriyāḥ । bhavanti yoṣitaḥ sarvā viṣamiśraṃ yathā madhu ।। mohayanti narān kāmairvākyaiścāpi viśeṣataḥ ।
na teṣāṃ viśvaseddhīmān puruṣo dhīramānasaḥ ।। ābhirvimohitāḥ kiṃ vā raṃjitāḥ puruṣāḥ svataḥ । na kurvanti hitaṃ vākyaṃ yathā muṣṇikagāmikam ।। devāsuranarān yakṣān piśācoragarākṣasān ।
indrajālamayā nāryo vañcayanti viśeṣataḥ ।। etadagrañca pāśānāṃ yadidaṃ strīmayaṃ dṛḍham । anena baddhāḥ puruṣā bhramanti bhavacārake ।। na kaścit pāśapāśo ayaṃ hṛtpāśo yoṣitaḥ param ।
hṛtpāśabandhanairbaddhāḥ puruṣā duḥkhamohitāḥ ।। dahayate chidyate pāśasstrīmayastu na dahayate । narakapretatiryakṣu gacchantamanugacchati ।। mūrtimān badhyate kāyaḥ pāśena mahatā tathā ।
amūrtigaṃ cittamidaṃ strīpāśena tu badhyate ।। dṛśyate pāśamanyaṃ yena badhnanti yoṣitaḥ । abhijñeyamapramāṇaṃ strīmayaṃ bandhanaṃ mahat ।। anenāpātaramyeṇa mokṣeṇa sarvadā ।
pāśena baddhāḥ puruṣā na mucyante bhavārṇavāt ।। ṣaḍindriyāṇi badhnāti pāśo yaḥ strīmayo mahān । pāśastu kāyamevaikaṃ kaścit badhnāti vā na vā ।। bandhanaṃ na dṛḍhaṃ hīdaṃ mokṣavārya ṣaḍāyasam ।
saṃraktacittabhoge hi mandabuddhernarasya ca ।। snāyuyantreṇa baddhāsu vistṛtakarmabhūmiṣu । tīkṣṇaraktāsinā yukto maraṇārthamihāgataḥ ।। vañcanācchalakūṭāsu rabhasā nu viśeṣataḥ ।
cañcalo bhrāntacittāsu bhrāntastvaṅgakṣaṇāriṣu ।। vibhrānto bhrāntakathitairbhūṣaṇānāṃ tathā svanaiḥ । haranti puruṣaṃ kṣipraṃ vañcanākuśalāḥ striyaḥ ।। nānāvidheṣu puṣpeṣu yathā carati ṣaṭ padaḥ ।
nānāvidheṣu martyeṣu tathemāścañcalāḥ striyaḥ ।। yathā madhurikā pītvā puṣpamanyatra gacchati । tathā puruṣamāpīyaḥ prayānti rabhasaṃ striyaḥ ।। arthādāneṣu kuśalāḥ kruddhā nityaṃ durāsadāḥ ।
vañcayitvā naraṃ śīghramanyatra saṃprayānti tāḥ ।। sādhyamāyāpraharaṇāḥ kālakūṭaviṣopamāḥ । striyaḥ puruṣaghātinyaścāturyeṣu vyavasthitāḥ ।। vāyvākāśānalā yadvan na śaktā grathituṃ naraiḥ ।
tathopāyaśatairnāryo śaktā rakṣituṃ naraiḥ ।। anarthavyādhimṛtyūnāṃ duṣkṛtānāñca karmaṇām । hetubhūtāḥ paraṃ nāryo mokṣacaryābadhasya ca ।। yadanekaprakāreṣu śaṭheṣu pāpakarmasu ।
manujā loke tatra hetuḥ parastriyaḥ ।। na bālayauvanenaiva vārdhakyenaiva śāmyati । cāpalyaṃ sahajaṃ strīṇāṃ bhāskarasya yathā prabhā ।। anityaṃ sauhṛdaṃ tāsāṃ dīptānāmarciṣāṃ kaṇaiḥ ।
vairañca śāśvataṃ tāsāmaśmanāṃ ca yathā vraṇaiḥ ।। dhanahīne virajyante dhanayuktā bhavanti ca । yāvadartha striyastāvadarthahīne kutaḥ striyaḥ? ।। na sevābhiścadānena nopakāraiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ ।
svīkarttuṃ na striyaḥ śakyāḥ jvalanopamacetasaḥ ।। yathā naro anukūlaśca chandakarttā yathā yathā । tathā tathā striyastasya vañcanākuśalāḥ param ।। puṣpacchatro yathā sarpo bhasmacchatro yathā nalaḥ ।
rūpacchannaṃ tathā cittamāsāṃ bhavati yoṣitām ।। viṣavṛkṣe yathā puṣpaṃ dṛṣṭiramyaṃ na śāntaye । viṣavṛkṣa nāryaḥ parivarjyāḥ samantataḥ ।। nārīṇāṃ darśanākāṃkṣī viṣayesu ca tatparaḥ ।
naro na sukhabhogāya smilloke na cāpare ।। nāgninā na ca śastreṇa na balena na jantubhiḥ । strīmayaṃ bandhanaṃ hetuḥ śakyate na durāsadam ।। doṣajālamidaṃ strīmayaṃ carate bhuvi ।
yastrīvivarjito dhīmān asmilloke mahīyate ।। yathā bhūtairmanuṣyāṇāṃ svakarmotthāpane na ca । tathā striyo hi rakṣanti viṣamārtha tyajanti ca ।। gatārthavibhavaṃ bhūyo varjitaṃ svena karmaṇā ।
devaṃ samīkṣya capalāḥ striyo naiva prabhāvikāḥ ।। kṣaṇabhaṅgamidaṃ saukhyamadhigatamavasthitam । catvāryetāni duḥkhāni sevitāni nṛbhiḥ sadā ।। tasmāt tāni vivarjyāni viṣāgnisadṛśāni hi ।
yaḥ kaściccapalo janturyaśca doṣodbhavaḥ sadā ।। tasmāt parisamāviṣṭāḥ striyaḥ kāraṇavatsalāḥ । na sūryastamaso heturnāgniḥ śītasya kāraṇam ।। na strīṇāṃ sauhṛdaṃ citte svalpamapyavatiṣṭhate ।
yathā sthirā bhūmiriyaṃ yathā vāyuḥ sadā calaḥ ।। tathā strīṇāṃ kṛtaṃ nāsti doṣamayyaḥ sadā smṛtāḥ । ciraprayatnāḥ puruṣaiḥ lobhitā bahuśaḥ striyaḥ ।। tyajanti vyasane prāpte śuṣkaṃ sara ivāśugāḥ ।
nordhvagāḥ sarito dṛṣṭā nāśmano gatiriṣyate ।। girīṇāṃ gamanaṃ nāsti strīṇāṃ naivāsti sauhṛdam । vapukarti sadā nṛṇāṃ dharmārthayaśasāṃ tathā ।। yoniścānarthajālasya doṣāṇāmudbhavasya ca ।
bhaved vajramayī mṛdvī tyajed ravim ।। na strī tyajedasādhyāni janmāpekṣā viśeṣataḥ । nopacārakriyā dānapriyavākyāpalāpanaiḥ ।। svīkartuṃ na striyaḥ śakyā jvalanopamacetasaḥ ।
sukheṣu samatāṃ yānti vyasaneṣu tyajanti ca ।। upakārāṃśca vismṛtya doṣamekaṃ smaranti tāḥ । vanopavanaśaileṣu bhuktvā sukhamanekaśaḥ ।। saṃprāpte vyasane tīvre striya paribhavanti hi ।
lokasya bandhanaṃ nāryo vañcanākṛtivardhikāḥ ।। adhamāḥ vinipātānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ cāspadaṃ । sarvalokavināśāya vaśīkurvanti tṛṣṇayā ।। yathā strībandhanamidaṃ durviṣahyaṃ kṛtaṃ mahat ।
yadidaṃ bandhanaṃ loke kāmarāgamayaṃ mahat ।। tathā cānyaprayatnena vicārya upalabhyate । vaśīkurvanti tā kāmavāṇairanekaśaḥ ।। svalpaiḥ parājitaṃ kṛtvā kāmasya vaśagāḥ striyaḥ ।
rāgerṣyāśāṭhyabhūmīnāṃ vidyuccañcalacetasām ।। lobhāhaṅkārayonīnāṃ na viśvāsyāḥ kathañcana । śastrāgnisadṛśāstīkṣṇāḥ kāmapāśaparātmanaḥ ।। svabhraprapātaviṣamaṃ gaṃbhīrasamacetasām ।
parābhidrohamāyendrajālatadgatamānasān ।। akālamṛtyuvajrāgnikālakūṭasamātmanām । anekadoṣasambhārananditānāmanekaśaḥ ।। yadi śīlalavaḥ kaścit strīṇāṃ manasi vartate ।
cireṇa dahate vahniḥ sa spṛṣṭāḥ pavaneritaḥ ।। strīdarśanasamucchreyamātraṃ dahati pāvakaḥ । tasmāt striyo vivarjyāḥ syuḥ yadicchet sukhamuttamam ।। etat sarva paraṃ loke nārīṇāṃ varjanaṃ sadā ।
yadṛcchājālinīhetuṃ yaḥ icched bhūtimātmanaḥ ।। ya icchati nivṛttiṃ tu sa naraḥ strīṃ vivarjayet । sukhāsaktastathārtho kusīdaścañcalaḥ śaṭhaḥ ।। pāpasevī sumṛṣṭāśī naro bhadraṃ na paśyati ।
udyukto vīryavān dhīro dhārmikaḥ strīṃ vivarjayet । dakṣo hetuphalaśraddho naraḥ kalyāṇavān bhavet ।। ।। iti strījugupsāvargo navamaḥ ।। madyapānaṃ na seveta madyaṃ hi viṣamuttamam ।
naśyanti kuśalā dharmā madyapānaniṣevaṇāt ।। yaḥ sevate sadā madyaṃ tasya buddhirasaṃsthitā । balabuddhī na dharmo asti tasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet ।। nāśānāmuttamaṃ nāśaṃ madyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।
tasmānmadyaṃ na seveta nāśayate naram ।। aniṣṭāḥ pāpakā dharmā madyapānaniṣevaṇāt । bhavanti tasmād viṣavanmadyapānaṃ vivarjayet ।। dhanakṣayaṃ pāpakaraṃ kausīdyakaramuttamam ।
madyapānasthitā doṣāḥ tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।। rāgasyoddīpanaṃ madyaṃ krodhasyāpi tathaiva ca । mohasyoddīpakaṃ bhūyastasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet ।। madyamūlamanarthasya hāsasya narakasya ca ।
sarvendriyavināśānāṃ hetubhūtaṃ hyanarthakam ।। atiharṣābhidhānasya śokasya ca bhayasya ca । vāgdoṣasyātidamyasya pāruṣyasyāspadaṃ hi tat ।। madyenākṣiptamanasaḥ puruṣāḥ paśubhiḥ samāḥ ।
kāryākārya na vindanti tasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet ।। madyakṣipto hi puruṣo jīvannapi mṛto mataḥ । ya icchejjīvitaṃ saukhyaṃ sa madyaṃ varjayet sadā ।। sarvadoṣāspadaṃ madyaṃ sarvānarthakaraṃ sadā ।
sarvapāpeṣu sopānaṃ tamasāmālayo mahān ।। madyena narakaṃ yānti pretalokaṃ tathaiva ca । tiryakṣu yānti puruṣā madyadoṣeṇa vañcitāḥ ।। viṣādapi viṣaṃ madyaṃ narakānnarakaṃ tathā ।
vyādhīnāṃ ca paraṃ vyādhirmadyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।। buddhīndriyavināśāya dharmaratnaṃ kṣayāya ca । yo atirekaparaṃ madyaṃ brahmacaryabadhāya ca ।। madyena laghutāṃ yānti pārthivā śāstracakṣuṣaḥ ।
kiṃ punaḥ prākṛtā martyā madyapānavilambitāḥ ।। kuṭhāraḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ hrīvināśakaraṃ param । madyaṃ niṣevitaṃ martyairvināśāyopakalpyate ।। na jñānaṃ nāpi vijñānaṃ na kāryāṇi na ca kriyām ।
jānīte puruṣaḥ sarva madyena hṛtacetasā ।। akasmāt tapyate janturakasmāt paritapyate । bhavatyakasmāt pāpī yo madyamanusevate ।। buddhisammohajanakaṃ lokadvayavināśakam ।
vahniśca mokṣadharmāṇāṃ madyamekaṃ vyavasthitam ।। abhyāse madhuraṃ madyaṃ vipāke paramaṃ kaṭu । kimpākādapi kimpākaṃ madyamuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ ।। na madye viśvaseddhīmān naraṃ vakṣyati māmiti ।
śītasparśa vipākoṣṇaṃ madyaṃ narakagāmikam ।। sampattau vyasanaṃ madyaṃ devānāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ । yathā yathā sukhā prītistannāśe vyasanaṃ tathā ।। madyapānamadonmattāḥ sattvā mohavaśānugāḥ ।
sākṣyamohamayaṃ pānaṃ pibanti rasatṛṣṇayā ।। madyaṃ mohamayaṃ pāna pītvā kālena coditāḥ । nākāt pratyakṣanarakaṃ tasmāt madyaṃ na saṃspṛśet ।। darśanāt sparśanāt pānāta madyaṃ mohayate naram ।
tasmāt sa madyapānaṃ ca dūrataḥ parivarjayet ।। darśanājjāyate lobhaḥ sparśanād gandhasambhavaḥ । gandhād rasābhilāṣaśca rasanādadhamā matiḥ ।। naikasarvādhamaṃ nyāsaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
nāmarūpaniṣedhāya yathā madyaṃ niṣevitam ।। vāgbhrāmayati mastiṣkaṃ cakṣuṣīdhvanireva ca । sambhrāntivimatirmūḍho na kiñcit pratipadyate ।। striyo apyupahasantīmaṃ puruṣaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi ।
niśceṣṭaṃ kāṣṭhasadṛśaṃ niścalaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi ।। sambhāvitasya maraṇaṃ madyapānaṃ prakīrtyate । hālāhalādabhyadhikaṃ kārāvāsādhikaṃ ca tat ।। ādīnavāśca ṣaṭ triṃśanmadyapānādavasthitāḥ ।
tasmādādīnavo jñeyaḥ sa hi tad varjayet sadā ।। atijātasya viduṣo malinīkaraṇaṃ mahat । kāśapuṣpasamaṃ jantuṃ kurute laghusattvaram ।। pramādauhyati magnānāṃ viṣayairapahṛṣyate ।
madyapānena bhūyaśca manovyāmohakāriṇā ।। viṣayānaladagdhasya kāryākāryamajānataḥ । vanopavanalabdhasya madyapānasya kiṃ punaḥ ।। rasena śobhanaṃ madyaṃ pariṇāmena dāruṇam ।
pariṇāmaphalaṃ pāpaṃ narakeṣūpapadyate ।। pītaṃ janayate mohaṃ mohāt pāpeṣu rakṣyate । saṃraktahṛdayo bālo narakānupadhāvati ।। prakarṣa janayatyādau vipāke dainyamuttamam ।
tṛṭ chedaṃ kurute cāsau paścāddāhaṃ sudāruṇam ।। tad buddhiṃ nāśayatyādau paścānnāśayate sukham । tasmāt sa puruṣo dhīro yo madyaṃ nānusevate ।। vihagaiḥ sadṛśaṃ yānti puruṣā madyasevinaḥ ।
tulyaṃ vyāmohajanakaṃ madyaṃ mohamahāviṣam ।। yairmadyaṃ viṣavad dṛṣṭaṃ tairdṛṣṭaṃ padamuttamam । yaistu tad virasaṃ pītaṃ pītaṃ tāmra lohitam ।। niṣpratīkārakarmāṇi yaḥ karoti vimohitaḥ ।
madyapānasamāviṣṭaḥ so ante gacchati durgatim ।। ekatra sarvapāpāni madyapāna । yasmānnāśayate cittamūlaśca saṃvaraḥ ।। naikāṅgitā hi cittasya na dharmāṇāṃ vicāraṇā ।
yaḥ pā nirato bhikṣurbhavenmadyaniṣevaṇāt ।। madyenākṣiptamanaso kuśalasya ca ghātakaḥ । naṣṭadharmasya sattvasya nāyaṃ loko na cāparaḥ ।। īryyāpathaṃ na jānāti na kālaṃ nāpi deśanām ।
saddharmato viruddhaśca tucchaṃ kimapi bhāṣate ।। svayaṃ tāvanna jānāti kimidaṃ kathyate mayā । vākpāruṣyaṃ kathaṃ cānyaṃ parijñāsyatyaśobhanam ।। lāghavaṃ yāti lokasya dharmācca parihīyate ।
nidhana puruṣairdṛṣṭaṃ madyajvalanasevanāt ।। nāśo bhavatyatīte hi vartamāne suhṛjjane । anāgate kutsitānāṃ madyaṃ traikālyanāśakam ।। nāmarūpavināśāya cittanāśāya dehinām ।
utpannadoṣajanakaṃ madyaṃ dharmapradūṣakam ।। samāhitā dharmaśīlāḥ puruṣā madyavarjakāḥ । te yānti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra mṛtyurna vidyate ।। ।। iti madyajugupsāvargo daśamaḥ ।।
(cittañca vāk tathā karma saṃyojanantu pāpakam । narakapretatiryakkṣutkausīdyāni vidurdaśa ।। ) agādhaṃ viṣamaṃ tīvraṃ sarvasattvagataṃ mahat । cittaṃ sarvasya jagato rājavat sampravartate ।।
adṛśyaṃ samprati bhayaṃ karma nārakacañcalāḥ । ye cittadhāriṇastajjñāste gatāḥ paramāṃ gatim ।। etannayati vyutthānametannayati durgatim । tadevādyantamamalaṃ nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।
manaḥ pūrvamaṅgamā dharmā manaḥ śreṣṭhā manomayāḥ । manasā suprasannena bhāṣate vā karoti vā ।। yo na cittasya vaśagaścittaṃ tasyāntagaṃ sadā । sa nirṇāśayati kleśān tamaḥ sūryodayo yathā ।।
cittaṃ śatruḥ paraṃ śatrurna śatruraparaḥ smṛtaḥ । cittadagdhāḥ sadā sattvāḥ kāladagdhā yathā jaḍāḥ ।। yaścittavaśamāpanno bālo mūḍho ajitendriyaḥ । tena duḥkhe samo nāsti nirvāṇaṃ tasya dūrataḥ ।।
āvarjyaḥ śatruraparo na cittāni । eṣa badhnāti puruṣo nṛpateryamaśāsane ।। viṣayeṣu ratā nityaṃ na sa dharmaḥ kathañcana । saddharmapathasammūḍho narakaṃ nayate mahat ।।
durdamānāṃ paraṃ cittamanīnāmagniruttamaḥ । durdāntaṃ śīghragantṛ ca narakaṃ nayate dhruvam ।। ye cittasya vaśaṃ yātā yātāste narakaṃ purā । yaistu tad vāryate śīghraṃ na te duḥkhānugāminaḥ ।।
yathā yathā cittaṃ pariṇāmastathā tathā । kalpānāṃ śubhakarttuśca pāpakarttuśca pāpakam ।। cittāyattaṃ bhavet karma karmāyattaṃ mano bhavet । cittakarma samutthāya saṃsāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
duṣṭena cetasā karma yaḥ karoti pumāniha । pacyate narake tena jālinyā sa viḍambitaḥ ।। cittādhīnaṃ bhavet pāpaṃ saṃsāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ । cittapratyayajaṃ hyetat hetupratyayasambhavam ।।
cittena vañcitāḥ sattvā pāpasya vaśamāgatāḥ । gacchanti narakaṃ pāpāt kāraṇāgramahābhayā ।। na gacchet cittavaśatāṃ gacched dharmavaśe sadā । dharmacārī sukhī nityaṃ pāpacārī na śarmabhāk ।।
cittāyattā kriyā sarvā cittāyattaṃ phalaṃ smṛtam । vicittaṃ hi phalaṃ cittaṃ tathā phalamadhismṛtam ।। cittena cintitaṃ sarva lokaścittabhavānugaḥ । na hi tad vidyate sthānaṃ yanna cittavaśānugam ।।
mokṣa bandhanayormūlaṃ hetubhūtaṃ paraṃ matam । śubhena mucyate janturaśubhenāśu badhyate ।। jālinyā mohitāḥ sattvāścittasya vaśamāgatāḥ । nirvāṇaṃ nāpi gacchanti jātyandhā iva satpatham ।।
pañcendriyāṇi jitavān pāpaṃ bhuṅkte na karhicit । ekacittaṃ tathā karma kurute vividhe bhave ।। pañcaraṅgojjvalaṃ cittaṃ yathā dṛśyaṃ praśasyate । pañcendriyavicitraṃ hi tathā karma bhave bhavet ।।
cittakartā hi puruṣo dṛśyairbhavati naikadhā । cittaṃ cittakaraṃ śūnyaṃ sarvathā naiva dṛśyate ।। śobhanāśobhanaṃ citraṃ yathā bhittiḥ kṛtistathā । śobhanāśobhanaṃ karma tathā cittaṃ karoti hi ।।
divārātrau yathā cittaṃ sthitaṃ bhavati citragam । divārātrau tathā karma bhave samanuvartate ।। akṛtvā sukṛtaṃ karma cittavṛttyanugā narāḥ । patanti vivaśāḥ pāpe cittāriparivañcitāḥ ।।
karmacittakaro hyeṣa yatra yatra niyujyate । caracittena mahatā taccittaṃ ca karotyayam ।। pariṇāmaviśeṣeṇa yatra yatra niyokṣyate । preṣyante tatra cittena tridhā tu gaticāriṇaḥ ।।
cittādhināni vartante sarvakarmāṇi dehinām । tasmāccittaṃ sadā dāntaṃ nayate padamacyutam ।। durviṣahyasya laghunā yatra yatra nipātinaḥ । cittasya damanaṃ sādhu cittaṃ dāntaṃ sukhāvaham ।।
yena cittaṃ sadā dāntaṃ tena doṣāḥ sadā jitāḥ । jitadoṣasya dhīrasya duḥkhaṃ naiva prapadyate ।। yacca svakaṃ bhaved duḥkhaṃ yacca duḥkhaṃ paratra ca । tat sarvamaviṣahyasya cittasya laghuceṣṭitam ।।
sasurāsuranāgānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām । prabhurekaḥ paraṃ cittaṃ rājā tribhavasya tat ।। cittaṃ nayati deveṣu cittañca narabhūmiṣu । cittaṃ nayatyapāye cittaṃ bhrāmayati prajāḥ ।।
cittād bhrāntasya naṣṭasya viṣayairmohitasya ca । tṛṣṇayā dahyamānasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanuttamam ।। ekacāri sadāmūḍhaṃ durviṣahyaṃ mahābalam । sampradāri sadādṛśyaṃ capalaṃ śīghragāminam ।।
evaṃ vidhaṃ hi ye cittaṃ damayanti manīṣiṇaḥ । te mārabandhanātītāḥ pāraṃ prāptāḥ sukhodayam ।। saṅkalpakuṭilaṃ tīvramagādhaṃ capalaṃ hi tat । cittaṃ tamaḥśritaṃ śubhraṃ narakāyopakalpyate ।।
tadevaṃ doṣanirmuktaṃ nendriyārthavaśānugam । aliptaṃ pāpakairdharmairnayate padamacyutam ।। hetupratyayajaṃ cittaṃ yogavāhi paraṃ ca tat । pariṇāmavaśācchīghraṃ tathā tat sampravartate ।।
ekaṃ karoti karmāṇi vividhāni calaṃ ca tat । ekānekaṃ caraṃ sūkṣmaṃ kṣaṇādūrdhva na tiṣṭhati ।। durvijñeyaḥ sadā tasya niḥśarīrasya sarvadā । ko asau nayati lokāntamatha kena ca gacchati ।।
gataśca tiṣṭhati kutra śarīrakarmakārakam । dṛśyāni tasya karmāṇi sañcayo na ca dṛśyate ।। damanaṃ duṣkaraṃ tasya yasya bhūtirna vidyate । sarvasattvagataṃ ghoraṃ laghukāri ca cākṣuṣam ।।
pāpāt pāpataraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ māyopamamidaṃ bhavet । puṇyāt puṇyataraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ samyagmārgasamāśritam ।। na gatirjñāyate tasya gamanaṃ naiva dṛśyate । nīyate ca kṣataṃ sarva jātyuttarasamāni ca ।।
śastreṇa chidyate nedaṃ jvalanena ca dahayate । chidyate dahyate caiva janaḥ sarvamacakṣuṣā ।। dṛḍhaṃ yat karmarajjvādi naraṃ badhnāti duḥkhitam । jātyantarasahastrāṇi nayate na ca dṛśyate ।।
muhūrtena śubhaṃ bhūtaṃ muhūrtenāśubhaṃ ca tat । śubhāśubhābhyāṃ racitaṃ dāntaṃ sukhāvaham ।। ṣaḍ bhirdvāraiḥ prasūteṣu viṣayeṣvatilolupam । cittaṃ nayati lokāntaṃ vyasanaṃ na ca budhyate ।।
viprasannaṃ yathā toyaṃ viprasannaṃ yathā nabhaḥ । viprasannaṃ tathā cittaṃ nīyate sukhamuttamam ।। janāḥ sātiśayā vitarkaviṣayodbhavāt । pauravāścittarājñaste bhavanti sahacāriṇaḥ ।।
dhāvati yatra ca manastatra dhāvantyajñāninaḥ । parasparabalānnī bhramanti tribhavārṇa m ।। cittavaiśadya bhāvānāṃ viśeṣaḥ karmaṇāstathā । na karmaguṇahīnasya viśeṣa upalabhyate ।।
susamāhitacittaḥ sa nityaṃ dharmānudarśakaḥ । na doṣavaśamāyāti yathā divyastamonudaḥ ।। samyagdṛṣṭeścādhimātrā yasya cetasi vartate । gṛhastho api sa me jñeyo muktaḥ saṃsārabandhanāt ।।
kalyāṇanirmalaṃ yacca tato doṣeṇa bādhyate । vijño malamāpnoti devaloke sa jāyate ।। viṣayadvāracapalaṃ nadīkuṭilagāminam । yairvinītamidaṃ cittaṃ te surāḥ śubhabhāginaḥ ।।
adharmapathamāśritya janāḥ pāpavaśānugāḥ । ciraṃ bhramanti saṃsāre cittena parikheditāḥ ।। kṣaṇe kṣaṇe cittamidaṃ naikaśaḥ parivartate । laghusvabhāvacapalaṃ māyāgandharvasannibham ।।
tasya bandhanameveṣṭaṃ jñānavijñānasammatam । dūravṛttirmahāvegaḥ paridhāvatyanekadhā ।। hriyamāṇaṃ sadā cittamindriyārthe durāsadam । sandhārayati yo dhṛtyā sa dhīraḥ pāragāmikaḥ ।।
dhṛtimajñānamohaṃ ca viṣayottānamānasam । sandhārayati yo dhīmān sa loke paṇḍito naraḥ ।। yo yathā kurute cittaṃ tathā kāmān sa paśyati । śubhena kāmaśamanaṃ nāśubhena pravardhanam ।।
śāntacittaṃmanāḥ kāmānasyatīha viṣāstravat । apraśāntamatiḥ sarpamaṇivat tān sa paśyati ।। indriyāṇīndriyārthāśca cittādhīnā bhavantyamī । citta saṃśleṣayogena pariṇāmaḥ pravartate ।।
tasyaiva vyavadhānena dhīraśca pratibudhyate । rūpasāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ pariṇāmaḥ kathaṃ pṛthak ।। yathā rūpaṃ tathā sarva viṣayāścittahetavaḥ । cittaṃ dāntaṃ sadā śāntaṃ doṣamiśravigarhitam ।।
ekamekaṃ yathā śāli gandharūpe pṛthagvidhe । saṃśleṣo yāti nānātvaṃ tathācittaṃ pravartate ।। kriyāṃ hi tatra kurute yatra pradhāvati । cittasaṃvāhanaṃ tadvākyaṃ loko ayaṃ sampravartate ।।
viṣayād bhrāntamanasaś tivego mahābalaḥ । cittaṃ karaṃ dāntaṃ śivaṃ bhavati dehinām ।। tenādāntena śīghreṇa sarvapāpavihāriṇā । bhrāmyate tribhavaḥ sarvaḥ na ca tattvaṃ sa paśyati ।।
samīraṇaraṇodbhrānto yathā bhramati sāgaraḥ । citteśvarasamāyukto loko ayaṃ bhrāmyate sadā ।। śubhopanītaṃ cittaṃ śubheṣvevāpanīyate । tathā śubhānucaritamaśnute teṣu dhāvati ।।
yogavāhi nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ vāyvambusamameva ca । pratyayaśca yathā labhyastathā tat paridhāvati ।। śīghraṃ pradhāvate cittaṃ śīghrañca parivartate । śīghraṃ nayati deveśa dāyabhūmiṣu ।।
karttṛtvaṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ bharttṛtvaṃ sarvakarmaṇām । netṛtvaṃ sarvakarmāṇāṃ cittatvamiti lakṣyate ।। na viśvaseddhi cittasya nityaṃ chidraprahāriṇaḥ । durlabhasyāpi vaśyasya capalasya viśeṣataḥ ।।
muhūrtena śubhaṃ yāti muhūrtena tathāśubham । bhavatyavyākṛtaṃ śīghraṃ gatirasya na vidyate ।। nāyatirjñāyate tasya gamanaṃ naiva vidyate । abhūtaḥ sambhavastasya bhūtvā ca pratigacchati ।।
nākāro vidyate tasya sañcayo api na vidyate । grahaṇaṃ tasya naivāsti niḥśarīrasya sarvataḥ ।। hetupratyayasāmagrayā prāptaḥ sañjāyate punaḥ । maṇisomapratyayo pratyayo jñāyate analaḥ ।।
tathaivendriyarūpādīn prativijñānasambhavaḥ । naikasya jñāyate cittaṃ samavāyyanulakṣyate ।। tadevaṃ viṣayaṃ matvā durnivārya ca sarvataḥ । saddharmamatirāstheyā na kāmeṣu kathañcana ।।
caṇḍāticapalaṃ tīvramaviṣahyaṃ mahāvalam । cittaṃ karoti karmāṇi yanna paśyanti bāliśāḥ ।। sarvasya karmaṇaścittaṃ hetubhūtaṃ bhave bhave । bhavet pravartakaṃ duḥkhaṃ yena dhāvati bāliśaḥ ।।
vātādayo na doṣāḥ syurdoṣā rāgādayo matāḥ । vātādibhirapāyeṣu mānavo nopapadyate ।। cittadoṣo mahādoṣo nityaṃ vidarśakaḥ । tasmātteṣāṃ samāśreyo na vātādigamādiha ।।
vātādayaḥ praṇaśyanti dehanāśāccharīriṇām । na tasya syurjanmāntaraśatairapi ।। tasmād rāgasya vaśagaṃ na vidheyaṃ kadācana । ābhyantikaṃ paraṃ śreyaḥ prāpyate rāgasaṅkramāt ।।
yaścittavaidyaḥ sa bhiṣag na śarīrabhiṣag bhṛśam । manaścikitsako jñeyo na tathā laukiko mataḥ ।। karmacintyaṃ samaṃ cintyaṃ na cittena prapadyate । svacittakarmaṇā dagdho narakānupadhāvati ।।
yacchreyaḥ samacittasya na tat padyate । saṃrakṣyaṃ hṛdayaṃ mūḍhaḥ prayātamanudhāvati ।। dhyānād dhyeyena kūṭena yaḥ pumān vanamāśritaḥ । taṃ muktvā cittakaḥ so ayaṃ saṃprahṛṣyati bāliśaḥ ।।
ye bālāścittapāśena cittakarmavicāriṇaḥ । nīyante hyavaśā ghoraṃ narakaṃ karmamohitā ।। sucittamapi yaccitaṃ na taccittaṃ satāṃ matam । karmacittaṃ mahācittaṃ tridhātugatacitritam ।।
sattvā citrairupāyairhi bhramanti gatipañcake । tat sarva karmasācivyaṃ citrakartṛ vicitritam ।। cittacitrakareṇedaṃ karmajātaṃ vicitritam । yena sarvamidaṃ baddhaṃ jagad bhramati mohitam ।।
varṣātaparajodhūmaiścittaṃ naśyati bhūbhujaiḥ । kalpakoṭisahastreṇa citraṃ cittaṃ vinaśyati ।। nāśaṃ prayāti basudhā sāgaraścāpi śuṣyati । cittenāpi kṛtaṃ citraṃ tasyānubhavane sthite ।।
nānāgatisamāvṛttā nānākarmasamānugāḥ । nānācittavaśāḥ sattvā bhramanti gatipañcake ।। bāliśā nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ viṣayaṃ dhāvati । na cinotyaśubhaṃ karma yena dhāvati durgatim ।।
tasmāccittaṃ sadā rakṣyaṃ cañcalaṃ viṣamaṃ kharam । nityaṃ viṣayasaṃsaktaṃ tṛṣṇāviṣasamāvṛttam ।। dhāvate viṣayaṃ caitad vyasanaṃ nāvabudhyate । paścāttu vyasane prāpte phalaṃ vindati karmaṇaḥ ।।
apāyabhīrutā tasya tasya cittaṃ samāhitam । samāhitena cittena sukhāt sukhamavāpnute ।। viṣamaṃ capalaṃ tīvramaviṣahyaṃ mahābalam । yaiścittaṃ nirjitaṃ dhīraiste loke sukhino matāḥ ।।
।। iti cittavarga ekādaśaḥ ।। pāruṣyaṃ varjayet dhīmān samyagvāg bhīrato bhavet । mādhuryābhirato jarntunirvāṇasyāntike sthitaḥ ।। vācaṃ paśyan sadābhāṣenmalināṃ ca vivarjayet ।
vāṅmanenābhibhūtā ye te yānti narakaṃ narāḥ ।। ekadharmavyatītasya mṛṣāvādasya dehinaḥ । pratīrṇapratilokasya nākārya pāpamastiha ।। mṛṣāvācaṃ na bhāṣeta sarvā pratyayakārikām ।
yathā badhyati saṃsāre sugatiṃ naiva paśyati ।। sādhupratyayatenīhā sarvavidveṣakārikā । kāntāraḥ sarvādharmāṇāṃ mṛṣāvāca pravartate ।। jātamātrasya martyasya kaṭhārī jāyate mukhe ।
paścāt chinattyātmānaṃ vācā durbhāṣitaṃ vadan ।। sarvā kāryapatākā sā sarvapāpaprasūtikā । tamasāṃ yonirekā sā yāṃ vācaṃ bhāṣate mṛṣā ।। satyena hīnāḥ puruṣāḥ sarvasādhuvivarjitāḥ ।
tṛṇavad yānti loke asmin pratyapāyeṣu duḥkhitāḥ ।। na vadedanṛtaṃ dhīraḥ kaṣṭā hyanṛtavāditā । pūtigandhyasukhī cāpi paścāttāpena tapyate ।। satyaṃ ca na vivarjeta tasya dharmo na vidyate ।
vinivartitadharmasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanekajam ।। pradīpaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ sādhūnāṃ ratnavat priyam । svargasya ca paraṃ vartma satyamuktaṃ gatajvaraiḥ ।। satyaṃ na hi divaṃ yāti mokṣasyāsatyavādinaḥ ।
satyahīnā hi puruṣāḥ paśutulyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। jaghanyānāṃ jaghānyāste yeṣāṃ na vidyate । satyaṃ dharmasya sopānaṃ jyotiṣāmākaro mahān ।। panthāśca mokṣadharmāṇāṃ dhanānāṃ dhanamuttamam ।
pāpakaiśca trāṇāṃ satyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।। jyotiṣāṃ paramaṃ jyotiścakṣuścakṣuṣmatāmapi । draviṇena vinā satyaṃ bhūṣaṇasyāpi bhūṣaṇam ।। nidhānamatulaṃ satyamahārya ।
gacchanti puruṣāḥ paramāṃ gatim ।। na tathā bhāsate rājā nānālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ । satyena bhūṣito dhīmān śobhate devavad yathā ।। na mātā na pitā cātha mitrāṇi na ca bāndhavāḥ ।
trāṇamevaṃ yathā śrutvā tasmāt satyaparo bhavet ।। vahnīnāṃ paramo vahnirviṣāṇāṃ paramaṃ viṣam । durgatīnāṃ ca sopānamanṛtaṃ parikīrtitam ।। viṣāgnitulyasaṃsparśa vartayedanṛtaṃ pumān ।
anṛtena hi yo deva dagdhaityabhidhīyate ।। tasmāt sarvābhisāreṇa nṛtaṃ pumān । sarva bhayādikaṃ kaṣṭamanṛtaṃ kīrtitaṃ budhaiḥ ।। vahnīnāṃ paramo vahnirnirdahedapi sāgaram ।
kiṃ punaryo mṛṣāvādī kāṣṭhaloṣṭhasamākṛtiḥ ।। satyaṃ tyaktvā mṛṣāvādaṃ yo naraḥ pratipadyate । ratnaṃ tyaktvā sa pāpātmā pāṣāṇaṃ pratipadyate ।। yasyātmā na bhavet dviṣṭo yasya vā narakaṃ priyam ।
mṛṣāvādaṃ svadehāgnim abuddhiḥ sa niṣevate ।। sadedaṃ satyavacanaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ sarvadehinām । satyaṃ tyaktvā mṛṣāvāde kasmād yānti kubuddhayaḥ ।। satyaṃ guṇānāmagryaṃ vai doṣāṇāmanṛtaṃ smṛtam ।
guṇāṃstyaktvā kathaṃ mūḍho doṣeṣu paridhāvati ।। bījaṃ sarvasya duḥkhasya mṛṣāvādaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । tathā satyaṃ sukhasyaiva tasmānnānṛtako bhavet ।। satyavādī hi puruṣaḥ priyaḥ sarvasya dehinaḥ ।
cakṣurdoṣaimṛṣāvādī tasmānnānṛtako bhavet ।। devakalpāḥ sadā kṛṣṭāḥ puruṣāḥ satyavādinaḥ । nārakeyāstathā mūḍhā janā hyanṛtacetasaḥ ।। kalyāṇānāṃ paraṃ satyaṃ doṣāṇāmanṛtaṃ tathā ।
doṣavarjī guṇadveṣī puruṣaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।। sukhodayaṃ sukhodarkaṃ sukhena paripacyate । sukhena labhate satyaṃ nirvāṇagāmikam ।। duḥkhodayaṃ kaṭuphalaṃ duḥkhena saha pacyate ।
anṛtaṃ sarvaduḥkhāntaṃ kaḥ pumān na vivarjayet ।। nānyadeśāgataṃ satyaṃ nānyasmāt prārthyate hi tat । sarvatīrthottamaṃ satyaṃ na tīrthasalilāvṛtam ।। dīpānāṃ ca paro dīpaḥ satyaṃ buddhena deśitam ।
auṣadhānāṃ paraṃ tacca sadā duḥkhaniṣūdanam ।। amṛtañca viṣañcaiva jihvāpāśe sthitaṃ nṛṇām । amṛtaṃ satyamityuktaṃ viṣaṃ tūktaṃ mṛṣāvacaḥ ।। yasyānṛtamabhipretaṃ tasya satyaṃ dhruvaṃ sthitam ।
viṣantu yasyābhimataṃ tasyeṣṭaṃ syānmṛṣāvacaḥ ।। viṣeṇa niścitaṃ nāśo mṛṣāvādena niścitaḥ । mṛtavat sa pumānasti yo mithyātvabhibhāṣate ।। nātmano hi hitaṃ pathyaṃ sya na kathañcana ।
paścāttu paraduḥkhāya tat kathaṃ sevyate nṛbhiḥ ।। deśe deśe mayā dṛṣṭaṃ janmamṛtyusahasrakam । paraḥ sahastraṃ janayennāśayedanṛtaṃ vacaḥ ।। abhijātasa niṣkarṣo dvijātīnāṃ ca bhūṣaṇam ।
darśanaṃ mokṣamārgasya satyamityabhidhīyate ।। tṛṣṇānadī hayamārāṇāṃ satāṃ satyena karmaṇām । pūrvavat satyamityuktaṃ paraṃ sugatadeśikam ।। anādinidhane loke tṛṣṇāpāraṅgatā ।
nāstyatrāṇaṃ yathā satyamiti dharmavido viduḥ ।। satyavadhyā sadā kleśā vajravadhyā yathā nagāḥ । hatā puruṣā bhidhyā parivañcitāḥ ।। paracittasamenedaṃ rūpādyaiḥ parivañcyate ।
abhidhyāmānasaṃ pāśaṃ sevitaṃ na vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। dahyate avikṛta ātmā tailadīptirivānalaḥ । abhidhyādagdhamanasaḥ kāraṇaṃ nopalabhyate ।। yasmāt tat sarvadā varjyaṃ kaṭukāśāviṣodayam ।
vyāpādamohitāḥ sattvā nityaṃ tadgatamānasāḥ ।। na śāntimadhigacchanti sarpā iva bileśayāḥ । atha kūrasvabhāvā ye vyāpādaparamā narāḥ ।। na teṣāṃ vidyate saukhyamādityena yathā tamaḥ ।
na dharme nārthanikaro na dharmā na ca bāndhavāḥ ।। rakṣanti puruṣān sarvān vyāpādāhatacetasaḥ । tamasāmākaro hyeṣa vyāpāda iha kathyate ।। vyāpādayati janakaṃ vyāpādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।
avyāpādaḥ paraṃ śreyo na vyāpādaḥ kathañcana ।। avyāpādaparā ye tu te yānti padamacyutam । niyatātathavādī yo adharmavādī na dhārmikaḥ ।। sa cauraḥ sarvalokasya na cauraḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
dharmavādī naro yastu carate dharmameva yaḥ ।। sa yāti śāśvataṃ sthānaṃ yatra gatvā na śocyate । mithyāvacohata laukikaḥ samprakīrtyate ।। lokottaraiḥ kalpaśataiḥ kadācit kathyate na vā ।
tasmāt lokottaraṃ vākyaṃ laukikaṃ na kathañcana ।। saṃsārabandhanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ laukikaṃ viṣavad vacaḥ । tṛṣṇārataḥ sadā puṇyānmucyateti suniścitam ।। lokottaro dhanyo vidvadbhiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।
hitaṃ tattvaṃ ca yo mūḍho na gṛhṇāti gurorvacaḥ ।। sa paścād vyasane prāpte tapyate svena cetasā । satyavādī sadā dānto devatābhiḥ puraskṛtaḥ ।। priyo bhavati lokasya paścād deveṣu modati ।
priyo bhavati lokasya paścād svāntena । darśanīyaṃ mukhaṃ cāsya devalokeṣu jāyate ।। abhūtavādī puruṣaḥ sarvasattvopapātakaḥ । tamonicayasaṅkāśo jīvannapi mṛtaḥ samaḥ ।।
kathaṃ na jihvā patitā vākyasaṃstutikattṛkā । mṛṣā vadati yo vācaṃ sadbhūtaguṇanāśikām ।। mukhe sannihito byālo mukhe sannihito aphalaḥ । sañjvalito vahniryo vācā bhāṣate mṛṣā ।।
jihvā saṅgrathitaiḥ pāśaiḥ narakasyāgrahetukaiḥ । chettā ca dharmahetūnāṃ mṛṣāvādaḥ pravartate ।। na tasya mātā na pitā buddho nāpi samvaraḥ । yaḥ pāpabuddhiḥ patito mṛṣāvādaṃ prabhāṣateḥ ।।
akasmāllaghutāṃ yāti ṣaḍbhiśca parivartate । mucyate devatābhiśca yo vācaṃ bhāṣate mṛṣā ।। asaṅgṛhītavākyasyāvicārya krodhanasya ca । capalasyālpabhāgyasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanantakam ।।
parasya duḥkhaṃ dṛṣṭvāpi sattvaḥ sattvopapātakaḥ । paravyasanavat tajjñaḥ pumān narakagāmikaḥ ।। ye yathāvādino marttyā na ca tatkāriṇaḥ sadā ।। satyaṃ svargasya sopānaṃ nirvāṇadvārameva tat ।
tasmāt satyaparo nityaṃ nityaṃ dharmagatiḥ smṛtiḥ ।। aśokamajaraṃ sthānaṃ prayāti puruṣottamaḥ । varjayedanṛtaṃ dhīmān ninditaṃ tattvadarśibhiḥ ।। ।। iti vāgvargo dvādaśaḥ ।।
śubhānāmaśubhānāṃ ca karmaṇāṃ phalaniścayaḥ । bhujyate sukṛtaṃ sarva karmabaddhā hi dehinaḥ ।। kriyate karma tatkṛdbhiranubhūyate । cittamānena mūḍhena tṛṣṇānagaravāsinā ।।
sahāyairbahubhiḥ sārdha kurute karma duṣkṛtam । ekākī karmaṇastasya phalaṃ bhuṅkte bhave bhave ।। karmaṇāmavisaṃyogaḥ sarvaiḥ svajanabāndhavaiḥ । śubhāśubhaṃ paraṃ loke gacchantamanugacchati ।।
yatra prayānti puṇyāni gandhastatrānudhāvati । tathā śubhāśubhaṃ karma gacchantamanugacchati । svakarmaphaladāyādā prāṇena karmayojinaḥ ।। sukṛtaiḥ suralokeṣu duṣkṛtaiśca tathāpyadhaḥ ।
yadduḥkhaṃ karmaphalajaṃ jāyate kaṭukodayam ।। tasyopamānamasuraṃ triṣu dhātuṣu jāyate । tridoṣajaṃ tricittotthaṃ triṣu dhātuṣu pacyate ।। tasya karmavipākasya triṣu dhātuṣu lakṣyate ।
hetupratyayasāmagrīsamutthaṃ ca prameva tat ।। na hyanyena kṛtaṃ pāpamanyena paripacyate । sukarmaphaladāyādaḥ prāṇināṃ sarva eva hi ।। karmaṇastrividhasyāsya na cāpyanyasya pacyate ।
catvāriṃśadvipākasya ghoraṃ bhavati ceṣṭitam ।। ekaḥ karoti karmāṇi ekaśca phalamaśnute । ekastarati durgāṇi sahāyo jāyate aparaḥ ।। jalāpekṣī jano yastu kurute karma duṣkṛtam ।
na jano janaśatānāṃ bhuṅkte hi vyañjanaṃ ।। na hyanyena kṛtaṃ karma saṅkrāmatyaparasya tat । na manye anādinidhanamasmiṃlloke na cāparaiḥ ।। duḥkhāsvādaṃ sukhodbhūtaṃ yena duścaritaṃ kṛtam ।
tena carati saṃsāre prerite karmavāyunā ।। anapekṣitatattvasya vyākulīkṛtacetasaḥ । vardhate sakalo dharmāvṛtamanoharaḥ ।। manasā vañcitāḥ sattvā manasā vipramohitāḥ ।
gacchanti narakaṃ pāpāstamastamaparāyaṇāḥ ।। tamovṛte hi saṃsāre durlabhaṃ buddhaśāsanam । duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ yānti yebhyaḥ dharmo na rocate ।। anādimati saṃsāre karmajālāvṛtā prajā ।
jāyate bhriyate cai svakarmaphalahetunā ।। jāyante narake devā nārakeyāstathāvidhāḥ । manuṣyāḥ pretaviṣaye narakaṃ vā prayānti hi ।। anyonyaprabhavaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā yadi vā sukham ।
kleśadharmodbhave janmanyaparādikṛtaṃ ca tat ।। asaṅkhyeyakṛtaṃ karma saṃsāre prāṇibhiḥ sadā । tatra śakyaṃ budhairgantuṃ varjayitvā tathāgataiḥ ।। nādharmasya phalaṃ sādhu viparītaṃ na pacyate ।
hetoḥ sadṛśatā dṛṣṭā jalasya vividhasya vai ।। sādṛśyasya hetuphalaṃ viparītaṃ na jātu hi । saṃskṛtānāmarūpāṇāṃ hetuḥ pratyayasambhavaḥ ।। nāhetukaṃ phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ narake tu viśeṣataḥ ।
hetusaṅghātasaṃsaktaṃ narakeṣu vipacyate ।। kṛtoparatagāḍhānāṃ niyataṃ pāpagāminām । karmaṇā phalasambandho narakeṣu vipacyate ।। deśānāṃ prati kālaṃ tu yat karma nivartate ।
tasya neṣṭaṃ phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tattvamārgavidarśakaiḥ ।। dīpādhīnā prabhā yadvat karmādhīnaṃ phalaṃ tathā । anyo anyaphalasambhūtaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ sarva eva hi ।। anyonyahetukā dṛṣṭā hyanyonyavaśavartinaḥ ।
sādṛśyasyānubandhena dṛśyante tattvadarśakaiḥ ।। nāhetuphalasandhānamīśvarādibhirāsthitam । bhavanti saṃskṛtā dharmā deśitāstattvadarśibhiḥ ।। anādimatisaṃsāre hetupratyayasambhave ।
sādṛśyaṃ karmaṇā dṛṣṭaṃ viparītaṃ na kalpyate ।। tatstheṣu karmavaśagāḥ prāṇinaḥ karmahetujāḥ । sa karmaphalatattvajño ityabhidhīyate ।। mārgāmārgaviruddhā ye mūḍhā buddhasya śāsane ।
teṣāṃ vidyate śāntirādityasya tamo yathā ।। karmāyattaṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sukhāyattaṃ manastathā । mano avaboddhayā dharmā ye vyutpattivicāriṇaḥ ।। anityāḥ sarvasaṃskārā jalabud budasannibhāḥ ।
tasmāt sucaritaṃ karma loke martya paratra ca ।। dṛṣṭaṃ karmaphalaṃ loke dṛṣṭā eva vicitratā । yaḥ pramādaparaḥ puṃsāstasyātmā dhruvamapriyaḥ ।। karmarajjvātidṛḍhayā duṣpramokṣasugāḍhayā ।
baddhā bālā na gacchanti nirvāṇapuramuttamam ।। ।। iti karmavargastrayodaśaḥ ।। jñānaśastre tāṃ chitvā nirmuktā vigatajvarā । prayānti nirvṛttiṃ dhanyā yatra jñānyeva vidyate ।।
sadṛśaṃ hi phalaṃ hetoḥ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ । hetorasadṛśaṃ naiva phalaṃ pacati dehinām ।। hetupratyayasambaddhajanmapratyayasaṅgatāḥ । yathā baddhā hi saṃsāre pramucyante dehinaḥ ।।
tāṃ viśliṣya susambaddhāṃ gāḍhāṃ durviṣehāṃ parām । gacchanti paramāṃ śānti yatra duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।। karmaṇā niyataṃ jantuḥ karmaṇā paripacyate । sūpagaṃ saṃsāre sukhaṃ naivopalabhyate ।।
duḥkhe duḥkhābhiṣaktānāṃ jantūnāṃ mūḍhacetasām । sanmārgadeśiko nāsti yo asmād duḥkhāt pramocayet ।। ye na dharmaparā nityaṃ ye na satyaparāḥ sadā । ye ca yoniratā nityaṃ teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na hīyate ।।
mātṛvat pitṛvaccaiva bandhuvat sadā । dharmo vai deśito buddhairiha loke paratra ca ।। trigatyavasthitāḥ sattvāstridoṣavaśamāgatāḥ । tridhātugatikā nityaṃ trilokyāṃ patitāḥ ।।
trikarmopāntavaśagāḥ strīpānādiparāśca ye । na bhavānmuktigatikāḥ syurbhūmau vicaranti te ।। triratne pramādyanti tribodhivaśagāśca ye । tridṛṣṭivarjakā ye tu teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।।
trikālasthitisaṃlagnā vijvarāstattvadarśinaḥ । tribhāgakṛtisantuṣṭā vītaśokā nivṛttigāḥ ।। trirāśisamavetā ye trikarmapravicāriṇaḥ । na te vatsyanti saṃsāre vītadoṣā gatajvarāḥ ।।
mārgāmārgavidhijñā ye bhāvābhāvavicintakāḥ । maitrībhāvaviviktā ye te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।। anāvilena viprasannena । sarvadā dharmavaśagān dhīrān viprān bhajennaraḥ ।।
satyameva prapannā ye smṛtyā manomalam । bhāvābhilāṣād viratā muktā niḥsaṃśayaṃ hi te ।। nityaṃ duḥkhasukhairbaddhā vipralabdhā hyanekaśaḥ । narā nidhanatāṃ yānti prāṇino mohavañcitāḥ ।।
nāhrīkyamanapatrāpyaṃ kausīdyaṃ pāpamitratā । naitāni nākabījāni tebhyo rajyenna paṇḍitaḥ ।। āhrīkyamanapatrāpyaṃ nityaṃ pāpānucāriṇaḥ । naraḥ prapātāt patati sa paścāt pratibudhyate ।।
krodherṣyāstyānamiddhaṃ hi tvaśraddhaṃ yanmanastathā । mohaśokabhayagrastā na svarga prabhavanti te ।। amṛtaṃ madyapānaṃ ca mithyādṛṣṭiśca lubdhatā । kāraṇāni karaṇasya vyāpādakrūrakarmatā ।।
adarśanaṃ paraṃ śreyo na kudṛṣṭiḥ kathañcana । kudarśanena saṃmūḍhāḥ prayānti narakaṃ narāḥ ।। ahetuṃ hetumāpaśyantya nityavannarāḥ । prayānti narakaṃ tīvraṃ mithyāvādena vañcitāḥ ।।
kaṣṭena tejasā teṣāṃ mithyādarśanatatparāḥ । prajñābhimānino bhūtā mohayantyaparān janān ।। mohāndhakāragahane patantyeva mahārṇave । loke prakṛtiduḥkhe asmin hetubhūtā hi te janāḥ ।।
śarāṇāṃ tāpanaṃ kṣepaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ । cittatā yā tudatyante sarvataḥ kleśaparvataḥ ।। kleśanāgād vimokṣo yo yasya jñānapuraḥ saraḥ । prāpyate vītakai rūpaiḥ puruṣaistattvadarśibhiḥ ।।
anyo anyamatibhiḥ sarvā loko ayaṃ vipralobhitaḥ । na yāti paramāṃ śāntiṃ yatra mithyā na kathyate ।। auddhatyapāpasaṃsargaḥ kausīdyaṃ lubdhatā tathā । hetavo narakasyaite śīlasya hi vivarjanam ।।
madyapānaṃ sadā hiṃsā paradārābhidarśanam । lobhaḥ kūrā matiścaiva hetavo narakasya te ।। paiśunyaṃ pāpasaṃsargo mithyādṛṣṭirasaṃyamaḥ । cāpalyaṃ manasaścaiva nāśayanti naraṃ sadā ।।
avidyayā saha pāruṣyaiḥ mithyāvāgabhimānitā । na sukhāya bhavantyete asmiṃlloke na cāpare ।। yadyasau bhramati prāyo lokesmin kinna cāpare । yadyasambhrāmite loke ye ca duḥkhe nimajjati ।।
tacceṣṭitamavidyāyāḥ kathayanti tathāgatāḥ । mithyāmāno atimānī ca sarvathā । parivarjyāḥ sadā hyete duḥkhavṛkṣasya hetavaḥ ।। jñāninaḥ paramodārā nityaṃ kleśavadhe ratāḥ ।
chitvā bandhanaṃ sarva gacchanti padamacyutam । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇamasmiṃlloke na cāpare ।। doṣāṇāṃ sevanaṃ dṛṣṭamavidyāsampravartakam । varjanīyāḥ sadā kleśāḥ sevyaṃ jñānamanuttamam ।।
jñānena muktirbhavati na ca kleśairihocyate । jñānāgninā hi dahayante kleśakāṣṭhā na śeṣataḥ ।। kleśaiḥ kimartha saṃruddhā jālinī viṣa ratā । punaḥ kāmamayaṃ jñānaṃ cakṣuḥpaṭalabādhakam ।।
nirvāṇayati sambuddhavākyabhaiṣajyabhojanaiḥ । saddharmasenāpatinā rāgasenā vigarhitāḥ ।। udīritā śubhā vāṇī niścetavyā prayatnataḥ । catvāro hi viparyāsā budbudavaccakāsate ।
lokadharmāstathā cāṣṭau nāśayantyakhilaṃ jagat ।। jālinīprabhavā nadyo vitarkaśatadustarāḥ । jñānaplavaṃ samāruhya taranti munayaḥ śivāḥ ।। mūḍhā ye bhūtamanaso narāḥ kāmasya sevinaḥ ।
sadā ca pañcabhiḥ sthānairmuktisteṣāṃ na vidyate ।। ayoniśomanaskārairyo vahniḥ samudīryate । sa yoniśomanaskāravarṣaṇaiḥ pratikalpate ।। andhatvaṃ cirakālotthamavidyāsambhavaṃ nṛṇām ।
tadalpakāle jātena pradīpena na paśyati ।। rāgamūḍhā vipacyante narake mandamedhasaḥ । jñāninastu na naśyanti nirvāṇagamanā yathā । trayo do vinaśyanti jñānalokena dehinām ।।
tasmādaśeṣavijñānaśīlakṣāntirato bhavet । amūḍhānāṃ praṇaśyanti trayo doṣāḥ śarīriṇām ।। jñānānalena mandaśca kleśendhana mahāttviṣaḥ । vyādhinirmagnatanavaḥ śayyāveṣṭanagocarāḥ ।।
yatra yāti paraṃ vedaṃ manomohamayaṃ phalam । yāni duḥkhānyanekānyanekā bhujyate gatiḥ ।। pañcakaiḥ prāṇibhinityametanmohasya ceṣṭitam । trayo vā nirjitā doṣā yairidaṃ dahyate jagat ।।
tamagniṃ jñānayogena nirvāpya sukhito bhavet । tasmājjñānāgninā nityaṃ nirdahet kleśaparvatam । kleśaparvatadagdhasya sukhaṃ padamavasthitam ।। ।। iti saṃyojanavargaścaturdaśaḥ ।।
kriyamāṇasya pāpasya vijñeyaṃ kaṭukaṃ phalam । yo na jānāti mūḍhātmā paścāt sa paritapyate ।। labhate puruṣaḥ sarvapāpasya karmaṇaḥ । tasmāt pāpaṃ na seveta yadīcchet sukhamātmanaḥ ।।
alpādapi mahāghorāt narakāt pāpacetasaḥ । muktyartha pāpāni bhūyo mohavaśaṃ gatāḥ ।। na viśvaseddhi pāpasyā narakagāmikām । alpena vahninā śaile dahayante sarvato drumāḥ ।।
pāpena narakaṃ yāti pāpena paridahyate । pāpena naiti nirvāṇaṃ nāsti pāpasamo ripuḥ ।। pāpācāro hi puruṣo na kvacit sukhamedhate । tasmānna seveta yadīcchet sukhamātmanaḥ ।।
sādhukāraṃ ca sādhūnāṃ pāpamārgasya duṣkaram । kurvantaḥ pāpakān sattvā modante ।। vipākakaṭukaḥ paścāt paritāpo alpacetasaḥ । kuto apacitagātrasya karmaṇo dṛśyate phalam ।।
tasmāt pāpaṃ na kurvīta kaṣṭā pāpasya vedanā । pāpaṃ pāpavipākaṃ ca pāpināṃ pacyate dhruvam ।। na hi pāpaṃ na pāpasya tasmāt pāpaṃ vivarjayet । parivarjitapāpasya na pāpād bhayamasti hi ।।
svakṛtaṃ bādhate pāpaṃ parīkṣyaṃ naiva bhujyate । kalyāṇasya phalaṃ sādhu kaṣṭaṃ pāpasya pacyate ।। kṛtvā tu puruṣaḥ pāpaṃ kalyāṇaṃ nānusevate । na śastrāgniprapātebhyo duḥkhaṃ syāt tādṛśaṃ nṛṇām ।।
yathā niṣevitaṃ mithyāpāpaṃ pāpeṣu kalpyate । vinivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ ca śubhacetasaḥ ।। śāntavaktrasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ । tīvrāt tīvrataraṃ yānti narāḥ kukṛtakāriṇaḥ ।।
sukhāt sukhataraṃ yānti narāḥ sukṛtakāriṇaḥ । na hi tīvrasya pāpasya sukhaṃ phalamavāpyate ।। sukhasya vā phala tīvraṃ viparītaṃ na pacyate । anādimati saṃsāre sukṛtānāṃ phalaṃ sukham ।।
karmaṇāṃ sukṛtānāṃ ca tathā duḥkhaphalaṃ smṛtam । pāpaṃ pāpānugaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śubhasya ca śubhaṃ tathā ।। pāpācāraḥ śubhadveṣī narakeṣūpapadyate । parivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ ca śubhacetasaḥ ।।
hastāvalambi nirvāṇamadṛṣṭaṃ tadanāvilam । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇā dharmā nityaṃ sukhodayāḥ ।। ādimadhyāntakaṭukaṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ । tasmāt pāpaṃ sadā varjyamālambyañca śubhaṃ sadā ।।
parivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ sukhamavasthitam । anādimati saṃsāre dagdhāḥ pāpaiḥ punarnarāḥ । khedaṃ kasmānna gacchanti bālā mohavaśānugāḥ ।। āpātamadhuraṃ pāpaṃ pariṇāme agnisannibham ।
pāpakārī tu puruṣaḥ sarvaloke vigarhitaḥ । śubhakārī sadā śāntastasmāt pāpaṃ vivarjayet ।। aniṣṭamahitaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vipāke kaṭuvedanam । pāpaṃ pāpavipākaṃ ca tasmād dhīmān vivarjayet ।।
asti pāpaṃ dhruvaṃ pāpe pāpamasti na pātakam । pāpāceṣṭā kṣayāpekṣā kṛpā cittasugāmitā ।। pāpaṃ pāpāśritaṃ nityaṃ dharmo dharmāśritastathā । unnayatyuktametaddhi dhīraistattvanidarśakaiḥ ।।
acetanā dhruvaṃ bālā yeṣāṃ duścaritaṃ priyam । vinivarjitapāpāstu gacchanti paramāṃ gatim ।। atīva vañcanāghorā niyatā pāpagāminī । mānuṣyaṃ durlabhaṃ prāpya yasya pāpaṃ priyaṃ bahu ।।
pāpād virajyate yastu śubhe vātīva rajyate । sa sukhāt sukhamāpnoti nivṛttiṃ vā prayāti hi ।। naro bhavati dhanyo ayaṃ yaḥ śubhānyupasevate । sa tvadhanyatamo loke yaḥ pāpamupasevate ।।
ādimadhyāntanidhanaṃ sadbhireva vigarhitam । pāpaṃ pāpānugaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ narakāyopakalpyate ।। atīva śobhate loke śubhakarmā jitendriyaḥ । kāyasya bhedāt satataṃ devaloke sa jāyate ।।
sukṛtasya tathā dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ sukhavipākajam । bījasyāśuvibhītasya pariṇāmaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।। nimittaṃ sadṛśaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ । pāpenākṛṣyate jantuḥ durgatau baḍiśairiva ।।
baḍiśairmucyate mīnaḥ pāpaṃ pāpānna mucyate । dina pīḍāpi pāpasya sarvathā duḥkhakārikā ।। amedhyasya yathā gandhaḥ pratikūlo hi dehinām । śubhasya vāsanā ramyā vipraṇaṣṭasya durgatau ।।
vileṣu vāsanaṃ yadvat puṣpe naṣṭe pradṛśyate । calatyayaṃ pāpakārī nityaṃ kāmavaśānugaḥ ।। ālasyānṛtiko nityaṃ nāsau kalyāṇamarhati । anantā rajanī teṣāṃ pāpe sthitaṃ manaḥ ।।
prabhātaṃ rajanī teṣāṃ yeṣāṃ pāpe sthirā matiḥ । anīrṣyakāḥ sakalyāṇāḥ puruṣāḥ śubhacāriṇaḥ ।। ye na pāpātmano bhūtāste nityaṃ koṭacāriṇaḥ । alpabhārā yathā nāvā plavate na nimajjati ।।
tathālpapāpapuruṣaḥ plavate na nimajjati । na pāpamitrasaṃsargāt puruṣaḥ sukhavān bhavet ।। pāpamitraṃ samāsādya sarvānalaparo bhavet । karmārambha vidhijño yo nityaṃ sūkṣmārtha ।।
nāsau limpati pāpena paṅkena gaganaṃ yathā । aśrutaṃ puruṣaḥ śṛṇvan śrutañcāpi bhaved dṛḍham ।। pāpaṃ ca varjayed dhīmān pretya deveṣu jāyate । guṇadoṣaparijñānammetat paṇḍitalakṣaṇam ।।
guṇadoṣāparijñānametanmūḍhasya lakṣaṇam । guṇeṣu guṇasañcāro doṣeṣu ca tathaiva ca ।। sadoṣaguṇatattvajño nityaṃ bhavati śokabhāk । pāpakarttā puruṣaḥ śatruvaccātmanaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
śubhakarttā tathā puṃso mitravat pratipadyate । tamonirayabhūmiṣvamṛto ayaṃ pratipadyate ।। yasya pāparatā buddhirnityaṃ viṣayatatparā । viṣayārāmacapalā nityaṃ rāgānucāriṇī ।।
yasya buddhirna dharmeṣu narasya duḥkhabhāginaḥ । hetutaśca mahāduḥkhāntahetorvahnisaṃyutāt ।। kṣīṇapāpā vayaṃ sarve bhūyo lokamihāgatāḥ । sukṛtasya phalaṃ sādhu hyanekaguṇamaṇḍitam ।।
duṣkṛtasya phalaṃ duḥkhaṃ visaṃvādakamiṣyate । te vayaṃ sukhaduḥkhābhyāṃ bhūyāma bhavasaṅkaṭe ।। karmavāyusamudbhrāntāḥ samudrasya yathormayaḥ । kṛtaṃ pāpeṣvamanasaḥ pāpaiḥ rakṣanti ye janāḥ ।।
te tasya hetornarakaṃ prayāntyaśubhacāriṇaḥ । tasmāttu narakānmuktāḥ te gacchanti triviṣṭapam ।। te hi duḥkhaṃ saṃsmṛtya punaḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ । kharībhūtamidaṃ cittaṃ dolādolaiḥ sukhāsukhaiḥ ।।
viyogo ayaṃ parīghāto na ca duḥkhairna vidyate । apāradārasaṃyukta indriyaiḥ parivañcitaḥ ।। jano bhramati saṃsāre tṛṣṇāpāśavaśānugaḥ । narakāt pretabhuvanaṃ tiryagyoniṣu pretataḥ ।।
tiryagbhyo nākabhuvanaṃ nākād bhūyo nṛjātiṣu । ekakarmaparibhrānto jagad bhramati cakravat ।। na ca khedavaśaṃ yānti vaśamāgatāḥ । rakṣanti nākabhuvanaṃ virajyante tathā sukhaiḥ ।।
sukhāt sukhaparibhrāntā bhramanti bhramacāriṇaḥ । duḥkhaṃ padmasahasrāṇi padmakoṭiśatāni ca ।। duḥkhāni bhuṅktāni na ca kliśyanti bāliśāḥ । na sukhaṃ vidyate loke sarvaduḥkhaiḥ pariplutam ।।
udvegaṃ naiva gacchanti prāṇino mohapīḍitāḥ । duḥkhena khidyate bālo duḥkhahetau ca vartate ।। hetau śataphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ bījaṃ prati yathā phalaiḥ । sukhaduḥkhakaśābaddhāḥ prāṇinastribhavānugāḥ ।।
na yānti paramaṃ kṣemaṃ sarvaduḥkhavivarjitam । smaryate yadā duḥkhaṃ tadā vidhyati dehinam ।। vismṛte ca punarduḥkhe caranti vigatajvarāḥ । nārakaṃ tu sadā duḥkhaṃ smṛtaṃ bhavati dehibhiḥ ।।
tadā kṛṣṇamidaṃ saukhyamanumānena tiṣṭhati । tadeva viditaṃ matvā jagat sarva samanvitam ।। śreyasi kriyatāṃ buddhirdoṣebhyo vinivāryate । kṣaṇādhikāracapalaṃ jīvitaṃ veti vartate ।।
kṣīyante cāpi karmāṇi tasmācchreyaḥparo bhavet । cittavegaṃ manaḥ sarva jīvitaṃ veti vartate ।। tasmānna jīvikāhetau pāpaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ । anāgatasya duḥkhasya na vibheti mahājanaḥ ।।
yenā pacyate pāpaṃ mohapāpavaśaṅgatam । mohitaḥ pāpakairdhamairaśubhaiḥ śuklavarjitaiḥ ।। nīyate narakaṃ mūḍho yatra pāpaṃ vipacyate । yasya pāpād bhayaṃ nāsti sa pāpaṃ kurute bahu ।।
sa pāpānantasandagdhaḥ paścānnarakamāpnute । sūkṣmāgnikaṇikā yathā dāhāya kalpate ।। anyairapi tathā pāpairnarakaṃ yāntyabuddhayaḥ । apāpabhīrutā tasmāt kartavyā sukhamicchatā ।।
hiṃsā mithyāvaco abrahmacarya bhūyaḥ sukhodayam । āhrīkyamanapatrāpyamauddhatyaṃ pāpamitratā ।। viṣāgnisadṛśā hayete tebhyo rakṣet prayatnataḥ । duḥkhaṃ hi māradharmo ayaṃ sukhaṃ dharmasamantataḥ ।।
lakṣaṇaṃ duḥkhānāṃ vidustattvavido janāḥ । satyaṃ dānaṃ tathā kṣāntiḥ sadā cāpāpamitratā । maitrī sadābhibhūteṣu prasthānaṃ tridivasya ।। ।। iti pāpavargaḥ pañcadaśaḥ ।।
kṛtvā duṣkṛtakarmāṇi sattvā viṣamajīvinaḥ । yā gatiḥ pretya gacchantī tānapāyān śṛṇu ।। sañjīvaṃ kāmasūtraṃ ca sampātaṃ dvau ca rauravau । tamoparaṃ mahācitrapatanaṃ ca pratāpanam ।।
ityete narakā aṣṭāvākhyātā duratikramāḥ । raudrakarmābhisaṅkīrṇāḥ pratyekaṃ kṣobhadā ।। catuḥskandhāścaturdvārā vibhaktā bhāgaśo mitāḥ । ayaḥ prākāraparyantā ayasā pratiduḥkhitāḥ ।।
taptāyomayasaṃ bhūmirjvalantī tejasodgatā । anekayojanaśataṃ dahati svaciṃṣā ।। kandarpadamanā ghorā arciṣmanto durāsadāḥ । romaharṣaṇarūpāste apyāhurduḥkhā bhayānakāḥ ।।
ete patanti narake ūrdhvapādā avāṅmukhāḥ । ṛṣīṇāmativaktāraḥ saṃyatānāṃ tapasvinām ।। te punastatra pacyante taptāmbhasi kṛtā iva । krandamānā divārātrau, nagā vāteritā iva ।।
praṇadanti mahānādaṃ tīvraduḥkhaiḥ pratāpitāḥ । sarvā diśaśca dhāvanti nārakaiḥ puruṣairdrutāḥ ।। kudṛṣṭyā mohayitvārthe mohapāśāvṛto janaḥ । prāpnoti narakaṃ ghoraṃ kāraṇodadhisaṃvṛtaḥ ।।
kudṛṣṭyā dagdhasarvasvo manuṣyaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ । tathā baddho asti narake mānināṃ ghorakāraṇam ।। ye mithyāvaśamāpannāḥ puruṣā mandamedhasaḥ । te sarve narakaṃ yānti cittairhi parivañcitāḥ ।।
yastvayā duṣkṛtaṃ pūrva kṛtaṃ cittānuvartinā । tasya bhuṅktaphalaṃ mūḍha vipākottama ।। hāryāṇi paricittāni, saṃsevyāḥ parayoṣitaḥ । hrasvā jantavo nityaṃ svacittaparivañcitāḥ ।।
tasya karmavipākasya vaśa eva tvamāgataḥ । kiṃ krandasi svayaṃ kṛtvā kukarma puruṣādhama! ।। ye narāḥ kukṛtaṃ kṛtvā pañcatvaṃ yāntyamedhasaḥ । yeṣāṃ tu niṣphalaṃ janma bījamuptaṃ yathoṣare ।।
alpamādhuryasaṃyuktān kāmān kaṭuvipākinaḥ । sevate yastvasau mūḍhaḥ sa yāti tamaso tamaḥ ।। kiṃ kṛtaṃ mūḍha bhavatā putradārasukhārthinā । dahasye narake caikaḥ svakarmaphalavañcitaḥ ।।
yaḥ putradāravaśagaḥ sevate duṣkaraṃ naraḥ । sa yāti narakatvaṃ pāpaṃ tadanubhūyate ।। na dārā na sutā nārtha na mitrāṇi kathañcana । mṛtyukāle samutpanne rakṣanti samupasthitāḥ ।।
yeṣāṃ sāṃkleśikaṃ cittaṃ tṛṣṇayā parivañcitam । sahāyatā kutasteṣāṃ kasmāt paritapyase? ।। hṛto asi pūrvaviṣayaistṛṣṇayā parivañcitaḥ । kiṃ krandasi svayaṃ kṛtvā kukṛtaṃ mūḍhacetanaḥ ।।
na tathāgnirna śastrāṇi na viṣaṃ nārayaḥ sthitāḥ । bādhate puruṣaṃ loke yathā duṣkṛtyamātmajam ।। digbhāge hi yathā gatvā saṃśrayante vanaspatīn । vihagāḥ kālamutthāya tathā prāṇisamāgamaḥ ।।
nāśayitvā paraṃ dravyaṃ kṛtvā lokavyatikramaṃ । kiṃ karotyaśubhaṃ karma mohena parivañcitaḥ ।। yena yāti parāṃ śāntiṃ yena yātyasurālayam । tatra hetuḥ paraṃ mohastamasāmapi yat tamaḥ ।।
putradāramayaiḥ pāśaiścānītā narakālayam । yadartha kriyate pāpaṃ yuṣmābhiścittavañcitaiḥ ।। mitrāṇi putrāḥ bandhujanabāndhavāḥ । yeṣāmarthe kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhavadbhirmandabuddhibhiḥ ।।
nūnamātmā na te kānto babhūva narabhūmiṣu । yena tvayā kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ putrārthena narādhamaḥ ।। yena pūrvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paścānna paritapyate । sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ putrakāraṇavañcitaḥ ।।
kiṃ kariṣyanti putrāste kiṃ dārāḥ kiṃ ca bāndhavāḥ । dahasyanādinarake vahniḥ karma dunotyasau ।। svayaṃ kṛtvāśubhaṃ karmāsukhodayamaninditaḥ । tapyase api vṛthādhānaḥ paścānmohena vañcikaḥ ।।
rāgadveṣānugāḥ pāpaṃ mohena parivañcitāḥ । aghaṃ prayānti te sarve putradārasukhārthinaḥ ।। antargatena ca punarbahiḥsthena ca vahninā । dahyamāno duḥkhena narake pāpakarmaṇā ।।
vaśaṃ prāptāḥ svacittasya sarva eva viḍambitāḥ । kiṃ krandasi vṛthā nāde vahninā paritāpitaḥ ।। atha pāpāni karmāṇi kṛtavānasi manyase । durmate tatra mā kranda kiṃ vṛthā paridevase ।।
pāpeṣu rakṣyate mūḍhaḥ kāraṇāśuci rakṣyate । pāpānugaphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hetupratyayasambhavam ।। kasmānna sevito dharmaḥ pāpañca nahi varjitam । pāpād bahiśca puruṣo narakaṃ naiva paśyati ।।
yo na vindanti mūḍhātmā phalaṃ pāpasya karttṛkam । so avaśyaṃ labhate doṣān kathaṃ bhokṣyasi durmate ।। pāpena vañcita pūrvaṃ pāpena paridahyate । na kariṣyasi pāpāni tvaduḥkhenaiva yāsyasi ।।
kṛtavānasi pāpāni śubhāni na kathañcana । pāpena dahyate tasmādaśubhe na manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। nāsti duḥkhādato duḥkhaṃ yaḥ pāpamanusevate । tasmāt pāpaṃ na seveta yadi duḥkhaṃ na vāñchasi ।।
tasyāntarhṛdaye bimbaṃ kintu śāntirna vidyate । kāruṇyāspadabhūtāḥ smo nāsmākaṃ karuṇāhṛdi ।। yathā kṛtaṃ bhavadbhiśca pāpaṃ mohāvṛtairbahu । tad vaḥ pradhāvate gāḍhaṃ na ca ye tatra hetavaḥ ।।
śīlaṃ na rakṣitaṃ mūḍha pāpaṃ ca bahu sañcitam । sambhūtasya ca pāpasya phalametadupasthitam ।। na vayaṃ kāraṇaṃ tatra yūyameva hi kāraṇam । yaḥ pāpaṃ kurute karma sa hetustasya karmaṇaḥ ।।
bhavadbhiryat kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tṛṣṇāśāpaviḍambitaiḥ । tad vo prapadyate ghoraṃ kimasmān paribhāṣata ।। nākṛtaṃ pacyate pāpaṃ na pāpaṃ syādahetukam । yena yaddhi kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tasya tat paripacyate ।।
tad bhavantaḥ kriyāhīnā madyapānena vañcitāḥ । patitā narake tīvre kiṃ vṛthā paritapyatha ।। te yūyaṃ kāmaparamāḥ ghoraṃ narakamāgatāḥ । kāraṇeṣvapi tīvreṣu kiṃ tathā paritapyatha ।।
yadā kṛtāni pāpāni bhavadbhiḥ kāmamohitaiḥ । tadā kasmānna nikṛṣṭaṃ kimadya paritapyatha ।। hetubhūto hi narako mṛṣāvādasya deśitaḥ । heturvai sevitaṃ pūrva niṣphalaṃ paridevatha ।।
nārthena labhate satyaṃ na kṛcchreṇopapadyate । tasmāt satyaṃ parityajya mṛṣāvādeṣu rajyase ।। pūrveṣu pāpamahitaṃ bhavatā mūḍhacetasā । kṛtaṃ bhavadbhiḥ kukṛtaṃ paripacyate ।।
pāpakṣayād vinirmukto narakaṃ nopalabhyate । nākrandamānāḥ puruṣāḥ vimucyante kathañcana ।। kiṃ krandatha vṛthā mūḍhā vañcitāḥ svena karmaṇā । muñcitā vañcitā bālā vṛthā krandantyabuddhayaḥ ।।
ahitairhitarūpaistvaṃ mitrarūpaiśca śatrubhiḥ । vipralabdho asi bho martya! gacchannasi mahat tamaḥ ।। nānyaḥ śatruryathā karma duṣkṛtaṃ tava pāpakam । karmaṇā trividhenātha nīyase yamasādhanam ।।
kasmādasi tato mūḍha, vañcitaḥ putrasaṃjñakaiḥ । na dānādiṣu buddhistaiḥ kṛtā mohavañcitā ।। asmāṃllokātparaṃ lokaṃ śatrupṛṣṭhorago yathā । śatrūṇāṃ prathamaḥ śatruḥ sarvapāpanidarśakaḥ ।।
viṣāgniśastrapratima! svayaṃ hi duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam । tvayā kṛtāni karmāṇi tvamevamanubhokṣyase ।। yasya śāntaṃ sadā cittaṃ viṣayairyo na hanyate । na hyavasthāmimāṃ yānti tathātvamanupaśyasi ।।
narakasya dhvaniṃ śrutvā kathaṃ krandasi durmate! । kiṃ punaryatra vahnistvāṃ dhakṣyati śuṣkakāṣṭhavat ।। na dagdhā vahninā ye ca dagdhāste kukṛtaiḥ svakaiḥ । vahnistu śāmyate kvāpi duṣkṛtāgnirna śāmyati ।।
nāgnirniryāti lokāntaṃ nāgnispṛṣṭo naro । kukṛtāgnimayaṃ pāpaṃ yad dhakṣyati hi tattvataḥ ।। kukṛtāgnividagdhā ye te dagdhā narake narāḥ । pāpāgnivarjitā ye tu na teṣāṃ narakodayaḥ ।
yadyātmanaḥ priyo nityaṃ vibheṣi narakād yadi ।। vivarjaya svapāpāni tato duḥkhaṃ na yāsyasi । yānti pāpamaye nityaṃ mohavaśānugāḥ ।। prāpnoṣi narakaṃ ghoraṃ kimaśrūṇi vimuñcasi? ।
duḥkhaṃ duḥkhavipākaṃ ca duḥkhāntagamanaṃ tathā ।। sukṛtaṃ nādimadhyāntaśobhanaṃ paripacyate । nātra loke tvayāpāpaṃ yatkṛtaṃ sukṛtaṃ ।। tasya tīvravipākasya phalamadyopabhokṣyase ।
hetupratyayasādṛśyaṃ viparītaṃ na kalpyate ।। hetuḥ kṛto yathā pūrva tathā phalamavāpsyasi । yathā tava tathānyeṣāṃ prāṇarakṣā prayatnataḥ ।। kasmāt prāṇātipātāste kṛtāḥ pāpānuvartinā ।
prāṇatyāgena puruṣairyad dhanaṃ samupārjitam ।। karmodayakṛtaṃ tatte yattvayā samupārjitam । sarveṣāṃ dayitā dārāḥ prāṇebhyo api garīyasaḥ ।। tattvayā rāgaraktena kasmādapakṛtāvanāt ।
buddhervyāmohajanakaṃ dharmāṇāṃ dūṣaṇaṃ param ।। dharmapānaṃ tvayā kārya karmānuparivarjitam । jihvāviṣasamutthaṃ yat sarvāpratyayakārakam ।। mṛṣāvādaṃ tvayā pāpaṃ karmānuparivarjitam ।
evaṃ pañcavidheyeṣu yasmāt tvamanuraktavān ।। tasmāt saṃmukṣya mā rodi kiṃ vṛthā paridevase । viṣayaṃ pāpakā dharmā yasmānnu parivañcitaḥ ।। tasmāt prāpnoṣi narakaṃ jvālāmālākulaṃ mahat ।
etat tṛṣṇāgninā sarva pradīptaṃ bhuvanatrayam ।। dṛṣṭvā nācarito dharmaḥ kimadya paritapyase । te madhuraṃ cittaṃ kāmamandirakaṃ vacaḥ ।। udīrite mahāpāpe tasmai tatphalamāgatam ।
sa kṛtvā pāpakaṃ karma niyatā pāpavedanā ।। karuṇaṃ vikalaṃ dīnaṃ kimadya paritapyase । karmakṣayeṇa narakāt mucyante pāpakāriṇaḥ ।। vikrośamagnā bahuśo na mucyante kathañcana ।
aniṣṭaṃ pāpakaṃ karma kṛtvā rogavaśe sthitāḥ ।। paridevati yo mūḍho vṛthā sa paridevati । anāgataphalajño yaḥ pratyutpannaśubhe rataḥ ।। krośate narake nāsau yathā tvamanutapyase ।
mayā kṛtāni karmāṇi phaladāni mamaiva hi ।। rogeṇa śatruṇā dagdhaḥ paścānnarakamāgataḥ । pramādabhūmiraśubhā rāgadagdhasya dehinaḥ ।। tena pāśena baddho ahaṃ gato avasthāmimāṃ bhṛśam ।
durācāraratānāṃ tu nṛṇāmasya phalaṃ kaṭu ।। ajñānabādhito asmīti svakṛtaṃ bhujyate mayā । nirdayānāṃ sughorāṇāṃ pāpānāṃ vaśamāgataḥ ।। muktirasmāt kathaṃ syādvai duḥkhasaṃsārasāgarāt ।
duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ karma mayedaṃ paripacyate ।। sukhāvāptiṃ na paśyāmi kṣemaṃ vā narakasya me । jīvalokādahaṃ bhraṣṭo abuddha iva mārgataḥ ।। jīvo ayaṃ vivaśo bhūtvā vikṛtaiḥ parivāritaḥ ।
jvālāmālākulaṃ sarvamantarikṣaṃ nirantaram ।। diśaśca tridiśaścaiva pṛthi ca nirantarā । kṛpaṇo ajñānago duḥkhī nivāsaṃ nopalakṣaye ।। kṣuradhārāvitaptasya nṛpasyāsyātibhīṣaṇam ।
kāntāre bāhyamānasya niḥ sahāyasya sarvataḥ । trātāraṃ nāvagacchāmi yo asmād duḥkhāt pramocayet ।। niḥśaktiravaśo duḥkhī vahninā paritāpitaḥ । nīye ahaṃ vivaśaḥ kvāpi bāhubandhanayantritaḥ ।।
na vārthā nāpi mitrāṇi na putrā na ca yoṣitaḥ । trāyante vyasanādasmāt kṛtaghnā bata te mama ।। nirānandasya na sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ । mṛtyupāśena baddhasya śaraṇaṃ nopalakṣyate ।।
saṃkruddhā iva te, krūrā bhaviṣyanti samantataḥ । nirānandā diśaḥ sarvā vyālaiśca parivāritā ।। narakaṃ pātakasyaiva pateyaṃ dhṛtibhāvataḥ । yacca yaccehaṃ paśyāmi jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ tathā ।
tat sarva vyākulaṃ caiva vahninā paridīpitam ।। nādhigacchāmi śaraṇaṃ niḥsahāyo asmi sarvataḥ । ghore tamasi majjāsi sāgare ca hṛtaplavaḥ ।। gaganaṃ naiva paśyāmi nakṣatragrahatārakam ।
viparītamidaṃ sarva tamasā parivāritam ।। pañcendriyāṇi sarvāṇi viratāni hi sarvataḥ । krakacaistu tadā sarva śarīraṃ paripāṭayate ।। nādhigacchāmi śaraṇaṃ kāmaṃ bandho bhaviṣyati ।
vardhante duḥkhanikarā sarvataḥ parivārataḥ ।। muhurmuhuśca vardhante vedanāñcitadehajāḥ । duḥkhaiśca nissahāyaṃ ca sarvataḥ ।। samīkṣya karmajaṃ nityaṃ dhyeyo hetuḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
kathayanti sukhaṃ vṛddhāḥ svakarmaphalajairdṛḍham ।। yat pūrva karaṇīyaṃ te tatpaścāt paricintyase । mohena vañcitaḥ pūrvaṃ kimadya paritapyase । kiṃ punaḥ pāpakartturyaḥ kaṭukaṃ paripacyate ।।
anekaduḥkhahetūtthaṃ tava duḥkhaṃ bhaviṣyati । trāṇaṃ naiva yatrāsti vinā karmaparikṣayāt ।। evaṃ satyasya nāśena yamadūtairanekaśaḥ । nīyate narakaṃ ghoraṃ karmapāśavaśaṅgataḥ ।।
catuṣkoṇaścaturdvāro vibhakto bhāgaśo mitaḥ । pacyate yatra vivaśā nārakeyā hyanekaśaḥ ।। bhedaprāyeṇa bahuśo yattvayā kathitaṃ bahu । kalmaṣaṃ bhūtadharmāṇāṃ tasyaitat phalamāgatam ।।
bhasmībhavanti te nityaṃ mitrasvajanabāndhavaiḥ । eṣāmabhimataṃ duṣṭaṃ paiśunyaṃ sadvigarhitam ।। tasmānna carito dharmaḥ paiśunyaṃ ca na varjitam । paiśunyaṃ saphalaṃ bhuktvā kimadya paritapyase ।।
jihvādhanavinirmuktaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ viṣamamucchritam । pāruṣyamiti sandṛṣṭamaho! tatphalamīdṛśam ।। sattvaṃ pāruṣyaparamaṃ ghoraṃ narakamāgatam । jihvāyātaṃ tavākṛtyai kimadya paridevase ।।
sahastraguṇaparyantaḥ svato hṛdayasambhavaḥ । kṣutpipāsāmayo vahniḥ samādahati mārutam ।। yadantaraṃ himāgnyorhi merusarṣapayośca yat । tadantaraṃ jihvayoktyā narake jvalanasya ca ।।
narakaprabhavo vahnirna kvāpyanyatra prāpyate । kṣutpipāsāmayo vahnirdeveṣvapyupalabhyate ।। yo hyataḥ kāraṇāttīkṣṇo vahnirbhavati nārakaḥ । na tathā sa prabhavati yathā vahnistadudbhavaḥ ।।
pūrvottarā baddhapadaṃ nirarthakamasaṅgatam । vistrabdha yattvayā proktaṃ tasyaitatphalamāgatam ।। pareṣāṃ sampadaṃ dṛṣṭvā mama syāditi cintitam । tamo abhikhyāsamutthasya viṣasya phalamāgatam ।।
vyāpārānaladagdho asi mānuṣyaṃ puruṣādhama! । dahanād dahanaṃ prāpto tapyase ca vikatthyase ।। vyāpāraparamohe tu narakāyopapattaye । rajjvaitayaiva baddho asi puruṣaḥ parikrandase ।।
vyāpādenākṛṣṭo asi ghoraṃ narakamāgataḥ । karmakṣayād bhavenmokṣo narakācca vimokṣyase ।। adharmo dharmarūpeṇa sādhurūpeṇa pāpakam । yat tvayā kathitaṃ pūrva tat tvāṃ dahati nānalaḥ ।।
kathaṃ tattvavinaṣṭānāṃ dharmādharmanicchatām । deśitaṃ vivaraṃ pāpaṃ niyataṃ pāpagāmikam ।। tvayā varjito dharmaḥ sādhavaścāpi ninditāḥ । yattvayopārjitaṃ kṛṣṭaṃ tattvayādya vipacyate ।।
tṛṣṇāviṣayayuktena mohavegena sarvadā । yataḥ sadharmavinayaiḥ kiṃ tathā paridevase ।। sa bhavet pāpakṛnnityaṃ mohapāśavaśaṅgataḥ । ki tapyase rodiṣi ca karma kṛtvā sudāruṇam ।।
hetupratyayamūḍhasya dharmādharmeṣu sarvadā । prāpto asi narakaṃ ghoraṃ nārakāgraṃ sudāruṇam ।। kāmaiḥ kramati saṃyuktairyanna bhavati ceṣṭitam । sukṛtaṃ karmavirasaṃ phalametadupasthitam ।।
kṣapayitvā pramādena sukhāsaktena cetasā । sukṛta narakaṃ yānti devāḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ ।। āryāpavādakā ye ca ye ca karmaphaladviṣaḥ । te mṛtvā narakaṃ yānti ye ca mithyāvinītakāḥ ।।
jananīgṛhapāpīyā ye cānye dharmavañcakāḥ । teṣāmiṣṭakarā loke narakasya ca gāminaḥ ।। ye cānye sukhasaṃsaktā nityaṃ pāparatā narāḥ । duḥkhād duḥkhaṃ tu te yānti cittena parivañcitāḥ ।।
tasmādavadyakārye na matiṃ । hīnānyavadyakāryāṇi narake pātayanti ca ।। kuryāt kuśalāni nityaṃ parārthabaddhena manorathena । । sevyo apavargo daśadharma eṣaḥ ।।
।। iti narakavargaḥ ṣoḍaśaḥ ।। adāntasya kutaḥ śāntiranuptasya kutaḥ phalam? । adīpikā prabhā nāsti adānasya kutaḥ sukham ।। hṛcchāntirhi tathā nāsti nayanārthasya dehinaḥ ।
dānena virahāt tadvat sukhaṃ pretairna labhyate ।। yaṃ pretya pretalokasya triloke ca yathādhamāḥ । bhrameṇa paramodvignāstanmātsaryakṛtaṃ phalam ।। na dātrā labhyate kiñcit kṛtanāśo na vidyate ।
svakarmaphalabhoktāraḥ prāṇinaḥ karmabhoginaḥ ।। tava yatkukṛtaṃ dagdhāḥ pretyalokeṣvavasthitāḥ । kṣutpipāsāmayeneha vahninā paridīpitāḥ ।। kadā tu viṣayo asmākaṃ bhaviṣyati sukhodayaḥ ।
paridāhāt kadā cāsmāt parimokṣo bhaviṣyati ।। mārgāmārgavivikto ahaṃ na jñātaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam । kṣutpipāsāmayo vahnirajñātaḥ prakaṭodayaḥ ।। kleśāndhakāravadanā nirāśāstyaktajīvikāḥ ।
tvaksnāyujālabaddhāḥ sma jīvāmo bata duḥkhitāḥ ।। na trātā sarvato asmākaṃ hanta kṛcchragatā vayam । utpanneṣu manuṣyeṣu khaṇḍitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।। kasmānna carito dharmo ratnadīpeṣu sañcitaḥ ।
yaḥ karoti śubhaṃ nityamaśubhaṃ na ca sarvadā ।। samadṛṣṭipathenaiti svargasopānamāśritaḥ । yeṣāmarthe kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kleśayan mānasaṃ bahu ।। anena te gatāḥ sarve bhavānāṃ trāsane sthitaḥ ।
baddho asi bandhanaistīvrairyamadattairadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। prāpto asi tamaso ghoraṃ yamalokaṃ durāsadam । ihopabhokṣyase karma yattvayā kukṛtaṃ kṛtam ।। svakṛtaṃ bhujyate bāla! pareṣāṃ naiva bhujyate ।
ākṛṣyamāṇa eṣo atra pāparajjvā sughorayā ।। analaḥ pretalokasya kṣutpipāsāmayo mahān nāgniśastraviṣāṇāṃ hi nipātastādṛśaḥ kaṭuḥ ।। kṣutpipāsāmayāgneśca nipāto yādṛśaḥ । na kṣaṇo nāpi hi lavo na muhūrto na śarvarī ।।
yatra saukhyaṃ bhavenmṛtyurnityaṃ duḥkhāvṛtā vayam । duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ prāpto duḥkhaheturniṣevitaḥ ।। duḥkhāt kadācinmokṣaḥ syād bhaviṣyati sukhodayaḥ । notsave dṛśyate toyaṃ taḍāgeṣu ca śuṣyati ।।
sarito nāśamāyāsuḥ kathaṃ dhāvāmahe cayam । te vayaṃ śuṣkasalilāḥ saśailavanakānanāḥ ।। paridhāvāmahe bhūmau nityaṃ salilakāṃkṣiṇaḥ । te vayaṃ dagdhatanavaḥ kṣutpipāsāhatā narāḥ ।।
śaraṇaṃ nādhigacchāmaḥ kaṣṭaṃ vyasanamāgatāḥ । vajradaṃṣṭrairmahātīkṣṇaiḥ kākolūkaiśca sammataḥ ।। abhidruto na paśyāmi śaraṇaṃ saukhyadāyakam । pratibimbamidaṃ tasya karmaṇaḥ samupasthitam ।।
kṛtaṃ karma yathāsmābhistathedaṃ phalamāgatam । karmavāyuragā baddhāḥ karmasūtreṇa pācitāḥ ।। palāyanaṃ na paśyāma ṛte karmakṣayāditi । yasya pāpānyaniṣṭāni vahnivat tāni paśyati ।।
sa naiti pretabhavanaṃ kṣutpipāsānalāvṛtam । muhurmuhuḥ pravardhante vedanā narakodbhavāḥ ।। jvālāmālākulasyaiva śailasya sadṛśā vayam । jvalitaḥ śāmyate śailaḥ salilenaiva sarvathā ।।
sa samudropamo vahnirammākaṃ naiva śāmyati । kasmin kṣaṇe samudbhūtastṛṣṇāvāyusahāyavān ।। karmāgnirnirdahatyasmān parivāryasamantataḥ । te vayaṃ pāpakarmāṇaḥ śukladharmavivarjitāḥ ।।
pretalokamimaṃ prāptāḥ svargasya phalamohitāḥ । kṣutpipāsāmayo vahnirdvitīyaścāgnisambhavaḥ ।। mudgarāśimayā na putrāḥ na ca bāndhavāḥ । vañcito asmi svacittena karmaṇā parivañcitā ।।
prāpto asmi pretabhavanaṃ mitrajñātinirākṛtaḥ । na dārāḥ nāpi mitrāṇi na putrāḥ nāpi bāndhavāḥ ।। trāyate karmapāśena nīyamānaṃ balīyasā । nānyastrātā yathā karma trividhaṃ bhujyate mayā ।।
dānaṃ śīlaṃ śrutaṃ cāpi trividhaṃ parikīrtitam । mohajālavṛteneha yanmayā kukṛtaṃ kṛtam ।। karmaṇo hetubhūtasya yatkṛtaṃ phalamāgatam । yadi mucyāmahe pāpāt pretalokād durāsadāt ।।
na bhūyaḥ pāpakaṃ karma kariṣyāmi kathañcana । uṣṇānyuṣṇavipākāni mahāpīḍākarāṇi ca । kukarmāṇyaśubhānīha tasmāttāni vivarjayet ।। ।। iti pretavargaḥ saptadaśaḥ ।।
bhakṣaṇaṃ bhavadanyonyavadhabandhāvarodhanam । tiryagyoniṃ samāsādya tasmād drohaṃ vivarjayet ।। mohopahatacittāśca śīladānavivarjitāḥ । tiryagyonau va jāyante bālāstṛṣṇāviḍambitāḥ ।।
gamyāgamyaṃ na vindanti bhakṣyābhakṣyaṃ tathaiva ca । kāryākāryabahirbhūtā dharmādharmatiraskṛtāḥ ।। pañcendriyajarāmūḍhāstṛṣṇāpāśavaśānugāḥ । krodherṣyāmatisaṃgrastāstiryagyonyupagā narāḥ ।।
paryeṣṭyupahatā martyāḥ pramādopahatāḥ surāḥ । kṣuttarṣavyasanāḥ pretāḥ kāraṇātte ca nārakāḥ ।। parasparabadhātyuktāstiryagyoniparāyaṇāḥ evaṃ bahuvidhaistaistairvyasanairākulaṃ jagat ।। na kuryāda duṣkṛtaṃ karma mātsaryopahataḥ param ।
mātsaryopahatā yānti pretāstiryakṣu jantavaḥ ।। teṣāṃ hi saphalaṃ janma teṣāṃ buddhiravañcitā । te ca pūjyāḥ sadā sadbhiryeṣāṃ dharme sadā matiḥ ।। evaṃ tridoṣākṛtakarmasāraṃ jagad bhramatyeva durāvagādham ।
karoti yastasya ca śuddhasattvo avamānanāṃ jñānarathāvarūḍhaḥ ।। ।। iti tiryagvargo aṣṭādaśaḥ ।। saṃsāre prāyaśo duḥkhaṃ traidhātukakṣudhāmayam । yeneme pīḍitāḥ sattvāḥ kurvantyaśubhamātmanaḥ ।।
svadehe yuktito vahnirbubhukṣetyadhīyate । śeṣo dahati lokān vai kalpānala iva drumān ।। lokottaramimaṃ vahniṃ gacchantamanugacchati । nātmanirvāṇasandṛṣṭaṃ kalpāntaraśatairapi ।।
nānalasya hi tadvīrya kṣudhāyā yādṛśaṃ balam । traidhātukamidaṃ kṛtsnamāhāraṃ prati vartate ।। mohayed vividhā cintā loke manujasambhavāḥ । tāḥ sarvā bhojanārthāya bhavanti tribhavārṇave ।।
antarābhavasaṃsthasya kṛṣyamāṇasya karmabhiḥ । dīrghāgamasya yad duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।। avidyendhanamagnasya dahyamānasya coṣmaṇā । garbhasthasya hi yad duḥkha na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।
āhārarasagṛddhasya nityaṃ tadgatacetasaḥ । yad duḥkhaṃ paragṛddhasya na ca varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।। dṛḍhā vidagdhamanasaḥ kāme vā taptacetasaḥ । yad bhavatyadhikaṃ duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।
apriyaiḥ saha saṃsargo viṣayāstasya nityaśaḥ । praṇaṣṭe hṛdi yad duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।। tṛṣṇāviṣavidagdhasya nityaṃ paryeṣaṇātmakam । āmṛtyu yad bhave duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।
avyucchinnaṃ bahuvidhaṃ yad duḥkhaṃ pāpamitrajam । apāyajanakaṃ yasya na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।। vyasanaṃ putradārāṇāṃ yad dṛṣṭ hṛdi jāyate । narakāṇāṃ mahāmārgo na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।
kṣutpipāsāvidagdhasya dīpyamānasya vahninā । yad duḥkhaṃ naṣṭamanaso na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।। ajastraṃ paribhūtasya mitrajñātisuhṛjjanaiḥ । yad bhavecchokajaṃ duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।
dārapralambanagataṃ duścalaṃ priyacetasaḥ । yad duḥkhaṃ jīrṇakāyasya na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।। mṛtyunā hriyamāṇasya tasmāṃllokātmano rasāt । yad duḥkhaṃ jāyate vṛttau na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।
yat kurvantyaśubhaṃ bālā yacca gacchati durgatim । tadāharati dānena kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। pratiduṣkṛtakarmāṇi varjanīyāni sarvadā । sukṛteṣu manaḥ kārya dānaśīlavibhūṣitam ।।
।। iti kṣudhāvarga ekonaviṃśaḥ ।। kausīdyamatimāyā ca dambhaḥ pāruṣyameva ca । niyātabhūmayo dṛṣṭā jñānasya ca vivarjanam ।। saṃśleṣaścāpyasādhūnāṃ sādhūnāṃ varjanaṃ tathā ।
nāśasya hetavaḥ śaktā mithyādarśanameva ca ।। adeśakālasaṃraṃbho vācyāvācyamajānataḥ । anarthabhūmayo hyetā visrambhaścāpi tanmayaḥ ।। yena tena ca samprītiḥ yatra tatra ca bhojanam ।
lāghavaṃ janayatyante apraśaṃsā cātmanastathā ।। dhairyanāśaḥ smṛtibhraṃśo virodhaḥ pārthivena ca । akrāntamṛtyavo hyete krūratā manasi sthitā ।। akarmāphalatattvajño dharmādharmavahiṣkṛtaḥ ।
puruṣaḥ sādhunirmuktaḥ prapātagamanāśayaḥ ।। kausīdyamatinidrā ca rasanā gṛhyate tathā । puṃdveṣayonayaḥ proktāḥ pāruṣyavacanaṃ tathā ।। atilobho apamānaśca atimānaśca cāpalam ।
dharmavarjyā kāmasevā mohasya paridīpikāḥ ।। trayāṇāmiha doṣāṇāṃ kausīdyaṃ mūlamucyate । vīryārambheṇa duṣyante doṣā manasi sambhavāḥ ।। vīryārambheṇa hi phalaṃ hyavaśyamupabhujyate ।
nyāyenārabdhatattvasya karmaṇo dṛśyate phalam ।। karmaṇastrividhasyāsya phalaṃ trividhamucyate । trirāśiniyataṃ tacca triśūlaṃ tribhavānugam ।। pāpasevī pracaṇḍo yaḥ kausīdyamapi sevate ।
dharmavidveṣakaḥ krūro anutpathānupadhāvati ।। yasya tasya ca santuṣṭo yasya tasya prakupyati । yatra tatra ca saṃsakto sa mūḍha iti kathyate ।। kausīdyaṃ svamanasaḥ pramādaviṣamūrcchitam ।
prapātaṃ taṃ ca saṃrabdhamavisaṃvādakaṃ param ।। vīryārambhe mahāpāpakausīdyamalavarjitāḥ । vimukterupabhoktāraste janāḥ sukhabhāginaḥ ।। kausīdyaṃ sarvadharmāṇāmajarāmarakārakam ।
tena doṣeṇa mahatā narā duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ ।। sahāyaśca sukhāveśī tasmāt tat parivarjayet । tena viddho hi puruṣaḥ svadhistutyaḥ samantataḥ ।। kusīdasyālpabhāgasya mohāpahṛtacetasaḥ ।
kutsitaḥ svajanaiḥ sarvairna gatirvidyate śivā ।। kausīdyapāpasaṃsargīstyānamiddhaṃ tathaiva ca । mokṣadvāravighātāya bhavantyete mahābhayāḥ ।। āhrīkyamanapatrāpyamauddhatyaṃ pāpamitratā ।
duḥkhasyaitāni harmyāṇi tebhyo rakṣennu paṇḍitaḥ ।। kausīdyenābhibhūtā ye nirārambhā gatitviṣaḥ । socchvāsamaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi niṣphalam ।। jīvamānā na jīvanti kausīdyopahatā narāḥ ।
mṛtyoratyadhikaṃ hyetat kausīdyamiti manyate ।। kausīdyapaṅkamagnā ye magnāste duḥkhasaṃstare । ārabdhavīryā ye puṃsaste tīrṇā bhavasāgarāt ।। kausīdyānmandavīryo yaḥ sadā pāparataśca yaḥ ।
sa jīvamāno api mṛto mṛtastu narakāya saḥ ।। nirdhanāḥ paśubhistulyāste narā duḥkhabhāginaḥ । parapiṇḍāśino dīnāḥ kausīdyaṃ tatra kāraṇam ।। prāyaśastu kusīdānāṃ paradāropajīvinām ।
ratābhilāṣo atyadhiko maithune ca sadā ratiḥ ।। te tattvakārikā riktāḥ kevalāhāratatparāḥ । mṛtyukāle samutpanne dahyante svena cetasā ।। śītoṣṇaṃ ca sahantyete kṣutpipāse tathaiva ca ।
gātrāntā ca kriyā kāryā yātrā dharmāya sarvadā ।। na kausīdye matiṃ kuryāt kuśīle śīlakāmukaḥ । saṃsāre sīdati nityaṃ na ca duḥkhāt pramucyate ।। paribhūya satāṃ madhye kusīdāllokavañcitaḥ ।
vañcitaśca bhavatyante śarmaṇo vā vimucyate ।। vīryavān smṛtisaṃlabdha ekāntanirataḥ sadā । vimuktapāpakaidharmairmokṣaṃ prāpnoti yatnataḥ ।। evaṃvidhā duḥkhaparamparā hi, sattvaḥ kukarmeṣu na kuryāt ।
loke tridoṣānalasampradīpte, kuryāt parāṃ śāntikṛpā mṛte na ।। ।। iti kausīdyavargo viṃśaḥ ।। cittañca vāk tathā karma saṃyojanantu pāpakam । narakapretatiryakkṣutkausīdyāni vidurdaśa ।।
।। iti dvitīyam udānam ।। (karuṇādānaśīlāni kṣāntirvīryamathāpi ca । dhyānaṃ prajñātha nirvāṇo mano bhikṣuśca te daśa ।। ) kṛpā sarveṣu bhūteṣu māteva hitakāriṇī ।
yāṃ samāśritya puruṣāḥ prayānti sukhamuttamam ।। dayānveṣīha puruṣaḥ sarvasattvahite rataḥ । pūjanīyaḥ satāṃ yāti pretya svarge ca modate ।। dayāvantaḥ sadāvarta sarvabhūtahite ratam ।
tamevaṃ puruṣaṃ nityaṃ praṇamanti divaukasaḥ ।। prayāti devalokaṃ ca śīlavān karuṇānvitaḥ । kṛpānvitaḥ sa puruṣo candramā iva śobhate ।। āśrayanti ca bhūtāni gataśokā gatavyathā ।
tasmād dayāprayatnena sevitavyā sukhārthinā ।। yasya vāk kāyacitte kāruṇyena vibhūṣite । tasya mitramayā lokā bhavanti yaśasā vṛtāḥ ।। kāruṇyārdrasya viduṣo nityaṃ mṛdvindriyasya ca ।
samyagdṛṣṭiprayatnasya nirvāṇaṃ nāti dūrataḥ ।। manuṣyaloke te devā ye kāruṇyena vibhūṣitāḥ । kāruṇyena daridrā ye te daridrāḥ satāṃ matāḥ ।। mṛdvāśayā hi ye martyāḥ sādhuvat kāñcanopamāḥ ।
kāruṇyamakṣayaṃ yeṣāṃ sadā manasi vartate ।। te ca sattvāḥ sadodyuktā nityaṃ dharmaparāyaṇāḥ । yeṣāṃ kāruṇyadīpena hṛdayaṃ samprakāśitam ।। na rātrau na divā teṣāṃ dharmo hi vinivartate ।
yeṣāṃ sarvāsvavasthāsu karuṇābhirataṃ matam ।। kāruṇyaśītalaṃ cittaṃ sarvasattvahite ratam । bhuktvā saukhyaṃ nirupamaṃ paścād gacchati nirvṛtim ।। kāruṇyaṃ munibhiḥ śastaṃ kāruṇyaṃ nirmalaṃ saraḥ ।
kāruṇyaṃ doṣanirghāti kāruṇyaṃ dhanamavyayam ।। guṇānāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ cāgraṃ sarvadoṣavighātakam । kāruṇyārdrā hi paramaṃ prayānti dhanamacyutam ।। kāruṇyaṃ dhanaṃ yasmānmādhuryapayasā yutam ।
na dāhaḥ krodhajastasya hṛdaye sampravartate ।। kāruṇyanāvamāruhya prītirdhairyaparāyaṇaḥ । tridoṣormimahāvege bhrāmyate bhavasāgare ।। guṇānāmadvayaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vinā cittena bhūṣaṇam ।
sādhūnāṃ dayitaṃ nityaṃ kāruṇyamiti kathyate ।। mārdavaṃ yasya hṛdaye vilīnamiva kāñcanam । sa jano hi tu kalpānte duḥkhādāśu vimucyate ।। yasya pātrīkṛtaṃ cittaṃ mārdaveṇa samantataḥ ।
śreyāṃsi tasya rohanti kedāra iva śālayaḥ ।। cetogṛhe nidhānaṃ tadavyayaṃ dehinaḥ । nirvāsayati dāridrayaṃ nṛṇāmadhyāśayaṃ mahat ।। tīkṣṇendriyasyāśāntasya nidhyānasya vicāriṇaḥ ।
viṣayeṣu pramattasya duḥkhaṃ naiva pradhāvati ।। maitreṇa cetasā nityamanukampādayā parāḥ । te hetuphalatattvajñā duḥkhapāśād vinirgatāḥ ।। na saṅkalpe mano yeṣāṃ ramate doṣavarjitam ।
te doṣabhayanirmuktāḥ padaṃ gacchantyanuttaram ।। kṣāntikriyāsamāyukte mitravānakutobhayaḥ । priyo bhavati loke asmin paścād deveṣu modate ।। mātṛvat pitṛvaccaiva sarvalokasya te janāḥ ।
dayāratnaṃ sadā yeṣāṃ manasi sthitamuttamam ।। sukhasya ca paraṃ mūlaṃ kṛpaiva parikīrtitā । yasya kṛpā nāsti sa duḥkhī parikīrtyate ।। ekasatyottaraṃ brahma ekasyānuttaraṃ śivam ।
ekavidyā paraṃ mātā maitrī caikā sukhāvahā ।। ahiṃsakāḥ sadā dhanyāḥ saddṛṣṭiḥ paramā śubhā । etad ṛju sadā satyaṃ pāpānāṃ cāpi varjanam ।। karttavyaḥ puruṣaistasmāt kṛpāsaṃvegamānasaiḥ ।
dānaśīlakṣamāmaitrījñānābhyāsaśca nirmalaḥ ।। ।। iti karuṇāvarga ekaviṃśaḥ ।। guṇadvādaśasaṃyuktaṃ malairdvādaśabhirvinā । dānaṃ bhavati śuddhaṃ tad viparītaṃ sakalmaṣam ।।
devānāmatha nṛṇāṃ dhanasya balamuttamam । dānena rahitā pāde patanti puruṣādhamāḥ ।। lobhamātsaryamalināḥ putradāravaśānugāḥ । manujā nidhanaṃ yānti kevalāhārakāṃkṣiṇaḥ ।।
lobhagranthivimokṣāya yāñcāvṛkṣakṣayāya ca । tamonicayanāśāya pradānamiha dīyate ।। aghatāṃ carate dānaṃ dātāpi tadanantaram । mārgasandarśavad dānaṃ paralokaṃ samṛcchati ।।
dānāmbhasi narāḥ snātvā śīlormiparibhāvite । jñānavistīrṇa pāraṃ duḥkhasya yānti vai ।। puruṣeṇa trayo dīpāḥ prajvālyā hitamicchatā । dānaṃ śīlaṃ tathā jñānamete doṣavināśakāḥ ।।
tṛṣṇāvivarṇā durgandhivitarkormijhaṣākule । duḥkhārṇave plutā hyete jñānaśīleṣu rakṣitāḥ ।। kleśavyādhinihantārastrayo vai bheṣajāḥ smṛtāḥ । dānaṃ śīlaṃ tathā jñānamete nityaṃ sukhāvahāḥ ।।
pramādaviṣamaṃ saṃkalpakuṭilaṃ laghu । vadhyate bandhanairetaistribhirjñānādibhirnṛṇām ।। doṣāgnibhiḥ pluṣṭo yairidaṃ dahyate tadā । dānādijñānayogena hatvā gacchati nirvṛtim ।।
na dānajñāna śīleṣu yeṣāṃ sammiśritā matiḥ । te nityaduḥkhitāḥ sattvāḥ sukhaṃ teṣāṃ na vidyate ।। adānavrīḍitasukhāścittadoṣeṇa vañcitāḥ । bhavanti vibudhāḥ hitvā tasmād dānaparo bhavet ।।
dānotkarṣakramairyuktāḥ mātsaryamalavarjitāḥ । bhavanti hṛṣṭamanaso devāḥ krīḍāparāyaṇāḥ ।। kṣutpipāsāmayo vahnirya pradhānaṃ pradhāvati । mātsarya vai phalaṃ sarva taduktaṃ tattvabuddhibhiḥ ।।
yo dadāti sukhaṃ tasya nīyate jāyate sukham । sukhaṃ bhavati dānāddhi tasmād dānaṃ praśasyate ।। lokālokakaraṃ dānaṃ gacchantamanugacchati । gataṃ ca mantradānena yujyate bhadravatsalaiḥ ।।
avisaṃvādakaṃ sthānametaduktaṃ tathāgataiḥ । avisaṃvādakatvācca nityaṃ dānaparo bhavet ।। mātsaryāriṃ vinirjitya kṛtvā cittaṃ śubhānvitam । ye prayacchanti dānāni te taranti bhavārṇavam ।।
kṣayaistu trividhairdānaṃ triṣukāraṃ tridhārjitam । tasya kṣatānvitasyaivaṃ phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tricakṣuṣā ।। dānamādau sadā deyaṃ śīlaṃ labhyaṃ prayatnataḥ । tṛṣṇā jñānena hantavyā mārga eṣa sukhāvahaḥ ।।
anityā pāpikā tṛṣṇā lokasyāhitakārikā । na śakyaṃ tadvinā śreyaḥ prāptuṃ padamanuttamam ।। adāne na manaḥ kārya nityaṃ dānarato bhavet । adānāt kṣutpipāsābhyāṃ dahyate pretabhūmiṣu ।।
rājā bhavati dānena cakravartī sudhārmikaḥ । dānabhūmiṃ samāśritya śīlaṃ rakṣanti paṇḍitāḥ ।। śīlavānapi kālajño ajñānād parimucyate । duḥkhanairyāṇiko mārgaḥ śasto ayaṃ munipuṃgavaiḥ ।।
taṃ viditvā mahāvīro nityaṃ dānarato bhavet । adā dapi deveṣu devā hi na sukhā matāḥ ।। ājanmavipine martyā bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ । dānasya tatphalaṃ sarvacetanābhāvitasya hi ।।
tiryakṣvapi samutpannā bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ । tatsarva dānajaṃ saukhyaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। yat pretāḥ pretabhavane bhavatyākārabhojinaḥ । svayaṃ kṛtasya dānasya phalaṃ bhavati tādṛśam ।।
dadyāt kṣutpipāse ca dahyante yena dehinaḥ । sarvadā na tapastābhyāṃ phalaṃ bhavati śītalam ।। pūrva pramādacārī yo na dānādiṣu vartate । sa paścānmṛtyusamaye dahyate svena cetasā ।।
priyo bhavati dānena cetasāmapi tuṣyati । paścād bhavati sa śrīmān dānasya phalamīdṛśam ।। yatra dānādi cittasyāstyupabhogāya sarvadā । tatra nirdhanataiṣā vā dayayā parirakṣitam ।।
yad bhujyate sadā cittaṃ gurubhyaścāpi dīyate । yad vanaṃ śobhanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ viparītaṃ yathā tṛṇam ।। durbalānāṃ sadārtānāṃ sattvānāṃ cakṣuranvitam । dānaṃ niḥkalpasaṃyantramasmiṃlloke paratra ca ।।
manuṣyabhūmau dānāni dattvā yānti śubhāṃ gatim । na devā dānapatayaḥ phalabhūmirasau matā ।। karmabhūmirmanuṣyāṇāṃ phalabhūmiḥ surālayaḥ । karmāyattaṃ phalaṃ sarva na phalaṃ syādahetukam ।।
dhyānādhyayananirmukto dānaśīlavivarjitaḥ । suvarṇakaṃkaṇairyukto jīvannapi mṛtaiḥ samaḥ ।। sa jīvati hi loke asmin yo dharmamanuvartate । dharmamūḍhaḥ sadā mūḍho jīvannapi mṛtaiḥ samaḥ ।।
manuṣyacarmaṇā channastiryag bhavati bāliśaḥ । yasya jñānapradīpena hṛdayaṃ nāvabhāsitam ।। bhavatyetāvatā puruṣaḥ yaḥ śīlamanuvartate । śīlabhraṣṭaḥ pumān sarvaścābhistutyo aparākramaḥ ।।
dānahīnaḥ pramādī pāpacārī calendriyaḥ । nāsau martya iti jñeyaḥ preto vigrahavānayam ।। jñānaśīlavinirmukto dānaratnavivarjitaḥ । jīvamāno api puruṣo mṛta ityabhidhīyate ।।
dānaśīlatapodhyānād vīryasmṛtisamādhimān । puruṣaḥ puruṣaireje devairapi sa vandyate ।। guṇavāṃstu naro vandyaḥ nirguṇaḥ paśubhiḥ samaḥ । guṇāguṇavidhijño yaḥ sa deva iti kathyate ।।
sujīvitaṃ bhavettasya yasya tyāge sthitaṃ manaḥ । nahi tyāgavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvanaṃ matam ।। pañcagatyupapannānāṃ sattvānāṃ svena karmaṇā । mātṛvat pitṛvad dṛṣṭaṃ dānaṃ nityaṃ sukhāvaham ।।
etāṃ bhūmimavasthāpya sattvo dānarato bhavet । dānaśīlaratā nityaṃ mucyante bhavasaṅkaṭāt ।। ।। iti dānavargo dvāviṃśaḥ ।। dhanānāmuttamaṃ śīlaṃ sūryo jyotiṣmatāmiva ।
vihāya gacchati dhanaṃ śīlaṃ sthitamivāgrataḥ ।। śīlena tridaśān yāti dhyānagocarameva vā । nāsti śīlasamaṃ jyotirasmiṃlloke paratra ca ।। alpena hetunā svarga prāpnoti svargakāmikaḥ ।
tasmād duścaritaṃ hitvā nityaṃ sucarito bhavet ।। cetanābhāvitaṃ dānaṃ śīlaṃ ca parirakṣitam । nīyate devasandattaṃ pañcakāmaguṇānvitam ।। na mātā na pitā nārthā dayitā nāpi bāndhavāḥ ।
na sukhā tathā dṛṣṭā yathā śīlaṃ surakṣitam ।। śīlaṃ trāṇamihāmutra śīlaṃ gatirihottamam । śīlavān puruṣo nityaṃ sukhāt sukhamavāpnute ।। dānaśīlasamācārā ye narā śubhacāriṇaḥ ।
te yānti devasadanaṃ racitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।। nidhānamavyayaṃ śīlaṃ śīlasaukhyamatarkitam । śīlādhikā hi puruṣā nityaṃ sukhavihāriṇaḥ ।। śīlaṃ rakṣatu medhāvī yathā yānaṃ sukhatrayam ।
praśaṃsāvṛttalābhaṃ ca pretya svarge ca modate ।। śīlavān yo hi puruṣaḥ śīlamevāti sevate । sasukho nirvṛttiṃ yāti yatra mṛtyurna vidyate ।। anādimati saṃsāre tṛṣṇāmohādibhirvṛte ।
jyotirbhūta sadāśīlaṃ tasmācchīlamanāvilam ।। śīlaṃ dhanamasaṃhārya rājacaurodakādibhiḥ । tasmācchīlaṃ sadā sevyaṃ dauḥśīlyaṃ ca vigarhitam ।। śīlābhiratapuruṣaḥ nirvāṇaṃ hyantike sthitam ।
śīlavān puruṣo dhanyaḥ śīlavāṃścāpi sevyate ।। ravivad bhrājate śīlaṃ dauḥśīlyaṃ caiva garhitam । nirmalaṃ vītakāntāraṃ nirjvaraṃ vītakāṅkṣi ca ।। śīlapraśastasambuddhairnirvāṇapuragāmikam ।
āyuryāti dhruvaṃ dhīmān nityaṃ śīlenaṃ vṛṃhitam ।। na bibhenmṛtyukāle ca śīlena parirakṣitaḥ । śīlamādyantakalyāṇaṃ sarvasaukhyapravartakam । śīlavān puruṣo dhanyo dauḥśīlyābhirataḥ paśuḥ ।।
tīraṃ naiva samāyānti puruṣāḥ śīlavarjitāḥ । kāryākārya na vindanti tasmācchīlaṃ samācaret ।। śīlavastreṇa ye channāste channāḥ puruṣā matāḥ । śīlena varjitā ye tu nagnāste paśubhiḥ samāḥ ।।
śīlavān puruṣaḥ svagamudyānamiva gacchati । bandhuvanmanyate tatra śīlavān pramāgataḥ ।। śuciśīlasamācārāḥ śubhadharmasamanvitāḥ । devalokopagāsteṣu janāḥ sukṛtakāriṇaḥ ।।
yo na prārthayate kāmān śīlavān puruṣaḥ sadā । guṇāstasya pravardhante śīlena paribṛṃhitāḥ ।। mahārghamuttamaṃ śīlamasmiṃlloke paratra ca । tasmāt prahāya traiguṇyaṃ śīlameva sadā caret ।।
devebhyo rocate taddhi trāṇaṃ śīlaṃ śubhānvitam । bhāvitaṃ paramaṃ dhanyaṃ paralokopagāmikam ।। śīlavān yadi jānīyāt phalaṃ śīlasya yādṛśam ।। śastraṃ sutīkṣṇamādāya vāṇaṃ chindyādihātmanaḥ ।
astropamasya nindyasya abhisaukhyasamanvitam ।। phalaṃ śīlasya vimalaṃ sugatena pradarśitam । ādau śastaṃ tathā madhye nidhane śastameva tat ।। phalaṃ śīlasya vipulaṃ sukhāt sukhamuttamam ।
śīlacaryā paraṃ saukhyaṃ dhanacaryā na tādṛśī ।। narā dhanena hīyante śīlena na kathañcana । śocate puruṣastena pṛthak vā tadvirājate ।। śubhaṃ tasmānmunivaraiḥ praśastaṃ sārvagāmikam ।
udyānamiva gacchanti puruṣāḥ śubhacāriṇaḥ । devalokasamaṃ teṣāṃ saukhyānāmākaraṃ ।। suśīlitasya śīlasya bhakṣitasyāpyanekaśaḥ । phalaṃ vipacyate svargastasmācchīlaṃ samācaret ।।
śīlaṃ svargasya sopānamākaraṃ sukhanirvṛte । śīlavarjī hi puruṣo na kvacit sukhamedhate ।। śīlāmbhasā prasannena viprakīrṇena sarvadā । snātvā gacchanti puruṣā devaloke ca nirvṛte ।
yaddivyamālyābharaṇairdivyaiḥ saukhyaiḥ samanvitāḥ ।। ramate devabhavane tat sarva śubhahetukam । asaṃkhyāni ca saukhyāni vardhamānāni sarvadā ।। labhate puruṣaḥ sarva yaḥ śīlamanuvartate ।
śubhacārī sadā satyaḥ pūjyate so aparājitaḥ ।। śubhena śobhate martyaḥ pūjyate rājabhiḥ sadā । śubhena śobhate martyastasmācchīlaṃ samācaret ।। anekasaukhyajanakaṃ sarvamāśvāsakārakam ।
śīlaṃ sucaritaṃ kārya duṣkṛtaṃ ca vivarjayet ।। ye dānaśīlakarttāraḥ svargatadgatamānasāḥ । teṣāṃ sakalmaṣaṃ śīlaṃ viṣamiśraṃ yathaudanam ।। nānāvidhasya śīlasya rakṣitasyāpyanekaśaḥ ।
