śubhakāryavipākāya deveṣu paripacyate ।। śīlāmbhasā prasanneṣu saṅkīrṇeṣu ca sarvadā । snātvā gacchanti manujā devāṃścātyantikaṃ sukham ।। dānaśīlāḥ sadā dāntāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।
jñānayuktā maitracitā gatāste devasammitim ।। hatadoṣāḥ kriyāvantaḥ śīlaratnena bhūṣitāḥ । sarvasattvadayāvantaḥ suralokeṣu te budhāḥ ।। viśuddhakāñcanaprakhyā nirdhmātamalakalmaṣāḥ ।
samyak karma susaṃlagnā devalokeṣu te budhāḥ ।। sarvasattvadayāvantaḥ sarvasattvahitaiṣiṇaḥ । sarvapāpaviraktā ye teṣāṃ vāsaḥ surālaye ।। ahanyahani ye śīlaṃ rakṣanti suparīkṣakāḥ ।
ahanyahani teṣāṃ hi sukhaṃ bhavati naikaśaḥ ।। śīlavājinamārūḍhāḥ puruṣāstattvacintakāḥ । prayānti devabhavanaṃ krīḍāyuktamanekaśaḥ ।। yā krīḍā devabhavane yacca saukhyamanuttamam ।
tat samagrasya śīlasya phalamuktaṃ tathāgataiḥ ।। yaddivyamālyābharaṇā divyāmbaravibhūṣitāḥ । krīḍanti vibudhāḥ sarve tatsarva śubhahetukam ।। padmotpalavane ramye vanopavanabhūṣite ।
svarge ramanti ye devāstat sarva śubhajaṃ phalam ।। yadākāśa ivātasthurdivyaratnavibhūṣitāḥ । virājante amalā devāstacchīlasya mahat phalam ।। yatkānaneṣu ramyeṣu citreṣu puṣpiteṣu ca ।
ramanti giripṛṣṭheṣu surāstacchīlajaṃ phalam ।। svagṛhaṃ hi yathā martyāḥ praviśanti gatavyathāḥ । tathā śīlasamācārāḥ prayānti tridivaṃ narāḥ ।। etat sujīvitaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ yacchīlaparirakṣaṇam ।
maraṇānāṃ paraṃ mṛtyuḥ yacchīlaparivarjanam ।। etān guṇān sadā matvā priyatvamapi cātmanaḥ । śīlaṃ surakṣitaṃ kārya dauḥśīlyaṃ ca vivarjayet ।। śīlacārī sadā dāntaḥ kṣamāvāṃśca sudarśanaḥ ।
sopānamiva cārūḍhaṃ prayātyānandasannidhim ।। phalaṃ śīlasya tu sukhaṃ devalokeṣu pacyate । śīlena plavabhūtena saṃsārāduttaranti ca ।। śīlāmbhasā viśuddhā ye svāyattā dhīracetasaḥ ।
jāmbūnadamayaiḥ puṣpaiste atrārcanti divaukasaḥ ।। ye navādātamanaso nityaṃ śīlena bhūṣitāḥ । te yānti devasadanaṃ yatra saukhyamanantakam ।। saukhyāt saukhyataraṃ yānti narāḥ sukṛtakāriṇaḥ ।
krīḍanti devasadane śīlena paribṛṃhitāḥ ।। śīlasopānamāruhya jñānena paribṛṃhitāḥ । narāḥ prayānti sugatiṃ jñānena ca parāyaṇā ।। suprasannena manasāśīlaṃ yadabhirakṣitam ।
tasya śīlasya śītasva sukhametadupasthitam ।। surakṣitasya śīlasya bhāvitasyāpyanekaśaḥ । pariṇāme sukhībhūtvā nirvāṇaṃ cādhigacchati ।। śīlaṃ rakṣatyupāyena śīlaṃ nayati saṅgatim ।
tasmācchīlaṃ sadā rakṣyaṃ pariṇāmo asya śītalaḥ ।। mṛtyukāle samutpanne śīlavānakutobhayaḥ । na me durgatinā trāṇaṃ śīlaṃ hi trāṇamuttamam ।। kācābhrapaṭalaṃ yasya śīlaṃ bhavati kutsitam ।
sa kutsitena śīlena kutsito jāyate naraḥ ।। śīlamūlena labdhvedaṃ sukhaṃ svargeṣu dehibhiḥ । tṛṣṇākṣayo na bhavati sa paścāt paritapyate ।। tasmācchīlavatā nityaṃ śīlameva viśiṣyate ।
niḥśīlaḥ puruṣo mūḍho na svargamadhirohati ।। pañcakāmopamaṃ divyaṃ yadidaṃ bhujyate sukham । tacchīlasya viśuddhasya prāpyate hi phalaṃ mahat ।। yattejaḥ kāñcanasyāsya meruparvataśālinaḥ ।
tacchīlatejasastejaḥ kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm ।। dīpyamānaiḥ sadā śīlaiḥ nirdhātukanakatviṣā । saṃyuktāstridivaṃ yānti paṇḍitā svena karmaṇā ।। hīnamadhyaviśiṣṭasya śīlasya trividhasya vai ।
phalaṃ hi trividhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hīnamadhyottamaṃ tathā ।। pramādarahitaṃ śīlamapramādopabṛṃhitam । nityaṃ tat sukhadaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ dharmateyaṃ vyavasthitā ।। śīlodbhavā yā vimalā prabhā bhavati dehinām ।
na sā sūryasahastrasya saṃyuktasya bhaviṣyati ।। śīlaṃ saptavidhaṃ ramyaṃ yo rakṣati narottamaḥ । sa kāmaṃ bhuñjati phalaṃ sugatena ca deśitam ।। śīlacaryā samāśritya samyagdarśanatatparaḥ ।
martyalokād divaṃ yānti na kaṣṭaṃ tapacāriṇaḥ ।। yacchīlaṃ śīlasaṃsparśa pariṇāme api śītalam । niṣevate sadāmūḍhaḥ sa paścāt paritapyate ।। śīlaṃ saptavidhaṃ dhanyamavisaṃvādakaṃ padam ।
śīlena rakṣitaḥ puruṣo devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ ।। yathā pakṣairdṛḍhaiḥ pakṣī svedacchatraṃ nihanti । tathā naro dṛḍhaḥ śīlairdevalokāya kalpyate ।। śrutimātraṃ ca ramyād ramyataraṃ ca tat ।
labhate puruṣaḥ kartā phalaṃ śīlasya śobhanam ।। dānaśīlataporatnaṃ hṛdayaiśca samāśritam । devatā vā manuṣyo vā labhate paramaṃ padam ।। antarbahiśca niḥsārāḥ puruṣā dharmavarjitāḥ ।
saṃsārāt phalakāṅkṣibhyaḥ saddharmo na rocate ।। antarbahiśca ye sārāste narā vastuto dṛḍhāḥ । ye dharmacāriṇaḥ śāntāḥ parasattvahitaiṣiṇaḥ ।। na ketakī campakapuṣpagandhā, tamālake nāgarucaśca gandhaḥ ।
prayānti gandhā hiṃ yathā sureṇa, anuttaraḥ śīlavatāṃ sugandhaḥ ।। tasmācchīlaṃ sadā kārya dānajñānatapodhanaiḥ । dauḥśīlyaṃ ca sadā varjyaviṣaśastrānalopanam ।। evaṃ surakṣitaṃ śīlaṃ narān nayati saṅgatim ।
na hi śīlādṛte kaścit padaṃ sukhamavāpnute ।। tasmād devaguṇaṃ matvā śīlameva sadācaret । na śīlasadṛśaṃ kiñcidanyat trāṇamihāsti vai ।। ।। iti śīlavargastrayoviṃśaḥ ।।
kṣāntyā vibhūṣitaḥ jīva bhūṣito netarairdhanaiḥ । dhanaṃ vinā samāyāti kṣāntiṃ naiva kathañcana ।। kṣamāvān puruṣaḥ sarvapriyo bhavati dehinām । pūjyate daivatairnityaṃ tasmāt kṣāntiḥ parantapa ! ।।
kṣamāvān puruṣaḥ sarvaiḥ krodhadoṣairvivarjitaḥ । yaśasā pūjyate nityamiha loke paratra ca ।। kṣāntirdhanaṃ dhanaṃ śīlaprajñāvardhanameva ca । dhanānyanyāni śastāni na hitasya kathañcana ।।
pūjyate satataṃ sadbhiryaśasā caiva pūjyate । kṣamāvān puruṣaḥ sarvastamāt kṣāntiparo bhavet ।। kṣāntiḥ krodhaviṣasyāsya bheṣajaṃ paramaṃ matam । kṣāntyāvināśitaḥ krodho anarthāyopajāyate ।।
jñānaśīlābhibhūtānāṃ bāliśānāṃ viśeṣataḥ । pratīpakārya kurute kṣāntirmārganidarśikā ।। sa dharmadhanahīnānāṃ bhramatāṃ gatipañcake । yeṣāṃ kṣāntimayaṃ dravyaṃ te loke dhaninaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
tamonicayakāntāre dṛḍhakrodhena dustare । kṣāntyā yathā smṛtāḥ sadbhistaranti khula mānavāḥ ।। saddharmapāṭhanaṣṭānāṃ deśikā kṣāntiruttamā । apāyabhayabhītānāṃ na bhayaṃ kṣāntirucyate ।।
sukhāvahā sadā nṛṇāṃ duḥkhasya ca vighātikā । kṣemasamprāpikā nityaṃ viśvāsaguṇakārikā ।। śubhāsti nāyikā dhanyā hyaśubhebhyo vivarjitā । mokṣasaṃdeśikā puṃsāṃ saṃsārabhayanāśikā ।।
svargasopānabhūtā sā narakāgnivināśikā । trāyate pretalokātsā tiryagyonau tathaiva ca ।। sā guṇaudhaiḥ sadā pūrṇā śivā bhavati dehinām । sā praśaste sukhe prāpte kṣāntiḥ kāryā prayatnataḥ ।
sarvalokasya māteva sanmārgāmṛtadīpikā ।। ।। iti kṣāntivargaścaturviṃśaḥ ।। deśakālopapannasya kriyātithyocitasya ca । nyāyenārabhyamāṇasya vīryasya sakalaṃ phalam ।।
nyāyadeśakriyāhīnā adharmeṇa vivarjitāḥ । sīdanti kāryanikarā vīryeṇa parivarjitāḥ ।। dhyānenārabdhavīryeṇa mokṣaṃ gacchanti paṇḍitāḥ । bhavakṣipta ivākāro devaloke prayānti ca ।।
yānyārabdhāni kāryāṇi vīryavad balinā nṛṇā । tāni tāni prasiddhāni vipulāni bhavanti ca ।। ye arthā lokottare siddhā ye ca lokeṣu sammatāḥ । te vīryeṇa prasādhyante vīryahīnā na jātu vai ।।
mandavīrya cirotsāhaṃ saddharmeṇa vivarjitam । naro viśati lokaṃ śaśāṅkamiva kalmaṣam ।। āryāṣṭāṅgena mārgeṇa na jñānaparipālitaḥ । vīryavattāmahotsāho prayāti paramāṃ gatim ।।
vīryaṇāvāpyate bodhiḥ svavīryeṇa tathā mahī । arhattvaṃ vīryavadbhiśca tasmānnāgnisamā gatiḥ ।। tasmād devān guṇān matvā vīryavān niyatendriyaḥ । vīryārambhe matiṃ kuryārnnāsti vīryasamarthanam ।।
vīryārthī smṛtimān yaśca naro jñānaparāyaṇaḥ । prayātyanuttamaṃ sthānaṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitam ।। ।। iti vīryavargaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ ।। asaṃsaktamaternityaṃ nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ ।
viśuddhamanaso nityamekāgrabhiratasya ca ।। yasyaikāgrakaraṃ cittaṃ tasya doṣā na bādhakāḥ । sa doṣabhayanirmuktaḥ svastha ityabhidhīyate ।। ekāgrābhiratañceto vivekamanudhāvati ।
sarvatarkavinirmuktaḥ svastha ityabhidhīyate ।। yasya cittaṃ dhruvaṃ śāntaṃ nirvāṇābhirataṃ sadā । na tasyendriyajā doṣā bhavasya śubhahetavaḥ ।। yacca dhyānakṛtaṃ saukhyaṃ yacca samādhijam ।
cittaṃ tatsarvamekāgramate bhavati dehinaḥ ।। ekārāmasya yatino yat sukhaṃ jāyate hṛdi । yat saukhyamativijñeyaṃ na saukhyaṃ laukikaṃ matam ।। ekāgrābhirataṃ cittaṃ viśuddhākṛtameva ca ।
doṣajālavinirmuktaṃ śāntiṃ samadhigacchati ।। ekāntamanasā nityaṃ saṃkṣiptendriyapañcakaiḥ । tṛṣṇāgninātivṛddhaṃ ca hanti jñānāmbhasā budhaḥ ।। tasya tṛṣṇāvimuktasya viśuddhasya sukhaiṣiṇaḥ ।
akṣayaṃ cāvyayaṃ caiva padaṃ hi sthitamagrataḥ ।। vitarkakuṭilaṃ ceto yatra yatropapadyate । ekālambanayuktena dhārya tena samādhinā । tasmādetat paraṃ vartma nirvāṇapuragāmikam ।।
etadagraṃ manaḥ kṣutvā hanyādarisamūhakam । mano hīdaṃ vinirgṛhya vetti dhyānajairdṛḍhaiḥ ।। । prayānti paramaṃ sthānamaśokaṃ hatakilviṣam ।।
nirviṣaskasya tuṣṭasya nirāgasyāpi dhīmataḥ yat sukhaṃ dhyānajaṃ bhāti kutastasyopamā parā ।। etatsāraṃ sudhīrāṇāṃ yogināṃ pāragāminām । yadevedaṃ manaḥ śrutvā prayānti padamacyutam ।। ।। iti dhyānavargaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ ।।
dharmānusāriṇī prajñā vīryeṇa parivṛṃhitā । samādhibalasaṃyuktā māteva hitakāriṇī ।। sā hi santrāyate sarvān puruṣān gatipañcakāt । na mātā na pitā tatra gacchantamanugacchati ।।
prajñāśikharamāruhya śīlakandaraśobhanam । bhavadoṣamidaṃ sarva paśyati bhūṣaṇaḥ ।। indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyo yadā vindanti tatpadam । tadā samādhinā jñāna bhavasāgaramuttaret ।।
dānaśīlatapodhyānairjñānamevāgramucyate । apavargād yadā jñānaṃ jñānaśīle sukhāvahe ।। cakṣuṣāṃ ca parā dṛṣṭā prajñoktā sunirmalā । mārgāṇāṃ cāṣṭamo mārgaḥ śivaḥ proktastathāgataiḥ ।।
caturṇā caiva satyānāmagre dve tu prakīrtite । bālānāṃ ca sadā dṛṣṭaṃ prajñābalamihottamam ।। jñānaśastreṇa tikṣṇena latā chedyā durāsadā । hantavyā doṣanivahāśchettavyā janmapaddhatiḥ ।।
amṛtānāṃ paraṃ jñānaṃ śreyasāṃ nidhiruttamam । na jñānācca paraṃ bandhurna jñānāddhanamuttamam ।। jñānaśīlayutāvṛddhā vītarāgā gataspṛhāḥ । sevitavyāḥ sadā santastattvamārganidarśakāḥ ।।
prajñāvajreṇa tīkṣṇena mahodayavasena ca । mahāyogarathārūḍhaḥ kleśādīn pravidārayet ।। ।। iti prajñāvargaḥ saptaviṃśaḥ ।। kleśakṣayāt paraṃ saukhyaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
eṣa nirvāṇago mārgaḥ kathitastattvadarśakaiḥ ।। tatpadaṃ śāśvataṃ juṣṭaṃ kathayanti tathāgatāḥ । yatra janma na mṛtyurna vidyate duḥkhasambhavaḥ ।। vibhūtasyāpramattasya śāntasya vanacāriṇaḥ ।
alolupasya vīrasya nirvāṇasya vibhūtayaḥ ।। mitrāmitraprahīṇasya bhavarāgavivarjinaḥ । viṣayeṣvapramattasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।। śubhakāryeṣu saktasya maitrīkāruṇyabhāvinaḥ ।
saṃsārabhayabhītasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।। kleśakṣayavidhijñasya nairātmyasyāpi tasya ca । kausīdyāccaiva muktasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।। catuḥsatyavidhijñasya tridoṣavadhasevinaḥ ।
vaśyendriyasya śāntasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।। sukhaduḥkhamayaiḥ pāśairyasya ceto na hanyate । sa doṣabhayanirmuktaḥ pārago munirucyate ।। puruṣo apāyabhīruśca pramādabalavarjakaḥ ।
śubhakārī śubhānveṣī nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।। ।। iti nirvāṇavargo aṣṭāviṃśaḥ ।। satyāni catvāri śivāni tāni, subhāvitānyeva samīkṣya vidvān । sucintako jātijarābhayebhyaḥ, pramucyaye pāramupaiti śāntaḥ ।।
acintako yastu vibhūtabuddhiḥ kāmeṣu sakto bhavabhogabaddhaḥ । sa bandhanaiḥ kāmamayairnibaddho, na mucyate jātijarābhayebhyaḥ ।। vicintya yo duḥkhamidaṃ viśālaṃ, na khedamāyāti bhavārṇavebhyaḥ । sa kāmavāṇairnihato hi mūḍhaḥ, kaṣṭāmavasthāṃ narake api yāti ।।
ābhyantaraṃ kṣemasukhaṃ ca hitvā, kiṃ kāmabhogābhiratā hi bālāḥ । naite bijānanti bhayaṃ ca tīvramabhyeti mṛtyurjvalanaprakāśaḥ ।। anityaduḥkhaśūnyo ayamātmā kārakavarjitaḥ । saṃsāraḥ kathito buddhaiḥ tattvamārgapradarśakaiḥ ।।
tena sarvamidaṃ tattvajñānaṃ jñeyaṃ samāsataḥ । jñānajñeyavinirmuktaṃ tṛtīyaṃ nopalabhyate ।। antapāravidhijño yaḥ ṣoḍaśākāratattvavit । ūrdhvagatividhijño hi kṣāntitattvavicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
agralokaikadharmajñaḥ samanantaratattvavit । sa dharmatāmanuviśed yathā na vikampate ।। dvayopāyavinirmukto naṣṭān nāśayate muhuḥ । naṣṭapāpagatirvīraḥ strotāpanno nirucyate ।।
srotāṃsya kuśalā dharmā jīryante pāpagāminaḥ । mokṣāgninā pratapyante srotāpanno bhavatyataḥ ।। prasrabdhijaṃ mahodarkamuktaṃ saṃsāramokṣakam । tṛṣṇākṣayasukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ satyataḥ sukhakārakam ।।
nāvabadhnāti yaṃ tṛṣṇā na vitarkairvihasyate । samprāptabhavapārastu sukhī bhavati sarvadā ।। anyonyaphalasambhūta sarvataḥ sampravartate । tadeva kāraṇaṃ jñeyamāryamārgacatuṣṭayam ।।
āryasatyeṣu viditaḥ puruṣo vidyate dhruvam । viṣayeṣu hi saṃghuṣṭaṃ jagad bhramati cakravat ।। sa mārgo deśakaḥ śreṣṭho yo mārgo bhāṣitaḥ śivaḥ । yena mārgeṇa prācīnā yātā manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya buddhau sthitaṃ manaḥ । nahi buddhivinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।। sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya dharme sthitaṃ manaḥ । nahi dharmavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।।
sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya saṅghe sthitaṃ manaḥ । nahi saṅghavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।। sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya satye sthitaṃ manaḥ । nahi satyavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।।
sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya mārge sthitaṃ manaḥ । nahi mārgavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।। nirvāṇagamane yasya nityaṃ buddhiravasthitā । sa doṣādeva nirmukto na devaḥ krīḍati svayam ।।
yā bhavavyāpinī krīḍā nityamekāgracetasaḥ । sā sukhodbhāvikā krīḍā na krīḍā rāgakārikā ।। sukhādīniha satyāni yathā dāntena vindati । tadā kṣemaṃ śivaṃ sthānaṃ prāpnoti puruṣottamaḥ ।।
।। iti mārgavarga ekonatriṃśaḥ ।। yo hinasti na bhūtāni mitravettā sadākṣayaḥ । pitṛvat sarvabhūtāni lokastamanupaśyati ।। adattādānavirato nityaṃ jñānī jitendriyaḥ ।
praśāntadehakarmā tīrṇasambhavasaṅkramaḥ ।। nāpyālekhyagatā nāpi cakṣuṣā sā nirīkṣyate । hatakāmo dṛṣṭasatyo muktastādṛśa ucyate ।। samaloṣṭāśmakanakaḥ vītaśokaḥ samāhitaḥ ।
na kleśoragasampṛktaḥ sa saukhyaṃ dhruvamāpnuyāt ।। arthānarthasamo yasya lābhālābhau tathaiva ca । sukhaduḥkhasamāyuktaḥ bhikṣuḥ sa khalu kathyate ।। mitrāmitraprahīṇo yaḥ samacetā jitendriyaḥ ।
vibheti yo na viṣayaiḥ vijñeyastādṛśo yatiḥ ।। viṣamatvāddhi viṣayān dveṣṭi dhīro gatavyathaḥ । na tasya dūre nirvāṇaṃ samyaksambuddhadeśitam ।। udayavyayatattvajñaḥ samyagdṛṣṭiralolupaḥ ।
himavāniva niṣkramya saṃsārānmuktahetukaḥ ।। tṛṇacandanatulyo hi samatṛṣṇāmbarāśinaḥ । sa kauśeyasaṅghaṭitatṛṣṇayā naiva bādhate ।। lābhasatkārasantuṣṭaḥ santuṣṭastṛṇasaṃstaraiḥ ।
vahnivallābhasatkāraṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।। vāhyate yo na viṣayaistṛṇanadyā na vāhayate । svakarmaphalatattvajñaḥ sa bhikṣurbuddhadeśitaḥ ।। nātītaṃ śocate yo hi buddhayā gataspṛhaḥ ।
pratyutpannakriyāyogī na buddhistasya lipyate ।। nirvāṇe matiryasya dharme nityaṃ sthitā bhavet । na vartate sa saṃsāre śukladharmasamāvṛtaḥ ।। nāvilaṃ kriyate yasya cittaṃ vidyāgnikalpayā ।
dāruvadviṣayā yasya tasya duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।। indriyāṇi vaśe yasya cendriyeṣu vaśānugaḥ । hriyate yaḥ pumarthaino nikaṣastādṛśo muniḥ ।। sādhuvaddhimano yasya kṣamāvān priyadarśanaḥ ।
prahlādayati cetāṃsi sa nṛṇāṃ śaśivanmuniḥ ।। aruṇābhirato yastu harmyāgreṣu na rajyati । santuṣṭaḥ pāṃśukūlena bhikṣurbhikṣārato bhavet ।। śānto dāntaḥ sudhīrarthāt tattvavit sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।
sa yātyuttamamadhvānaṃ yatra gatvā na śocati ।। ṛjumatpātakānyasya nityaṃ dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ । prākṛtaiśca malai sa yogī satyavartmani ।। sarvendriyavighātī yaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।
śānto dāntendriyaḥ svastho bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। ṣaḍindriyarathārūḍho rāgaśatrunivārakaḥ । prajñādhīraḥ kriyāvān yaḥ sa śāntipadamaśnute ।। araṇyavāsī santuṣṭo bhūmivāsī samāhitaḥ ।
dhunāti pāpako dharmaścāyurmeghānivāmbaraḥ ।। śubhaṃ vā dehakarmāntaḥ śubhacaryāsu saṃrataḥ । tattvadṛṣṭiḥ kriyādakṣo nāśayanmārasādhanam ।। rāgātyaye na bādheta śubhacittaṃ gatālayam ।
maitryā kāruṇyabahulo bhikṣurnairyyāṇike sthitaḥ ।। yasya rūpādayo neṣṭā viṣayā bandhahetave । sa yāti paramāṃ śāntiṃ yatra gatvā na śocyate ।। hetupratyayatattvajñaḥ sūkṣmārthe kṛtaniścayaḥ ।
mokṣasrotasyabhiratastṛṣṇayā naiva rajyate ।। yo nādatte aśubhaṃ karma śubhakarmarataḥ sadā । candrāṃśunirmalagatiryogī bhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। pradahan pāpakān dharmān śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।
vibhrājate tribhuvane muktapāyo gatavyathaḥ ।। mokṣe asti yasya tu mano na saṃsāre kathañcana । nāsau badhnāti saṃsāre muktaḥ pakṣī yathāmbare ।। vedanodayatattvajño vedanāphalaniścayaḥ ।
sa mukta iti vijñeyastattvavid ṛtavāṃśca saḥ ।। tathāpyete sukhaduḥkhe mṛṣṭāmṛṣṭairna lipyate । dīptaṃ paśyati saṃsāraṃ yaḥ sa yogī satāṃ mataḥ ।। athāmūḍhamatirnityaṃ nityaṃ dharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।
bhikṣuvṛttāvabhirato bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। na tṛptirdarśanārāmaiḥ sādhūnāṃ darśane ratiḥ । niṣkrāntagṛhakalmāṣo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। na nṛtyagītasandarśī ca punarīkṣate ।
saṃrakṣito śmaśāneṣu bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। ekāhaṃ paramaṃ piṇḍamādatte anyatra kāṅkṣati । tribhāgakukṣisantuṣṭo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। vastrottamavivarjī yaḥ pāṃsukūleṣu rajyate ।
muktāhāravihāro yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। karmāṇyārabhate yo na nirāśaḥ sa ca karmasu । niruddhako noparato bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। kāyakoṭivinirmukto mohadhvāntavivarjitaḥ ।
aliptaḥ pāpakairdharmaibhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। sarvāśayajanānītaḥ sarvāśayavivarjitaḥ । sarvāśayavinirmukto bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। āryāṣṭāṅgena mārgeṇa nirvāṇapurataḥ sthitaḥ ।
sarvārthadharmatā hyeṣā bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। śāntendriyo dṛḍhamatiḥ kāmapākavivarjitaḥ । ekāgrasaṃsthitamanā bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। bhūmisaṅkramaṇajño yo bhūmitattvanidarśakaḥ ।
bhūmeḥ parāparajño yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। sambhavāsambhavān dharmān hetupratyayasambhavān । jānīte vidhivat sarvān bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। brahmacārī ṛtujñānī styānamiddhavivarjitaḥ ।
kalpodagro avanau dakṣo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। śamasthovipaśyanāśca caturdhyānarataśca yaḥ । ālaye muditārāmo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। pakṣiṇo gaganasthasya chāyevānugataḥ sadā ।
saddharmasyānujīvī sa bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। kleśopakleśabadhakaḥ samadarśī śubhānvitaḥ । anāpānavidhijño yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। anukramavidhijño yo yogavit tattvadarśakaḥ ।
pārāpāravidhijño yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। yo na hṛṣyati harṣeṣu bhayeṣu na bibheti ca । mukto harṣabhayodvegairbhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। janmamaraṇatattvajñaḥ surāsuranamaskṛtaḥ ।
parāvarajñaḥ sattvānāṃ bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। saṅghāṭimātrasaṃhṛṣṭaḥ sañcayeṣu na rajyate । alpeccho brahmacārī yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। ekāśī vṛkṣamūle yaḥ sadā dhyānaṃ samīhate ।
lābhasatkāravirato bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। upekṣākaruṇārāgo mokṣadoṣavivarjitaḥ । nirdagdhadoṣasarvasvo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। mandavīryakusīdānāṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ darśanāya ca ।
nānyayogābhirakto yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। na śayyāsanasambhogī bhikṣurbuddhena bhāṣitaḥ । kausīdyabhirato yastu nāsau kalyāṇamarhati ।। kleśānāṃ mūlapākaṃ hi kausīdyaṃ yasya vidyate ।
tasya duḥkhaṃ mahāghoraṃ saṃsāre sampravartate ।। kausīdyameva yasyāsti tasya dharmo na vidyate । kevalaṃ vastramātreṇa abhikṣuḥ' sa iti kathyate ।। nādhyāpane ratiryasya na dhyānenāśu rakṣati ।
kevalaṃ vastumātreṇa bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। vihārābhirato yastu na rato dharmagocare । strīmadyalolupamatibhikṣurasti na tādṛśaḥ ।। pāpakarmaṇi ।
sa bhikṣurdeśito buddhaiḥ na bhoktā svakagocare ।। varamāśīviṣaviṣaṃ kathitaṃ tāmrameva ca । bhuktasyātyantaduḥśīlairadhikaṃ pāpabhojanam ।। yo hi nārhati piṇḍāya nāsau piṇḍāya kalpate ।
yasya piṇḍikṛtāḥ kleśāḥ sarpā iva vileśayāḥ ।। sa bhikṣuḥ piṇḍabhojī syānna strīdarśanatatparaḥ । bandhakaṃ yadi cātmānaṃ kṛtvā paraśubhakṣatim ।। kathaṃ sa bhikṣurvijñeyaḥ saṅgharatnapradūṣakaḥ ।
yasyeṣṭā lābhasatkārā viṣayā yasya sammatāḥ ।। nāridarśanasākāṅkṣī na bhikṣurna gṛhīva saḥ । rājaseviṣu sṛṣṭāśo madyapaḥ krodhanastathā ।। sadā bhikṣurbañcayate dāyakānnanu cetasā ।
upāyanānyupādāya rājadvārāśritā hi ye । saṃrabdhā gṛhibhiḥ sārdha yathā nāgā vanāśritāḥ ।। tasmāt tāneva puṣṇanti vāterṣyāste samāgatāḥ । putradārān parityajya ye śāntā ratnamāśritāḥ ।।
prahāya doṣān yo bhikṣurasti darśanatattvavit । rūpādiskandhatattvajño mokṣāya yatate sadā ।। dharmāvabodhābhirato dhyānārāmavihāravān tattvalakṣaṇasambodhāt prāpnuyāt padamavyayam ।। maitryārāmo hi satatamudyukto dharmagocare ।
tattvalakṣaṇatattvajño bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। yoniśastu matiryasya kāmakrodhairna hanyate । sa bhikṣuriti vijñeyo viparītastato anyathā ।। sarvabhūtadṛḍhaḥ śāntaḥ sarvasaṅgativarjitaḥ ।
sarvabandhananirmukto bhikṣurbhavati tattvavit ।। karmaṇi yasya vijñānaviṣayairyo na hanyate । nirmalaḥ syāt kanakavat santuṣṭo bhikṣurucyate ।। priyāpriye mano yasya na lepamanugacchati ।
saṅkalpānāṃ vidhijño yaḥ sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ ।। anyasaṃduṣṭacarito dharmaśīlo jitendriyaḥ । ahīnasatvo matimān bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। śāstre śāstrārthavijñāne matiryasya sadā ratā ।
na pānabhojanarataḥ sa bhikṣuḥ śāntamānasaḥ ।। vanāraṇyavihāreṣu śmaśāne tṛṇasaṃstare । ramate yasya tu mano bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।। doṣāṇāṃ karmatattvajñaḥ phalavit pariśeṣataḥ ।
hetupratyayatattvajño bhikṣuḥ syād vītakalmaṣaḥ ।। kilviṣakāntāro hatadoṣo jitendriyaḥ । punarbhavavidhijño yo bhikṣuḥ śāntamanāḥ ।। notkarṣo hṛṣṭahṛdaye nindayā naiva rūṣyati ।
samudratulyagāmbhīryo yogavān bhikṣurucyate ।। āveṇiko dṛḍhamatiḥ sūkṣmavādī na lolupaḥ । kāmavādī samo dakṣaḥ sa bhikṣuḥ śānta ucyate ।। kāmadhātūpagān hetūn rūpadhātau tathaiva ca ।
āruṣyeṣu ca tattvajñaḥ śāstrā bhikṣuḥ sa ucyate ।। na laukikakathāsaktaḥ śatrudoṣabadhe sadā । viṣavad yasya viṣayāḥ sa bhikṣurdeśito budhaiḥ ।। śuddhā yasya kāmeṣu matirbhavati nityaśaḥ ।
sa nirmuktamatirbhikṣurmuktaḥ saṃsārabandhanāt ।। dhyānādhyayanakarmaṇyaḥ kausīdyaṃ yasya dūrataḥ । hitakārī ca sattvānām āraṇyo bhikṣurucyate ।। praśnottaramatiryasya pratibhāvan jitendriyaḥ ।
sa dharmaḥ kathito jñeyo viparītastṛṇaiḥ samaḥ ।। kāyamānasabhīryasya sarvadā naiva khidyate । sarvakṛtyakaro jñeyo yaḥ saṅghāya ca tatparaḥ ।। na parārtha na lobhārtha yaśo artha kurute na tu ।
saṅghakārye matiryasya sa muktaḥ sarvabandhanaiḥ ।। na svargārtha matiryasya lābhārtha yaśase na vā । nirvāṇārtha kriyā sarvā sa bhikṣuḥ srota ucyate ।। pāpebhyo nityavirataḥ satkṛtyeṣu rataḥ sadā ।
na pāpamitrasaṃsargī bhikṣuḥ syād buddhaśāsane ।। maitryā bhāvitacittasya dakṣasya ṛjucetasaḥ । śikṣāpadeṣu raktasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।। jarāmaraṇaśīlasya saṃsāravimukhasya ca ।
dhyāne api na pramattasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।। anityatāvidhijñasya śūnyatāvatkriyāvataḥ । dhyānotkarṣavidhijñasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।। dhīro ayamagracoro ayaṃ yo ayaṃ bhikṣurasaṃvṛtaḥ ।
antaḥpurīvarasrāvī bahiścīvarasaṃvṛtaḥ ।। yathā yatnamayo rāśiḥ sarvo asāraśca durbalaḥ । evaṃ sañcarati rikto vitatho bhikṣuvādikaḥ ।। sa nārakeyo duḥśīlaḥ saṅgharatnabahiṣkṛtaḥ ।
kāyasya bhedānnarakaṃ nīyate cittavañcitaḥ ।। vañcito dharmavinayād yāti tat svena karmaṇā । malinastamasā baddho duḥkhabhāgī bhaviṣyati ।। aprāvṛtaḥ śubhadhaman nagnaḥ sādhujugupsitaḥ ।
nayate narakaṃ ghoraṃ yathā dharmabahiṣkṛtaḥ ।। aśobhanasya nicayo duḥkhadvāramanāvṛtam । saṃsārabandhanaṃ tīvraṃ dauḥśīlyamiti kathyate ।। asaṃvareṇa yo dagdhaḥ sa dagdho vahninā bhṛśam ।
tasya saṃvarakṣīṇasya vinipāto dhruvaṃ sthitaḥ ।। manasā saṃvarasthena svācāraiḥ saṃvarāyate । samūḍhacaryāmāruhya narakāyopakalpate ।। aśubhaṃ vardhate tasya divārātrau ca sarvataḥ ।
yasya śīlamayaṃ ratnaṃ dauḥśīlyena nivāritam ।। dharmaśūnyasya riktasya tamasā saṃvṛtasya ca । vidyate asaṃvarastasya yo na śaucāya kalpate ।। asaṃvaramayaḥ pāśo malinaḥ sādhuvarjitaḥ ।
ākarṣati sa duḥśīlān pāpiṣṭhān śīlavarjitān ।। asaṃvaraiśca dauḥśīlyaiḥ pāpaiśca saha saṅgatiḥ । dūtakā narakasyaite kāmānāmapi sevakāḥ ।। asaṃvṛtaprasūtasya capalasya viśeṣataḥ ।
pāpakarmābhiyuktasya narakaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।। kimete nāvagacchanti karmaṇāṃ sadṛśaṃ phalam । akṣipātāya mūḍhāya durmatau vimohitāḥ ।। ahanyahani vardhante pāpanadyo durāsadāḥ ।
duḥkhormimālāścapalāḥ pāpiṣṭhajanahāriṇaḥ ।। na teṣāṃ sukaraṃ janma na teṣāṃ sukaraṃ manaḥ । aśīlāḥ puruṣā ye vā śukladharmavivarjitāḥ ।। atyuccaśca śubho mārgaḥ sa adharma' iti kathyate ।
taṃ prāpyamanujaḥ śīghraṃ prayāti padamacyutam ।। tato apavādāḥ sādhyante śaktimantaḥ sukhāstu ye । saṃvarasya sadā dāsāsteṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate । dauḥśīlyaparamo hyeṣa malinīkurute nṛṇām ।।
ye śaikṣyapadavibhraṣṭā bhāgino narakasya te । evaṃ jñātvā naraḥ sarva saṃvaraṃ pratipadyate ।। bhavārṇasya sarvasya setubhūto hi saṃvaraḥ । śuddhājīvaviśuddhasya śāntavaktrasya karmaṇaḥ ।।
dhyāyino vipramuktasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ । dhūrdharasyāpramattasya śmaśānavanasevinaḥ ।। śāyino bhūtale nityaṃ nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ । pāṃśuśayyāvalambāṃsapātamekaṃ sajarjaram ।।
santoṣaḥ phalamūlaiśca sa sukhī buddhasambhavaḥ । vipramuktasya kāmebhyaḥ santoṣo hītarasya ca ।। savimuktakacittasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ । kuhakāmalamuktasya rajo vā tasya tāyinaḥ ।।
ākāśasamacittasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ । bahubaddhapadairyuktā vijñeyā cārikā ।। nāśikā brahmacaryasya nirvāṇagatiduḥkhikā । sevyate yā janairnityaṃ prākṛtaiḥ śīlavarjitaiḥ ।।
ajastraṃ parivarjyā sā dhyāyibhistattvadarśibhiḥ । daurbalyamūlamekā sā manaskārapraṇāśikā ।। nāśinī brahmacaryasya narakasya pradarśikā । bhraṃśikā svargamārgasya duḥkhasāgaraśoṣikā ।।
dūtikā pretalokasya tiryagyoninipātikā । nāmnā saṅgaṇikā sevā saṃsāre bandhamātṛkā ।। dhyānādhyayanaśaktaiva varjyā nityaṃ hi bhikṣubhiḥ । dhyānādhyayananirmukto nimittābhirataḥ sadā ।।
vivarjitaḥ śubhairdharmairapāpagamanāya saḥ । svadharma yaḥ parityajya paradharmeṣu rajyate ।। dharmadvayaparibhraṣṭo vinipātāya kalpate । svagṛhaṃ yaḥ parityajya paraveśyāni tiṣṭhati ।।
sadāyaṃ lāghavaṃ yāti nidhanaṃ cāśu gacchati । tathā yo vimatirbhūto vidvanmānī janecchayā ।। svadharmaviratiṃ kṛtvā paradharmeṣu vartate । adharme cāśayastasya paraliṅgopajīvinaḥ ।।
tṛṇavidyābhilipto ayaṃ pretaḥ pāpeṣu pacyate । yaśo antaṃ padamāsthāya pāpakarmaṇi vartate ।। śaśvat sa patito dṛṣṭaḥ śāsanāntāt pravartate । nispṛhaḥ kāmacaryāsu nirāmodaḥ pravarjitaḥ ।।
ārabdhavīryaḥ santuṣṭo dhyāyī bhikṣurihocyate ।। na ca kāmeṣu saṃsakto nityāhāravihāravān । kāṣāyasaṃvṛtaḥ kṣauro nāsau bhikṣurihocyate ।। nimittabodhako nakṣatragaticintakaḥ ।
rājasevāpramattaśca na sa bhikṣurihocyate ।। vaidyakarmāṇi kurvaśca śruti saṅgrathanaṃ tathā । saṅkīrṇā dinacaryā ca kurvan bhikṣuḥ praṇaśyati ।। dhyānādhyayanavidveṣī rataḥ saṅgaṇikāsu ca ।
lobhasatkāralābhaṃ ca kurvan bhikṣuḥ praṇaśyati ।। suvarṇadhātusaṃsakto bahumitraratiśca yaḥ । anyalābhābhilāṣito bhikṣuḥ patati śāsanāt ।। tapasaḥ saṅganirmukto na pāpagaṇasevakaḥ ।
saktūdakena santuṣṭaḥ sa bhikṣurniṣṭhuraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। āgatān viṣayān sarvān tyajati jvalanopamān । viśuddhadoṣo maṇivacchuddho bhikṣurihocyate ।। antarbahirviśuddhātmā jñānādibhiralaṅkṛtaḥ ।
śraddhayā śīlavastreṇa kriyāvān bhikṣurucyate ।। lobhadharmavyatīto yaḥ sthito merurivācalaḥ । sarvalokapriyaḥ śāntaḥ pārago bhikṣurucyate ।। trirātrivāsī kutrāpi kuśāsanavidhārakaḥ ।
girigahvarasevī ca vimukto bhikṣurucyate ।। pāpabhīrurasaṃsparśī saṃvṛtaḥ ca susaṃvṛtaḥ । jñānasevī sthiraḥ śānta ekākī bhikṣurucyate ।। acalaḥ priyavādī ca pāpamitravivarjitaḥ ।
aśaktaḥ sarvakṛtyeṣu mukto bhikṣurihocyate ।। rājasevā vigarhyāsti bhikṣoścāraṇyavāsinaḥ । kukaṣāyoktisevāsau mṛtyutaskarajīvikā ।। na hi rājasevako bhikṣuryaḥ sevyo devatairapi ।
na hiṃsāsavasaṃsṛṣṭo mahate aśucisevakaḥ ।। nirmalasya nirāmasya nispṛhasya ca dehinaḥ । saṃsārabhayabhītasya rājasevā na śobhate ।। vanāraṇyaśmaśāneṣu palvalo giribhūmiṣu ।
prāntabhūmiṣu grāmasya sthitaḥ bhikṣuḥ praśobhate ।। vanāraṇyaśmaśāneṣu bhikṣurna rājasevayā । dhyānādhyayananirmuktaḥ kavalāhārabhojitā । na bhikṣuriti vijñeyaḥ piśācasamamānasaḥ ।।
dhyānāddhi vimalaṃ saukhyaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ । na tatsukhātsukhaṃ cānyadasti loke kathañcana ।। taduttamadhyānasukhaṃ muktvā yaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ । raseṣu ramate bālastena mūḍho vihanyate ।।
viṣayairbhrāmitasyāsya nityaṃ tadgatacetasaḥ । vardhante akuśalā dharmāḥ paralokāpakarṣakāḥ ।। ātmano yānahīnaśca gurupṛcchanakastathā । bhikṣurudyuktavīryaśca nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।
śrutaṃ yāvad bhavatyeva tāvadeva prabhāṣate । ātmajño mānahīnaśca bhikṣurbhavati tattvavid ।। mānāpamānahīno yo mārgāmārgavicakṣaṇaḥ । svaparārthavidhijño yaḥ sa tuṣṭo bhikṣurucyate ।।
māninaḥ krūramanasaścapalasyālpamedhasaḥ । lābhasatkārayātasya kutaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati? ।। prasannācārayuktasya jñānagocarasevinaḥ । saṃsāradoṣabhītasya pravrajyā saphalā matā ।।
svabhāvaparabhāveṣu yasya buddhirnamuñcati । na karmaṇyavipāke ca mārgāmārge tathaiva ca ।। sadācāraviyuktasya sukhaduḥkhābhayasya ca । nivāsopahato bhikṣurbālavad dṛśyate paraiḥ ।।
tṛṇavallaghutāṃ yāti svārthācca parihīyate । nivāsopahato bhikṣuḥ parihīṇavane sthitaḥ ।। dhyānādhyayanakṛtyeṣu mano naiva pravartate । nivāsopahato bhikṣurjanasañcayatatparaḥ ।।
sañcayavyagramanasā jīvitaṃ parihīyate । kṣiṇoti retasaṃ svasya jīvitaṃ naiva gacchati ।। na ca vindati yat kṛtvā sukhamanyatra bhujyate । nivāsopahato bhikṣurjanasañcayatatparaḥ ।
pāpāni yāti nityaṃ sa tena gacchati durgatim ।। anabhipretamanaso nirāśasya ca dehinaḥ । sarvasaṅgavimuktasya śrāmaṇyaṃ saphalaṃ matam ।। girigahvaravṛkṣeṣu nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ ।
prasīdati śubhaṃ jñānaṃ dauḥśīlyaparivarjitam ।। sarvasaṅgavinirmukto viṣayairna ca vañcitaḥ । bhikṣu niṣphalo jñeyaḥ śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।। nirvāṇābhirato yo hi bhītasya vibhavārṇavāt ।
bhikṣurbhavati śuddhātmā na nivāsena karhicit ।। lobhamoheṣu ye śaktāste śaktā tṛṣṇayā sadā । tṛṣṇābandhanabaddhānāṃ nāyaṃ loko na cāparaḥ ।। asaṃśaktā matiryasya mithyākarmasu sarvadā ।
apakṣapātī dharmajño na sa gacchati durgatim ।। doṣapaṅkemano yasya na limpati kathañcana । ekārāmavihārīyo nirāśo munirucyate ।। nirmukto vimalācāro nivṛttamalakalmaṣaḥ ।
mukto yo viṣayaiḥ sarvairāraṇyo munirucyate ।। lokadharmairna nirvedaṃ samāyāti kathañcana । sukhaduḥkhasamaprajño nirmalo munirucyate ।। santoṣaḥ paramo nityaṃ kāmavivarjitaḥ ।
nirāmayaḥ kṛcchrajīvī śucirmunirihocyate ।। nayenna tena saṃśleṣaṃ yatra yatrānugacchati । ekacārī dṛḍhamatiḥ kriyāvān munirucyate ।। śubhāśubhānāṃ sarveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalatattvavit ।
śubhāśubhaparityāgī loke asau munirucyate ।। udyukto doṣanāśāya nityakāmagatiḥ smṛtaḥ । udayavyayatattvajño buddhimān munirucyate ।। deśakālavidāṃ śreṣṭho advayavādī jitendriyaḥ ।
saṃsārabhayabhīto ayaṃ praśānto munirucyate ।। ekārāmagato bhikṣuḥ saṃkṣiptendriyapañcakaḥ । dehalakṣaṇatattvajño nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।। vīryavān bhikṣurnityaṃ doṣavivarjitaḥ ।
udyānamiva krīḍāyā nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।। dagdhe kleśe vayaṃ dagdhā vanaṃ dagdhaṃ yathāgninā । kalyāṇadharme saṃraktā na raktā kāmabhojane ।। nityaṃ prāptyutsukā ye nityaṃ svajanasaṃratāḥ ।
māyayā vañcakā mūḍhāste dharmavartmani ।। ramaṇīyānyaraṇyāni tatraiva ramate manaḥ । ramante vītarāgāste na tu kāmagaveṣiṇaḥ ।। sa kathābhirato yastu rato viṣayatṛṣṇayoḥ ।
na yāsyati puraṃ śāntaṃ yo ca mṛtyuṃ na vindati ।। yo atyantaśāntamanasā nityaṃ dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ । ādimadhyāntakalyāṇo nityamadvayagocaraḥ ।। ।। iti bhikṣuvargastriṃśaḥ ।।
karuṇādānaśīlānikṣāntirvīryamathāpi ca । dhyānaṃ prajñātha nirvāṇo mano bhikṣuśca te daśa ।। ।। iti tṛtīyam udānam ।। (puṇyadevasukhairmitrarājastutibhiranvitāḥ ।
saddharmasmṛtivaipulyai gṛhīto ayaṃ samuccayaḥ ।। ramaṇīyāni puṇyāni phalaṃ teṣāṃ paraṃ śubham । tasmāt kuruta puṇyāni nāsti puṇyasamaṃ dhanam ।। puṇyaṃ nidhānamakṣayyaṃ puṇyaṃ ratnamanuttamam ।
pradīpasadṛśaṃ puṇyaṃ mātṛvat pitṛvat sadā ।। puṇyaṃ kṛtvā gatā devāḥ puṇyaṃ nayati sadgatim । puṇyaṃ kṛtvā narā loke modante tridive hi ।। puṇyādhikā hi puruṣā bhavanti sukhinaḥ sadā ।
tasmāt kuruta puṇyāni nāsti puṇyasamaṃ sukham ।। puṇyaṃ kṛtvā gatā devāḥ puṇyapriyadhanasya ca । hetubhūtaṃ sadā dṛṣṭaṃ tasmāt puṇyaṃ paraṃ sukham ।। puṇyaṃ nityottamaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ chāyāvadanugāmikam ।
tasmāt sukhaṃ paraṃ puṇyaṃ nāsti puṇyādṛte sukham ।। puṇyottīrṇāḥ punardevā patanti sukṛtānugāḥ । puṇyāpuṇyaphalo lokastasmāt puṇyaṃ samācaret ।। ye puṇyahīnā durdāntā nityaṃ kugatigāminaḥ ।
kutasteṣāṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sikatāsu yathā ghṛtam ।। vittena vañcitā mūḍhāḥ puṇyena parivañcitāḥ । na teṣāṃ vidyate śarma duḥkhaṃ teṣāmanuttaram ।। mānuṣyaṃ sukṛtaṃ hyetat kṛte bhavati dehinaḥ ।
tena karmavipākena svargalokeṣu jāyate ।। priyo bhavati yasyātmā yasya saukhye sthitā matiḥ । sa karotu mahatpuṇyaṃ devalokopapattaye ।। dharmacārī hi puruṣaḥ sukhāt sukhamavāpnute ।
nirmalaśca parāṃ śāntiṃ kṣipramevādhigacchati । tasmāt kuruta puṇyāni sāṃpracāyikam ।। puṇyakārī sadā dānto padaṃ gacchati cāvyayam । ramaṇīyāni puṇyāni karaṇīyānyanekaśaḥ ।।
vicitraṃ hi kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ vicitraṃ paripacyate । dharmādharmapradhānasya jīvalokasya sarvataḥ । śamatrāṇo yathā dharmastasmād dharmarato bhavet ।। yo dharma parityajya ramate kukṛte naraḥ ।
tasya duṣkṛtadagdhasya duḥkhaṃ bhavati nityaśaḥ ।। yāvannābhyeti maraṇaṃ yāvat sakalacintanam । tāvad dharme manaḥ kāryamupaśāntirbhaviṣyati ।। yo hi deśayate dharma pareṣāṃ hitakāṅkṣayā ।
sa mātā sa pitā caiva nirvāṇapuradeśakaḥ ।। śubhādhikaparaścaikaḥ yo deśayati deśikaḥ । sa gatyantaramārgajño nātho bhavati dehinām । na mūlyaṃ vidyate śāstuḥ subhāṣitapadasya vai ।।
na padaṃ labhate śāntaṃ yad dhanairupalabhyate । dravyaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ na dharmo buddhibandhanam ।। dravyaṃ vinaśyati nṛṇāṃ dharmadravyaṃ na jātu vai । ābhyantarasahastrāṇi dharma eko anugacchati ।।
na dhanaṃ padamapyekaṃ gacchantamanugacchati । hīyate draviṇaṃ teṣāṃ rājacaurokāgnibhiḥ । dharmavittaṃ na tacchakyamapahartu kathañcana ।। acireṇāpi kālena bhuktvā saukhyamanekaśaḥ ।
bhavatyavaśyaṃ patanaṃ tasmād dharmaparo bhavet ।। dharma ekaḥ paraṃ trāṇaṃ dharma ekaḥ parā gatiḥ । dharmeṇa pūrvavartyeṣa maraṇaṃ cāpyadharmataḥ ।। varaṃ dharmo dharmacārī dharmameva niṣevate ।
sa sukhāt sukhamāpnoti na duḥkhamanupaśyati ।। adharmacārī puruṣo yadādharma niṣevate । sa tadā duḥkhamāpnoti narakeṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।। ratnatrayaprasādasya bhāvitasyāpyanekaśaḥ ।
phalaṃ bhavati nirvāṇaṃ pūrvasvargopajīvinaḥ ।। ātmanā kriyate puṇyamātmanā pratipadyate । sukhaṃ vā yadi vā duḥkhamātmanaivopabhujyate ।। nadīstrota ivājastraṃ puruṣasya pravartate ।
puṇyaprabhāvo vipulo yasya śīle rataṃ manaḥ ।। bhavajanyaṃ phalaṃ yasya dharmo na rocate । dharmo hi nayati svarga dharmacārī sukhānvitaḥ ।। etadeva hi paryāptaṃ yad dharmaparipālanam ।
dharmādṛte hi puruṣo narakānupadhāvati ।। śreyo bhaveddhi maraṇaṃ na tu dharmavigarhaṇam । dharmeṇa varjito lokaḥ saṃsāre sarvadā bhramet ।। dharmacakṣurvimuktasya mohenākrāntacetasaḥ ।
vṛthā saukhyamidaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā yāto yathāparaḥ ।। dharmāṅkuro manaḥ kṣetre naiva rohatyacetasaḥ । yasya śīlapradā buddhiḥ dharmācaraṇatatparā ।। śubhena saviśuddhena bhāvitena prayatnataḥ ।
prayānti tat padaṃ śāntaṃ yatra duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।। indriyāṇāṃ vaśe yastu viṣayeṣu tathaiva ca । sa sarvabandhanairbaddhaḥ sa māraṃ nātivartate ।। aliptapāpakairdharmaiḥ nirdhanāt kanakadyutiḥ ।
sa muktabhavakāntāraḥ svastho bhavati sarvataḥ ।। buddho yeṣāṃ bahumato nityaṃ dharmaśca gocaraḥ । śuśrūṣācāryapādānāṃ śraddadhānaśca karmaṇām ।। triratnapūjayā nityaṃ sadbuddhiśca nirmalā ।
mātāpitṛṇāṃ pūjātaḥ nirvāṇapuragāminām ।। pravrajyābhāvadharmāśca sameṣāṃ samprakīrtitāḥ । brahmacaryāttacaryāṇāṃ sarvasaukhyāgrakārakāḥ ।। dānānāmuttamaṃ dānaṃ dharmadānaṃ prakathyate ।
udyogānāṃ sadā dhyānaṃ yena gacchati nirvṛtim ।। ūrdhvādhastiryaguktasya lokasyānekakarmaṇaḥ । agrayastathāgataḥ prokto dharmāṇāṃ tattvadarśakaḥ ।। vargāṇāṃ cārthasaṅghore pravaraḥ śānta ucyate ।
kṣetrāṇāṃ trividhaṃ puṇyaṃ guṇaduḥkhobhayaṃ tataḥ ।। mātā pitṛsamaḥ pūjya upādhyāyaḥ sadā bhavet । sa unmīlayate cakṣurvaśagocaratāṃ prati ।। agrāhyā vā sadā dṛṣṭā muninā tattvadarśinā ।
sukhasya bhūmayo hyetā niḥsukhā viṣayā matāḥ ।। yadyevaṃ kurute dharma nirmalaṃ mārgadarśinam । saukhyaṃ tasya bhavennityaṃ na saukhyaṃ devabhūmiṣu ।। bhavāntareṣu sukṛtaṃ pṛṣṭhato dehināṃ sthitam ।
sa āhūya prayatnena sevitavyaḥ sadā naraiḥ ।। anāgate bhayaṃ yo hi paśyati buddhacakṣuṣā । sa paṇḍitaḥ sadā dhīro mūrkhatvādatibhīrukaḥ ।। vipattijaṃ bhayaṃ dṛṣṭvā paśyati buddhimān ।
sa hi vighne tu samprāpte na viṣādena bādhyate ।। atha mūḍhamatirnityaṃ viṣayāneva sevate । vimohitaḥ sa viṣayaiḥ paścāttāpena dahyate ।। yāvat samagraṃ janmedaṃ jñānaṃ yāti vināvilam ।
tāvat kuruta puṇyāni duḥkhaṃ hayakṛtapuṇyatā ।। kṣayaṃ prayānti puṇyāni tvaritaṃ yāti jīvitam । dharmasaṅgrahaṇe yatnaḥ karttavyastuṣite suraiḥ ।। yo hi dharma parityajya pramādopahato naraḥ ।
na sañcinoti puṇyāni sa paścādapi tapyate ।। na yāvadāyāti jarā na vyādhiḥ saha mṛtyunā । tāvat kāryāṇi puṇyāni mā paścāt paritapyatha ।। asaṅgṛhītapuṇyasya pramādopahatasya ca ।
narake kāraṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ pramādastvāṃ haniṣyati ।। kiṃ tasya jīvitenārthaḥ kiṃ bhāgyaiḥ kiṃ ca bāndhavaiḥ । sabalendriyatāṃ prāpya yo na dharmarataḥ sadā ।। ahanyahani karttavyaṃ dharmasaṅgrahaṇe manaḥ ।
viratiścāpi pāpebhyaḥ sādhūnāṃ darśane na ca ।। śīlena yaḥ suro janma labdhvedaṃ kāmamohitaḥ । na sañcinoti puṇyāni sa bhavaṃ nātivartate ।। jñānārambhābhiratayaḥ śīlaratnavibhūṣitāḥ ।
kāmarāgāddhi ye bhītā devānāṃ devasammatāḥ ।। devāste hi sadā vandyā ye dharme niratāḥ sadā । ye tu nityaṃ bhavāsaktāste sarve nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ।। dharmasetumimaṃ prāpya pārāvāragataṃ mahat ।
na sañcarati yastūrṇa bhavānnaiva pramucyate ।। śubhānucāridharmaiśca śubhaṃ bhavati sarvadā । kalpakoṭisahastreṇa śubhaṃ naiva praṇaśyati ।। saṅgṛhītaṃ sadā śīlaṃ jñānaṃ ca parivartitam ।
dānaṃ cābhikṣayā dattaṃ bhavati svarasātmakam ।। doṣāstrayaḥ praṇaśyanti tribhirdānādibhirnṛṇām । tasmād doṣān parityajya guṇāḥ sevyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।। saṃsargo dharmaśīlānāṃ jñānārambhaḥ prayatnataḥ ।
naśyati bhavajaṃ duḥkhamarkapādairyathā tamaḥ ।। abhyupeyo devarato devatābhiśca vandyate । prāpya janmāntara cāpi nirvṛtiṃ cāśu gacchati ।। ।। iti puṇyavarga ekatriṃśaḥ ।।
panthāno muninā śāstre uktā ye tattvadarśinā । taistu samprasthitāste puruṣā devasammatāḥ ।। satyaṃ hi dānaṃ ca tathaiva maitrī sattveṣu rakṣā priyavāditā ca । samyaktvadṛṣṭirvimalaṃ manaśca panthānamāhustridivasya buddhāḥ ।।
śukladharmasamāyuktaḥ śuklacittasamanvitaḥ । sukhāt sukhataraṃ yāti jyotirjyotiḥparāyaṇaḥ ।। jyoti rjyotiṣā pūrṇa dīpo dīpāntarād yathā । tasmāddhi paramāṃllokān prayātā samprapadyate ।।
yasya śuddhaṃ sadā cittaṃ nirmalaṃ maṇivat sadā । sa śānto nirmamo dhīmān devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। dhyānaśīlasamādhibhyo yasya cittaṃ śubhānvitam । sa dhīmān kāñcanaprakhyo devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
prāṇātipātād virataḥ sarvasattvadayāparaḥ । ṛtusroto anukampāśca devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। śrutavān sarvalokasya krūrakarmavivarjitaḥ । aliptaḥ pāpakairdharmairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
tṛṇavat kāñcanaṃ yasya kāmā yasya viṣopamāḥ । sa kāmavarjako dhīmān devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। nākṛṣyate manaḥ kāmairviṣayai rāgahetubhiḥ । samantātbhavakāntārairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
bhinnāḥ paramparā ādau mitravān dhanabāndhavaḥ । yaḥ karoti susaṃśliṣṭā devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। yasya buddhisthitaṃ veśma na buddhiḥ kvāpi rāgiṇī । sa jitārirviśuddhātmā devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
praśastakāyakarmānto yaḥ pāpavirataḥ sukhī । sa kāmavirato dhyāyī devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। pāpamitravinirmuktastṛṣṇāviṣavivarjitaḥ । na baddhaḥ strībhayaiḥ pāśairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
prayatnavādī yo dharme dānaśīlasamādhimān । nityodyukto dṛḍhamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। samyagbandhano yena pāśaśchinno yathāsinā । sacchinnapāśaḥ svavaśī devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
manuṣyabhūtā ye sattvāścaranti sukṛtāvahāḥ । tena karmavipākena suraloke prasūyate ।। manuṣyāṇāṃ balād devā devānāṃ balino narāḥ । anyonyabalino te ye saddharmapathamāsthitāḥ ।।
devānāṃ sugatirmartyāḥ martyānāṃ sugatiḥ surāḥ । apāyabhūmayastisraḥ śubhakarmavivarjitāḥ ।। dharmādhīnaṃ sukhaṃ sarva dharmādhīnā hi nirvṛtiḥ । dharmaḥ supteṣu jāgarti dharmo hi paramā gatiḥ ।।
dharmeṇa nirjito adharmaḥ satyenānṛtiko jitaḥ । jñānena varjito moho devaistu hyasurā jitāḥ ।। sopānabhūtā ye tāni karmāṇi tridivasya hi । yoniṃ tyaktvā narā yānti devalokaṃ sukhodayam ।।
caturvidho vāṅniyamaḥ ko api trividhapañcadhā । saptasopānamārūpyaṃ gacchanti tridivaṃ budhāḥ ।। prabhayā te ca divyantaḥ svaśarīreṇa jātayā । ramante svargabhuvane rañjitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।।
nityāmodavihārā nityaṃ saukhyavihāriṇaḥ । yad devā devabhavane śīlaṃ tatra hi kāraṇam ।। yadapsaraḥ parivṛtā yat sūryaśaśisannibhāḥ । devāḥ samantād deveṣu tatsarvaśubhahetukam ।।
yadīpsitaṃ sambhavati sambhūtaṃ ca na hīyate । vartate ca śubhaṃ nityaṃ tat sarva śubhahetukam ।। śubhacārī sadā dānī sarvabhūtadayārataḥ । dānamaitryā sadā yukto devānāṃ samatāṃ vrajet ।।
prāṇātipātād virataḥ sarvasattvadayāparaḥ । samyagājīvakarmānto devānāṃ saṅgatiṃ vrajet ।। adatte na ratiḥ kiñcid dāne cāsya sadāmatiḥ । śāntendriyamatirdhīmān devasaṅgatimaśnute ।।
mithyākāmairvimukto yaḥ satpathābhirataḥ sadā । nirvāṇakāṃkṣī vimalo devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। vimanaskaṃ hi yat prīte puruṣe kurute laghu । madyavarjī paraṃ dhīro devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
sukha hi yo devaḥ pramādaṃ nānusevate । sukhāt sukhamavāpnoti nirvṛttiṃ cādhigacchati ।। kṣayāvasānaṃ tat saukhyaṃ nirvāṇamiti śāśvatam । tat saprāpyavimāneṣu rājante puruṣottamāḥ ।।
uccāduccaro merustasmāduccaṃ sadā sukham । śubhena niyato janturakaniṣṭhān surān ।। niravadye kutastṛptirdevaloke viśeṣataḥ । atīva saukhyaṃ labhate kasmād deveṣu sarvadā ।।
tṛṣṇāgniparidagdhena na saukhyamupalabhyate । evaṃ sukṛtadagdhena na saukhyamupalabhyate ।। trividhaṃ sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā triprakāraṃ trihetukam । etadagryaṃ tribhūmiṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ mahat ।।
ahiṃsādānaparamā ye saddharmaparāyaṇāḥ । satyakṣāntidamairyuktāḥ tridivaṃ samāgatāḥ ।। divyābharaṇasampannā divyamālyavibhūṣitāḥ । yad devā divyamatayaḥ śubhameva tat ।।
devānāṃ yanmahatsaukhyaṃ nyūnādhikyamāsthitam । nyūnamadhyaṃ tu yasyaitat phalaṃ puṇyasya dṛśyate ।। yena yāvaddhi yat puṇyaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati dehinā । tasya tāvaddhi tat saukhyaṃ devalokeṣu pacyate ।।
svāgataṃ tava bho bhadra! sukṛtaṃ kṛtavānasi । saptadhā rakṣitaṃ śīlaṃ tasyaitat phalamāgatam ।। vanopavanaśaileṣu padmākaravaneṣu ca । harmyāgreṣu ramasva sadaivataḥ ।।
vanopavanaśaileṣu vaidūryaśikhareṣu ca । vanādriṣu ca naikeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।। kalpavṛkṣeṣu ramyeṣu nadīprastravaṇeṣu ca । saritsu ca viśālāsu saha daivataiḥ ।।
strotasvinyādiyukteṣu parvateṣu nadīṣu ca । nagareṣu mahārtheṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।। madagandhipraroheṣu nīlotpalavaneṣu ca । yakṣasadmasu ramyeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।।
bhūmibhāgeṣu cānteṣu ratnākaravaneṣu ca । vimāneṣu ca ramyeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।। pañcāṅgikena tūryeṇa manaḥprahlādakāriṇā । nṛtyamānaḥ sukhī nityaṃ ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।।
śīlabījaṃ śodhayitvā śīleṣu vividheṣu ca । krīḍa tvaṃ vividhairdivyairyathārthamanusevase ।। yatprabhāmālino devā ramante vividhaiḥ sukhaiḥ । tacchubhasya phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nirmalasya viśeṣataḥ ।।
yadetairvividhaiḥ saukhyairdevāḥ krīḍantyanekaśaḥ । na vayaṃ hetavastatra purākṛtam ।। kūṭāgārāṇi sarvāṇi karmacitrāṇi sarvadā । bhunakti devo deveṣu satkṛtenopabṛṃhitaḥ ।।
pāśatrayavimuktasya pañcabhiḥ pālitasya vai । ekadharmavyatītasya devaloko mahīyate ।। pramudyaccetasāṃ puṃsāṃ spaṣṭaceṣṭā samāhitā । āgatā devasadanaṃ svakarmaphalasākṣiṇī ।।
uparyupari saukhyāni sukṛtasya vai । bhuñjanti vibudhāḥ svarga yaddhi pūrvakṛtānugam ।। sākṣibhūtā ime sarvakarmaṇāṃ vividhā drumāḥ । nirantaraṃ susadṛśaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
yena yena vipākena yatra yatropapadyate । puruṣo labhate svasya prārabdhasya śubhāśubham ।। śubhena karmaṇā janturnityaṃ deveṣu jāyate । tathāśubhena narake patanti puruṣādhamāḥ ।।
śubhāśubhābhyāṃ saṃraktāḥ kāminaḥ kāmamohitāḥ । nāvagacchanti maraṇaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। śubhāśubhavipāko ayaṃ yo vṛkṣeṣūpalabhyate । na saukhyād viramantyete manaḥ saukhyena mohitāḥ ।।
trividhaṃ sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā bhāvayitvā ca saptadhā । trisaṃkhyākān ripūn hatvā yānti deveṣu mānavāḥ ।। nāsūyati kriyākleśān na ca nandīmasūyati । sa nandyasūyakaḥ śuddho devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ ।।
vinindya mātsaryamidaṃ duḥkhasyāyatanaṃ mahat । samaṃ ca trividhaṃ dattvā devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ ।। prāṇināṃ praṇayaṃ nityaṃ rakṣayitvānukampayā । maitracittaḥ sadā dānto devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ ।।
adattaṃ ca dhanaṃ dattvā dattvānandaṃ ca sarvataḥ । cetanābhāvitamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। mātṛvat paradārāṃśca dṛṣṭvā tattvārthacintakaḥ । alipto pāpakairdharmairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
svacittaprītyartha jihvāraṇisamudbhavaḥ । kathyate sa mṛṣāvādastaṃ hitvā sugatiṃ vrajet ।। paiśūnyaṃ ca sadā hitvā maitryanarthakaraṃ padam । ślakṣṇaprabhaḥ ślakṣṇamatiḥ devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
pāruṣyaṃ śatruvaddhīro varjayatyeva sarvadā । ślakṣṇaprabhāmatirnityaṃ sarveṣu gatigāmikaḥ ।। adharmo yasya jihvāgre na bhūto na bhaviṣyati । sadā duṣkālatattvajño devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
yenedaṃ rakṣitaṃ śīlaṃ saptadhā buddhadeśitam । sa dhīraḥ śīlatattvajño devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। vividhakarmavaśagaṃ janmedaṃ labhate suraiḥ । tatprāpya yo na dharmajñaḥ sa paścāt paritapyate ।।
vanopavanaramyo ayaṃ latāvedikamaṇḍapaḥ । yadvicitramayo lokastat sarva śubhajaṃ phalam ।। yena yena yathā karma kṛtaṃ bhavati śobhanam । tasya tasya tathā dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ tadanugāmikam ।।
pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyate devairhīnamadhyottamaṃ sukham । yena yena yathā cīrṇaṃ tasya tasya tathā phalam ।। vicitraveṣāḥ saṃmūḍhā devā mohavaśānugāḥ । tannāśānmanasā mūḍhā na paśyanti mahadbhayam ।।
vicitrakāmaratayo vicitraphalakāṅkṣiṇaḥ । na vā kurvanti karmāṇi te asurā mūḍhacetasaḥ ।। phalaṃ yeṣāṃ priyaṃ cittaṃ na ca śīle ratā matiḥ । te pradīpaṃ parityajya premālokaparāyaṇāḥ ।।
ye hetuphalasādṛśyenecchanti surasattamān । te hetuphalatattvajñā bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ ।। vinābījaṃ phalaṃ nāsti vinā dīpaṃ kutaḥ prabhā? । vinā śīlaiḥ kutaḥ svargo muktirjñānaṃ vinā kutaḥ? ।।
tatsukhaṃ tadvimuktasya gatakāṅkṣasya tāyinaḥ । vimuktakāmatṛṣṇasya nirmamasya ca dhīmataḥ ।। yadidaṃ karmajaṃ saukhyaṃ sarva kalmaṣam । yaṃ neṣṭakaṃ bhavatyeva tat sarvamamalaṃ smṛtam ।।
yo manorathakṛtsnasya bahirantaśca । sarvālokaḥ sadāloko devatāgaṇasevitaḥ ।। virājate girivaro ratnamāṇikyasannibhaḥ । prabhūtasalilo yaśca padminībhiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।।
vanopavanaramyo ayaṃ mṛgapakṣiniṣevitaḥ । kandarodarasaṃrambho bhitvā gaganamutthitaḥ ।। sevyate devatairnityaṃ divyamālyavibhūṣitaiḥ । nṛtyagītaprakṛṣṭābhirdevatābhiśca sarvataḥ ।।
pañcāṅgikena tūryeṇa prerita iva lakṣyate । śirobhūto mahāramyaḥ prabhāmālī samantataḥ ।। sukṛtena śubhenāyaṃ karmaṇādhiguṇena vai । yaṃ samāśritya krīḍanti devavṛndāni sarvataḥ ।।
dānaśīlayutā vṛddhā nityaṃ tadgatamānasāḥ । ye bhavanti sadā dāntāste janāḥsvargagāminaḥ ।। saṃkṣiptamanasaḥ śāntāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ । vairiṇāṃ viṣayo nityaṃ praśāntamanasastu ye ।।
svargagāminaḥ । bhavābhavena tīvreṇa bādhate sādhanam । sudāntamānasāṃ dhīrāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। satyamārgavilambena hayatīva sukhabhāginaḥ ।
sārāsāravidhijñāśca te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। saṃsāre ye na rakṣanti svamano dehinaḥ । nirvāṇābhiratā nityaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। vṛkṣamūle śmaśāne vā tathā ca girikandare ।
dhyāyinaḥ sattvamanasaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। mātrajñā deśakālajñāḥ pāpamitra varjitāḥ । maitreṇa cetasā ye tu te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। na snānadarśanaratā narāḥ manmathavāriṇā ।
ekāntagāminaḥ śāntāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। kṣaṇe kṣaṇe sadā kāyaṃ paśyantyaśucisambhavam । kāryākāryavidhijñā ye te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। dharmāṇāṃ dharmatāṃ ye ca paśyanti vividhā samāḥ ।
na ca rakṣanti saṃsāre te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। vedanā madhyatattvāntamanekavidhasambhavam । paśyanti ca na rakṣanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। māyopamaṃ ca kṣaṇikaṃ gandharvanagaropamam ।
ye jānanti cittāḥ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। ekalakṣaṇatattvajñā vilakṣaṇavidaḥ svayam । nirvāṇarāgamanasaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। mātṛvat paradārān ye pitṛvat sarvadehinaḥ ।
paśyanti ye bhayaṃ loke te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। śūnyavargagato nityaṃ sattvānāṃ priyavādinaḥ । akrūrā ṛddhimanasaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। kāṣṭhavalloṣṭhavat sarva paravittasamīkṣakāḥ ।
saṃtuṣṭāḥ svena cittena te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। na rātrau na divā yeṣāṃ kausīdyadyutiriṣyate । nityodyuktavihārā ye te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। kaukṛtyaṃ styānamiddhaṃ ca kausīdyaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
varjayanti sadā dhanyāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। dauḥśīlyaṃ pañcarandhrebhyaḥ pariśuddhamanekadhā । saṃkṣipanti sadā duḥkhaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। upādānacatuṣṭvajñāḥ satyāni ca tathaiva ca ।
ye paśyanti budhāḥ prajñāṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। duḥkhaṃ duḥkhavipākaśca duḥkheṣu ca manaśca yat । paśyanti ye sadā tattvaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। tīvravyasanamāpannā ye dharmāvimuñcakāḥ ।
śāntāśca dharmamatayaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। śuklāvadātaṃ ye vastraṃ pāṃsukūlaṃ tathaiva ca । piṇḍapātaratā nityaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। adaṇḍāḥ śāntamanaso nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ ।
naiṣkarmyaniratāḥ sarve te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। mṛṣṭaṃ ca yadi vāṅmṛṣṭaṃ yathecchāvidhimāgatam । santuṣyanti na kupyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। śuklāvadātaṃ ye vastraṃ pāṃsukūlaṃ tathaiva ca ।
saṃvṛtau caiva saṃtuṣṭāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। śayyātale yathā bhūmau harmyāgre vā tathāpare । na duṣyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। cakṣurviṣayamāpannaṃ yatkarma sāmparāyikam ।
tattvato ye prapaśyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। apriyaṃ vā priyaṃ vāpi ye śrutvā tīvrasambhramāt । akṣubdhamatayo muktāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। ṣaḍindriyāṇi sarvāṇi viṣayāṃstu tathaiva ca ।
saṃkṣipanti na rakṣanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। yathā karma kṛtaṃ sarvamaviśeṣeṇa tattvataḥ । paśyantyamanaso dhanyāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। karmaṇāṃ ca vipākaṃ ca kṛtaṃ ।
bibhyatīha sadā duḥkhete janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। ityetāni mahārthāni nityaṃ duḥkhakarāṇi ca । kurvanti vidhivat sarva te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। ।। iti devavargo dvātriṃśaḥ ।।
anuttareṣu saukhyeṣu dhyānopātteṣu ye ratāḥ । teṣāṃ sukhaṃ yathāvat syāt nirvāṇapuradarśakam ।। navena sukhaduḥkhena purāṇamabhihanyate । devasyaitannavenaiva purāṇamabhihanyate ।।
dhū miśraṃ yathā kāṣṭhaṃ vi miśraṃ yathodanam । tathā sukhamidaṃ sarvamasvatvaṃ nāvagamyate ।। tat sukhaṃ yad vitṛṣṇānāmekāntasukhacāriṇām । nirmohiṇāmarāgāṇāṃ nirvāṇapuragāminām ।।
teṣāṃ vimalamādyantaṃ saukhyānāmapi tat sukham । yeṣāṃ tṛṣṇānugā cāśā sarvathā naiva cetasi ।। saṅgṛhītasya cittasya nirātmasya ca sarvataḥ । kāryākāryeṣu mūḍhasya sukhaṃ nityamupasthitam ।।
sā bahirnihatā yena nandisaṃsārahetukī । sa dhīraḥ pāragaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sukhī nirvāṇamāśritaḥ ।। naitat sukhena tṛṣṇānāṃ yad rāgadveṣasaṃyutam । yatra rāgādinirmuktaṃ tat sukhaṃ nirmalaṃ matam ।।
devaloke samāsādya yaḥ suro nāvamanyate । sa sukhāt sukhatāṃ yāti yatra tṛṣṇā na bādhate ।। tadantyasukhi śreyo yatra mṛtyurna vidyate । mṛtyupāśairna baddhasya na sukhaṃ vidyate kvacit ।
yat sukhaṃ kāmajanakaṃ na tat saukhyaṃ satāṃ matam ।। yatra kāmavinirmuktastatsukhāt sukhamuttamam । yat sukhaṃ janayet śreyaḥ yathodanam ।। yatra tṛṣṇāvinirmuktiḥ payomiśraṃ yathodanam ।
yathā padmavane gṛddhā yānti kravyabhakṣiṇaḥ ।। evaṃ śānteṣvaraṇyeṣu na bhāntyaśubhacāriṇaḥ । kvacicchāntaṃ vanaṃ ramyaṃ kvacid devāḥ pramādinaḥ ।। viparītaṃ na sadṛśaṃ bhānoḥ śītā yathā prabhā ।
gatatṛṣṇasya yat saukhyaṃ muktaduḥkhasya tāyinaḥ ।। tasyāntareṇa saukhyasya sukhametanna gaṇyate । dhyāyinastvapramattasya muktapāpasya sarvadā ।। tat sukhaṃ tat paraṃ saukhyaṃ nedaṃ tṛṣṇāvidāṃ matam ।
munisevyaṃ vanamidaṃ sevitaṃ ca subhāṣitaiḥ ।। nārhā rāgagaṇaṃ sevituṃ bho surottamāḥ । yadetad bhavatāṃ saukhyametanna khalu śāśvatam ।। tat sukhaṃ paramaṃ śāntaṃ vītatṛṣṇai niṣevyate ।
niḥsevitaṃ vanamidaṃ ye gatāḥ paramaṃ padam ।। yat prāpya sarvaduḥkhasyacchedo bhavati sarvathā । brahmacaryādanirmuṣṭāḥ śīlālāpena vañcitāḥ ।। nārhanti sevituṃ ramyaṃ vanaṃ śāntaṃ subhāṣitam ।
śāntaṃ ca bhāvitaṃ ramate śubhagocare ।। na rāgacāriṇāṃ cittaṃ ramate vanagocare । na rāgavyākulaṃ cittaṃ vaneṣu labhate dhṛtim ।। śravyāmūḍhā matiryasya nityaṃ tribhuvanaṃ kare ।
sa ratiṃ labhate śāntiṃ vane puruṣasattamaḥ ।। sa kalparāgakuṭilo nityaṃ rāgādibhirvṛtaḥ । sa śāntiṃ naiva labhate vane śānte sukhāvahe ।। yeṣāṃ tu manasā nityaṃ vane dhyānaniyoginām ।
vanaṃ teṣāṃ sadāramyaṃ na tu rāgagaveṣiṇām ।। vaneṣu bhāvitaṃ cittaṃ nagareṣu na kupyate । tasmād vanaṃ sadā sevyaṃ nagaraṃ naiva śasyate ।। vikṣipyate hi nagare nṛṇāṃ rāgādibhirvṛtaḥ ।
vikṣipta mohakuṭilaṃ vanaṃ bhūyaḥ prasīdati ।। tasmād vanaṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ yogināmālayaṃ mahat । saṃsevyaṃ vītamanasā yasya tad vītakalmaṣam ।। praśāntendriyacittasya yā ratiryogino hṛdi ।
nāsau śaktiḥ sahasrasya bhaviṣyati ।। yā dhyāyino ratirdṛṣṭā vyavadānāya sarvadā । na yāmeṣvapi sā dṛṣṭā nityaṃ rāgānurāgiṇī ।। ratiryā kāmavaśagā sā nityaṃ duḥkhasambhavā ।
yā tu kleśavaśāt prītiḥ śāśvatā nahi ।। śreyo vaneṣu caritaṃ tattaduccaritaṃ nṛbhiḥ । yasmāt tat pratibaddhaṃ hi śreyasāṃ padamucyate ।। susambhṛtena dharmeṇa rakṣiteneva cetasā ।
sudṛṣṭaṃ labhate sthānaṃ yatra doṣo na vidyate ।। yaḥ kṣiptamanasā nityaṃ na ca dharmaparāyaṇaḥ । teṣāṃ vṛthā sukhamidaṃ gacchati na nivartate ।। ye tu tattvavido dhīrāḥ paśyanti jagataḥ sthitim ।
anityaduḥkhaśūnyānāṃ teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।। sukhadharmasya caraṇaṃ jñānasya ca niṣevaṇam । ahiṃsā satyavacanaṃ tadapyekāntataḥ sthitam ।। ekadharmavyatītā ye ye adharmaparivañcakāḥ ।
tristhānalakṣaṇāviṣṭāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। udayavyayadharmāṇāmanityaṃ karmajaṃ hi tat । tat sukhaṃ sāstravaṃ nityaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।। tat sukhaṃ tadvitṛṣṇasya nīrāgasya hi dehinaḥ ।
muktirbhavati doṣasya pārasthasya hi tāpinaḥ ।। tat kiñcit sāsravaṃ saukhyaṃ tat sarva kṣaṇikaṃ matam । rāgabandhād vinirmuktaṃ tat sarva niścalaṃ sukham ।। ye na kṣipanti duḥkhena sukhe yeṣāṃ na saṅgatiḥ ।
te duḥkhasukhanirmuktā nirvāṇasukhagāminaḥ ।। anupāyena ye mūḍhāḥ prārthayanti sukhaṃ sadā । bālukābhiryathā tailaṃ yallabhyaṃ nityameva tat ।। na cetasā naraḥ prājño manorathaśatairapi ।
śakro api tat sukhaṃ kartu yathā karma kṛtaṃ mahat ।। sasukhaṃ yasya tu manaḥ saddharmānucaro bhavet । duḥkhairmuktyabhilāṣo ayaṃ sa dharme kurute matim ।। nāhetukaṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā trividhātmakam ।
sukhe duḥkhe pṛthagbhāve tasmānnu sukṛta caret ।। nedaṃ saukhyaṃ sadā śastamadhruvaṃ vipralopi ca । tṛṣṇāviṣeṇa sammiśraṃ viṣamiśraṃ yathodanam ।। tat saukhyaṃ satāṃ śastaṃ yatra mṛtyurna vidyate ।
na ca priyeṇa viśleṣo nāpriyeṇa samāgamaḥ ।। yadetat strīmayaṃ saukhyametad duḥkhāya kalpyate । tadbījavartakā dṛṣṭā narakeṣūpapattaye ।। yat sukhaṃ duḥkhajanakaṃ kathaṃ tat sukhamiṣyate? duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ jñeyaṃ pariṇāmavaśena tat ।।
yadetad bhujyate saukhyametat kālena naśyati । sūryastāstaṅgatasyaivaṃ raśmayaḥ saha cāriṇaḥ ।। vikṛtiṃ yasya manaḥ sukhaduḥkhairna gacchati । sa dhīmān suraloke ca gatvānyallabhate sukham ।।
bhuktaṃ sukhaṃ purāṇaṃ tu hīnakarma karoti ca । purāṇaṃ sukṛtaṃ śīrṇa mṛtyukāle na budhyate ।। yadidaṃ dṛśyate saukhyaṃ manovākkāmajaṃbhṛśam । anityaṃ tad vināśatvamacireṇa bhaviṣyati ।।
phenabudbudasaṅkāśaṃ marīcyudakasannibham । cañcalormi sukhaṃ sarva vinipāto bhavārṇave ।। niṣpratīkāraviṣamaḥ sarvabhūtabhayāvahaḥ । cakravātapravego mṛtyurājaiṣa dhāvati ।।
nāśayitvā sukhaṃ sarva nāśayitvā ca jīvitam । karmasaṅkalpavāhyeṣu lokamanyatra neṣyati ।। yadatīva sukhaṃ nṛṇāṃ taddhi saukhyāya kalpyate । yannaiṣyati sukhaṃ kiñcit taddhi naiva vigaṇyate ।।
vartamānaṃ tu yat saukhyaṃ tṛṣṇāviṣavivarjitam । sarva hyanātmajaṃ duḥkhamanityaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ balam ।। yad sukhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu na śastaṃ tattvadarśibhiḥ । tena matvā kathaṃ devā bhavanti vigatajvarāḥ? ।।
aviṣṭovatakālo ayaṃ bhairavo yāti sattvaram । yo bhokṣyate surān sarvān śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।। atiyāti sukhaṃ sarva kriyatāṃ śraiyasaṃ manaḥ । mā paścāt saṃbhavo yoge mṛtyukālo bhaviṣyati ।।
janmāntarasahasreṣu yad muktaṃ karmajaṃ sukham । taraṅgasannibhaḥ kvāyaṃ bāliśo asthiram ।। na sukhaistṛpyate bālastathā kāṣṭhairyathānalaḥ । tasmānna saktasya sukhaṃ bhavati naiṣṭhikam ।।
viṣasya doṣamuktasya kāmadoṣānudarśinaḥ । dhyāyinaścāpramatasya tat sukhaṃ yadanāvilam ।। sukhī bhavati tat prāpya na sukhaṃ bhavajanmanaḥ । bandhamiśraṃ viṣaṃ yadvad dharmasaukhyodayastathā ।।
tasmāt tatsukhasaktānāṃ nityaṃ kāmagaveṣiṇām । bhavantyanekasaukhyā tasmāt kāmo na jāyate ।। nendriyāṇāṃ jayaḥ śakyaḥ karttu viṣayagocare । jñānena hi nivartante indriyāṇi svagocare ।।
duḥkhe sukhābhisaṃsaktā nityaṃ bālā medhasaḥ । viparyayā paribhrāntā bhramanti gatipañcake ।। yadatyantasukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tat sukhaṃ satyamucyate । yatra duḥkhaṃ vipākaṃ syāt tat sukhaṃ duḥkhameva tat ।।
anyāgatasya duḥkhasya pratighātayate budhaḥ । pāpasya hetujaṃ duḥkhaṃ pāpasyākaraṇaṃ sukham ।। ।। iti sukhavargo trayastriṃśaḥ ।। tanmitraṃ mitramityuktaṃ yanmitraṃ sāmparāyikam ।
nivartayati yaḥ pāpād vyasanāccāpi rakṣati ।। praveśayati yannityaṃ taddhitaṃ sāmparāyikam । mitraṃ bhavati tannṛṇāṃ na mitraṃ pāpakārakam ।। apūtiḥ pūtisaṃśleṣāt pūtirevopajāyate ।
na pūtiḥ pūtasaṃśleṣamapūtiṃ karttumarhati ।। yādṛśena saṃśleṣaṃ kurute puruṣaḥ sadā । taddoṣāt sadṛśo dṛṣṭaḥ śubho vā yadi vāśubhaḥ ।। śubhārthī puruṣaḥ sarvānaśubhānnaiva sevate ।
tenāsau duḥkhamāpnoti na śubhaṃ duḥkhakāraṇam ।। saṃśleṣajā guṇāḥ dṛṣṭā doṣāḥ saṃśleṣajātayaḥ । lakṣaṇaṃ guṇadoṣāṇāmidamuktaṃ svabhāvajam ।। yaśasā yujyate yo hi nityaṃ sādhusamāgamāt ।
asādhu'saṅgamācchrīghraṃ prayāti puruṣādhamaḥ ।। etat sāraṃ sadā kārya yadasādhuvivarjanam । sādhubhiśca sadā vāso duṣṭāṇāṃ ca vivarjanam ।। doṣān samuddhareddhīmān guṇavṛddhiṃ samācaret ।
mitraṃ prakurvīta kausīdyavimukho bhavet ।। na māninaṃ kusīdaṃ vā nityaṃ sarvānuśaṅkinam । liptapāpamatikrūraṃ mitraṃ kuryānna paṇḍitaḥ ।। udyuktaṃ mṛdujātīyaṃ dharmiṣṭhaṃ doṣavarjitam ।
samyagdṛṣṭiracapalaṃ mitraṃ seveta paṇḍitaḥ ।। na pāpakaṃ bhavenmitraṃ bhaveduttamapauruṣaḥ । uttamaṃ bhajamānasya na doṣebhyo bhayaṃ bhavet ।। rūpaiśvaryakulādīni bhidyante dehinaḥ ।
bhayapradaṃ taṃ mātaṅgaḥ prayāntaṃ naiva paśyati ।। udvṛttaḥ puruṣo nityaṃ pramādākulitendriyaḥ । laghutāṃ yāti loke asmin pretyapāpeṣu pacyate ।। rūpaiśvaryamadārthā ye te narāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ ।
teṣāṃ na suśamaṃ pretyapāpeṣu pacyate ।। rūpaiśvaryakulārthā ye na te tattvasya bhāginaḥ । atattvabuddhayo bālā na taranti bhavārṇavam ।। etatkulaṃ ye vibhavā yaccānyat sukhamiṣyate ।
sarvāṇyetānyanityāni tasmātteṣu na viśramet ।। na jñānaśīlanirmuktaṃ kuśalaṃ yānti paṇḍitāḥ । yeṣāṃ jñānaṃ ca śīlaṃ ca te kule mahati sthitāḥ ।। carituṃ cāmalaṃ śīlaṃ śīlameva mahādbhutam ।
mahākulaprasūtāste vaśamāninaḥ ।। dānaśīlatapodhyānasatyaiśvaryaparākramaiḥ । saṃyuktā ye kulīnāste ye na dharmavivarjitāḥ ।। naiśvaryajñānahīnasya na kulaṃ nāpi saṅgatiḥ ।
tasmātkulaṃ jñānamayaṃ jñānahīnaṃ na tat kulam ।। ।। iti mitravargaścatustriṃśaḥ ।। bhuvaṃ parijano paśyan dharmacārī jitendriyaḥ । sa rājā dhārmiko dhīmān svargalokopapattaye ।।
niyataṃ yaḥ karaṃ kāle dharmeṇa paribhujyate । sa rājā lobhanirmukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।। kṣamāvān priyavākyo yaḥ krodhaharṣādidhārakaḥ । sa mahīṃ pālayettvenāṃ loke hi śreṣṭhatāṃ gataḥ ।।
apakṣapātinaḥ śraddhā mitreṇa ca hanyate । sa rājanyasabhājetā devalokāya kalpyate ।। baddhadarśī mahātmā yo gurupūjaka eva ca । alolo yo dṛḍhamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।
pūrve yat pitṛbhirdattaṃ devānupadiśanti ca । na ca hiṃsati bhūtāni sa deveṣūpapadyate ।। dānaśīle sadā dakṣo dharmavādī jitendriyaḥ । sa matvāryāṃ mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ devalokaṃ mahīyate ।।
nādhārmikaṃ dhārayati dhārmikeṣu ca rakṣati । sa dharmaśīlasaṃśuddho devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।। na strīṇāṃ vaśago rājā sādhūnāṃ ca vaset sadā । sa nirmalamatirdhīraḥ suralokopapattaye ।।
na sarvasya vacogrāhī priyaḥ sādhujanasya tu । so amṛtastattvadarśīvā nākṛṣṭa iva rohati ।। yo dharmalobhamāyāti draviṇaṃ naiva lapsyate । sa lobhamalanirmukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।।
na mithyādarśanenāpi strītvadarśanatatparaḥ । sa śuddha eva vimalo yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।। prājñaḥ śīle sadāyukto dānenābhīkṣṇatāṃ gataḥ । pravijitya mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ pretya devapriyo bhavet ।।
priyasya tu bhaved vākyaṃ stotrotsavakaraṃ param । āhlādayitvā vasudhāmante devopapattaye ।। avisaṃvādakaṃ vākyaṃ yasya merurivācalam । satyasopānamāruhya devānāmantike gataḥ ।।
hrāsavṛddhī ca bhūtānāmakasmāt kurute hi yaḥ । sa rājā vai paro devairdevaloke ca tiṣṭhati ।। manuṣyāntaratattvajño yo vetti hi balābalam । sa dhībalābhyāṃ saṃyukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।।
traidhātukapadaṃ yacca ratnatrayamihocyate । yastat pūjayate rājā sa deveṣūpajāyate ।। kālaṃ niyatadarśī yaḥ prajānāṃ ca hite rataḥ । sarvato bhadrakāntāro devānāmadhipaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
nindāmalavinirmuktaḥ saṅgadoṣavivarjitaḥ । jñānagocarasampūjyo niyataṃ deva eva saḥ ।। kausīdyadoṣarahito nityaṃ dṛḍhaparākramaḥ । nāśayitvā sa doṣaughān pretya svargeṣu jāyate ।।
hitāni yasya mitrāṇi karmakartṛṇi nityaśaḥ । sa mitraiḥ samparivṛto nṛpo devādhipo bhavet ।। nānuseveta durvṛttān vākkṣepeṇa ca varjitaḥ । sa sadyo viṣanirmuktaḥ surāṇāmadhipo bhavet ।।
krodhaharṣavighātāya na ca pāpeṣu rakṣyate । sa pāpapaṅkanidhautaḥ suralokādhipaḥ sadā ।। na śaktaḥ pānabhojyeṣu saṃsaktastu śubhe sadā । sa śuddhadharmasandarśī vibudho adhikatāṃ vrajet ।।
sucintitaṃ cintayati dharmeṣu ca vartate । dharmodayena dṛṣṭena yathā yāti triviṣṭapam ।। saṃsārād dīrghasūtrād yastvaritaṃ dharmamācaret । sa dīrghasūtranirmuktaḥ prayāti padamuttamam ।।
dharmeṇaiva prajā nityaṃ prapālayati nṛpaḥ । sa dhārmikaḥ praśastātmā suraloke mahīyate ।। daśeme kuśalā dharmā ihoktāstattvadarśinā । yaste prakurute dharmān sa surādhipatāṃ vrajet ।।
hetupratyayasandarśī mārgāmārgau tathaiva ca । sa dṛṣṭimalanirmukto vibudho adhikatāṃ gataḥ ।। yo devatāṃ pūjayati yathā cāhni mahīpatiḥ । sa devapūjito bhūyo devānāmadhipo bhavet ।।
anāvilena manasā prasannaścādhidārakaḥ । svasvadāraiśca santuṣṭo devānāmadhipo bhavet ।। hīyate yo na viṣayaiḥ sarvabālāpahāribhiḥ । sa śīlavān divaṃ yāti nityaṃ śīlena rakṣitaḥ ।।
avidyāvarjakān nityaṃ sevate yaḥ sudhārmikān । saddharmacintakaḥ saukhyaṃ kalpate sura sadi ।। pārṣadālāpahāribhiḥ । sa śīlavān divaṃ yāti nityaṃ śīlena rakṣitaḥ ।।
sadvyāpārāddharmamimaṃ pālayan vasudhādhipaḥ । praśāsti ca mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।। satkarmanirato bhṛtyo nṛpe sadguṇaśālini । jano nirmalatāṃ yāti śaraccandra ivāmbare ।।
hetulakṣyavidhijñā ye aviruddhāḥ parasparam । samyaksvāmyarthakarttāraḥ devānāṃ vaśamāgatāḥ ।। ।। iti rājāvavādavargaḥ pañcatriṃśaḥ ।। samasattvāgravedāya sarvasattveṣu bandhave ।
sanmārgasārthavāhāya bhavabandhanabhedine ।। nādṛṣṭivibhedāya sarvasaṃśayamocine । samyagdṛṣṭiniveśāya namaḥ sañjñānacakṣuṣe ।। sarvasaṅkaṭabhedāya tridoṣamalaśodhine ।
namo nakṣatrabhūtāya sarvabījaphaloruhe ।। sarvaprajñākarāgrāya sarvadhyānāgravedine । sarvaratnottamāryāya namo alānāgradarśine ।। iyaṃ sā lokanāśasya viprayuktasya tāpinaḥ ।
pratimā dṛśyate śāntā mokṣamudghāṭyakārikā ।। samarcatīmāṃ nityaṃ puruṣaḥ śāntamānasaḥ । sa mucyate bhavabhayānnivṛttiṃ cādhigacchati ।। etacchāntapadaṃ ramyametannaiṣṭhikamucyate ।
yadayaṃ bhāṣate dharma nirvāṇapuradeśikaḥ ।। asya vākyaṃ samālambya puruṣādhīnavikramāḥ । ākarṣanti padaṃ nityaṃ yadanantasukhāvaham ।। etat pūrva samāruhaya puruṣāstattvacintakāḥ ।
trilokaughārṇavaṃ ghoraṃ taranti bhavasāgaram ।। ayaṃ sa cakṣurlokasya samantāddhi vicakṣuṣaḥ । ayaṃ jyotiḥ paraṃ jyotiryajjyotiḥkāṣṭhasambhavam ।। kalpāntaṃ prāṇināṃ citte nṛṇāṃ rāgādibhirmalaiḥ ।
jñānatoyena mahatā śodhayatyeva vāṅnṛpaḥ ।। yanna dṛṣṭaṃ padaṃ sarvaistīrthikairjñānapāṇibhiḥ । tatpadaṃ vimalairvākyaistvayā nṛṇāṃ pradarśitam ।। pramādaparamo anātho jano ayaṃ tāritastvayā ।
tīrṇaḥ pāragato nāthastārayatyaghanāśanāt ।। hitārtha sarvajagatastvamevaiko vyavasthitaḥ । ahitānāṃ hitāyaiva tvameva puruṣottamaḥ ।। anādimati saṃsāre nṛṇāṃ kleśāpahārakaiḥ ।
tvayā viśodhito vākyaistamaḥ sūryodaye yathā ।। akṣayaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ jñānalokakaro mahān । tvamevaiko jagannātha lokottaraguṇārṇavaḥ ।। ।। iti stutivargaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ ।।
puṇyadevasukhairmitrarājastutibhiranvitāḥ । saddharmasmṛtivaipulyai gṛhīto ayaṃ samuccayaḥ ।। ।। iti caturtham udānam ।। ye ca dharmā hetubhavā teṣāṃ tathāgato avadat ।
teṣāṃ ca yo nirodhaścaivaṃvādīmahāśramaṇaḥ ।। puṇyamavāptamantrakleśaṃ vibhidyājanavalāśrīkam । yāvajjagadvyākulaṃ tarkaniṣṭhaiḥ samākulaṃ vetti satyavacanaiḥ ।। vaipulyamahāgambhīrodadhisūtravarād bhikṣu avalokitasiṃhenoddhṛtamiti ।
mohāśivādirahitasya vākyavidyasya vipulārjanasya adharmasamuccayo' nāma dharmaparyāyaḥ samāptaḥ । ।।
